--[[
    ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
    ║   PORTAL GUN — Spider-Drone Model + Logic v6 + MEGA-VFX EDITION ║
    ║   LocalScript — place in StarterCharacterScripts                ║
    ║   or run via an executor.                                        ║
    ║                                                                  ║
    ║   Model built entirely from programmatic Roblox parts —         ║
    ║   no mesh imports or catalog assets required.                   ║
    ║                                                                  ║
    ║   NOTE: No point/upgrade economy of any kind. Every visual        ║
    ║   effect pack below is unlocked from the moment you spawn — no    ║
    ║   grinding, no currency, no ranks. Flip any pack on/off for       ║
    ║   free in the Settings → VFX tab.                                 ║
    ║                                                                  ║
    ║   Controls:                                                      ║
    ║     Left Click  / Activate = Blue portal                         ║
    ║     Right Click / Q key    = Orange portal                       ║
    ║     R key                  = Close all portals                   ║
    ║     Z / X keys             = Switch selected color               ║
    ║     [ / ] keys             = Rotate portal  −15° / +15°          ║
    ║     ; / ' keys             = Tilt portal up / down  −15° / +15°  ║
    ║     \ key                  = Reset portal rotation & tilt to 0°  ║
    ║     ⚙ button               = Settings (color, size, range, VFX)  ║
    ║     ↺ / ↻ mobile buttons   = Rotate portal (mobile)              ║
    ║     ⤴ / ⤵ mobile buttons   = Tilt portal up/down (mobile)        ║
    ║                                                                  ║
    ║   Works on walls, floors, AND ceilings.                          ║
    ║   The full detailed 3D spider-drone model is built               ║
    ║   programmatically — no meshes/imports required.                 ║
    ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
]]

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  SAFE TASK WRAPPERS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function safeWait(t)
    if task then pcall(task.wait, t) else wait(t) end
end
local function safeSpawn(fn)
    if task then task.spawn(fn) else spawn(fn) end
end
local function safeDelay(t, fn)
    if task then task.delay(t, fn) else delay(t, fn) end
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PLACE-ID SKIN SELECTION
--
--  Mel's Portal Gun skin is exclusive to the following games:
--    3522803956  Portal Stories: Mel (and look-alikes)
--    4786930269  De Pride Isle Sanatorium
--    3449573444  Eden Orphan Home
--    746820961   Equalia Falls Mental Institute
--    9675359772  Unit 1968 / Chicago 1949
--
--  On these PlaceIds the script:
--    • Uses Mel's portal-gun audio (Portal 2 / Portal Stories sounds)
--    • Sets the portal colors to the Bright-blue / Neon-orange BrickColor
--      palette from the original Mel skin
--    • When BOTH portals are placed the portal body (fill) turns nearly
--      black — the iconic Portal 2 "black hole" look — while the shimmer
--      ring stays the portal color.
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _MEL_PLACE_IDS = {
    [3522803956] = true,  -- Portal Stories: Mel
    [4786930269] = true,  -- De Pride Isle Sanatorium
    [3449573444] = true,  -- Eden Orphan Home
    [746820961]  = true,  -- Equalia Falls Mental Institute
    [9675359772] = true,  -- Unit 1968 / Chicago 1949
}
local SKIN = _MEL_PLACE_IDS[game.PlaceId] and "mel" or "default"

if SKIN == "mel" then
    -- Portal colors: Bright blue / Neon orange (BrickColor values)
    CFG.blueColor   = Color3.fromRGB(13,  105, 172)   -- BrickColor "Bright blue"
    CFG.orangeColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 128,  13)   -- BrickColor "Neon orange"

    CFG.sndFire     = "rbxassetid://182981554"   -- blue shot
    CFG.sndCreate   = "rbxassetid://171399373"   -- portal open
    CFG.sndTeleport = "rbxassetid://232806289"   -- teleport whoosh
    CFG.sndClose    = "rbxassetid://182981587"   -- portal close / fizzle
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  HELPERS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function getHRP()
    local c = LP.Character
    return c and c:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end

local function clamp(v, lo, hi) return math.max(lo, math.min(hi, v)) end
local function lerp(a, b, t)    return a + (b - a) * t               end

local function tw(inst, t, props)
    TweenService:Create(inst, TweenInfo.new(t, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), props):Play()
end

local function playSound(id, parent)
    if not CFG.soundEnabled or not id or id == "" then return end
    local ok, s = pcall(Instance.new, "Sound")
    if not ok then return end
    s.SoundId = id; s.Volume = 0.8; s.RollOffMaxDistance = 80
    s.Parent  = parent or SoundService
    s:Play()
    s.Ended:Connect(function() pcall(function() s:Destroy() end) end)
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  SPIDER-DRONE PORTAL GUN MODEL  (Model v2)
--
--  Design spec:
--    Head   — glossy white ovoid, bullet/egg taper, seam line, iris eye
--             (navy ring → cyan neon band → black pupil), fin nub behind eye,
--             rear flare before collar
--    Collar — dark gray rotation joint ring
--    Torso  — long black cylinder with beveled blue-white neon core strip,
--             faint horizontal ribs, PointLight
--    Rear   — wider black drum, concentric-ridge end cap, antenna nub
--    Cables — thin matte-black arcing tubes over the top
--    Legs   — 6 multi-jointed spider legs, angular elbow joints, claw tips,
--             asymmetric pose (one stiff upper-right, rest folded beneath)
--    Braces — small triangular lattice cross-brace near front/rear leg roots
--    Belly  — flat pale-gray wedge access panel on underside
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
-- ── Mel's Portal Gun model (Portal Stories: Mel skin) ────────────────
local function buildPortalGunModel(options)
    options = options or {}

    -- ── Tool root ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local tool          = Instance.new("Tool")
    tool.Name           = "Mel's Portal Gun"
    tool.TextureId      = "rbxassetid://14425003210"
    tool.ToolTip        = "Mel's Portal Gun  |  LMB=Blue  RMB=Orange  R=Close"
    tool.RequiresHandle = true
    tool.CanBeDropped   = false

    -- ── Handle (invisible brick — weld root) ──────────────────────────
    local H             = Instance.new("Part")
    H.Name              = "Handle"
    H.Size              = Vector3.new(1.1, 1.1, 2.8)
    H.Color             = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    H.Material          = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic
    H.Transparency      = 1
    H.CanCollide        = false
    H.Parent            = tool

    -- ── Mesh body ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local MeshPart      = Instance.new("Part")
    MeshPart.Name       = "MeshBody"
    MeshPart.CanCollide = false
    MeshPart.Orientation = Vector3.new(0, 180, 0)
    MeshPart.Parent     = tool
    local Mesh          = Instance.new("SpecialMesh", MeshPart)
    Mesh.MeshId         = "rbxassetid://5446245015"
    Mesh.TextureId      = "rbxassetid://14192504911"
    Mesh.Scale          = Vector3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)

    -- ── Neon ring emitter — named "Emitter" so VFX can locate it ──────
    local cylinder1         = Instance.new("Part")
    cylinder1.Name          = "Emitter"
    cylinder1.Shape         = Enum.PartType.Cylinder
    cylinder1.Orientation   = Vector3.new(0, 90, 0)
    cylinder1.Position      = Vector3.new(-0.04, -0.089, 0.136)
    cylinder1.Size          = Vector3.new(1.292, 0.4, 1)
    cylinder1.Material      = Enum.Material.Neon
    cylinder1.Color         = Color3.fromRGB(19, 238, 165)
    cylinder1.CanCollide    = false
    cylinder1.Parent        = tool

    -- ── Secondary neon pip — named "EmitterCore" for VFX brighten ─────
    local cylinder2         = Instance.new("Part")
    cylinder2.Name          = "EmitterCore"
    cylinder2.Shape         = Enum.PartType.Cylinder
    cylinder2.Orientation   = Vector3.new(0, 0, -90)
    cylinder2.Position      = Vector3.new(-0.06, 0.268, 0.961)
    cylinder2.Size          = Vector3.new(0.113, 0.266, 0.994)
    cylinder2.Material      = Enum.Material.Neon
    cylinder2.Color         = Color3.fromRGB(19, 238, 165)
    cylinder2.CanCollide    = false
    cylinder2.Parent        = tool

    -- ── Gravity-gun beam parts (hidden until activated) ───────────────
    local GGblock1          = Instance.new("Part")
    GGblock1.Name           = "GGblock1"
    GGblock1.CanCollide     = false
    GGblock1.BrickColor     = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGblock1.Material       = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGblock1.Position       = Vector3.new(0.025, 0.355, -2.077)
    GGblock1.Size           = Vector3.new(0.05, 0.743, 0.05)
    GGblock1.Transparency   = 1
    GGblock1.Parent         = tool

    local GGblock2          = Instance.new("Part")
    GGblock2.Name           = "GGblock2"
    GGblock2.CanCollide     = false
    GGblock2.BrickColor     = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGblock2.Material       = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGblock2.Position       = Vector3.new(-0.433, -0.377, -2.06)
    GGblock2.Orientation    = Vector3.new(39.204, -86.193, -4.388)
    GGblock2.Size           = Vector3.new(0.05, 0.05, 1.222)
    GGblock2.Transparency   = 1
    GGblock2.Parent         = tool

    local GGblock3          = Instance.new("Part")
    GGblock3.Name           = "GGblock3"
    GGblock3.CanCollide     = false
    GGblock3.BrickColor     = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGblock3.Material       = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGblock3.Position       = Vector3.new(0.486, -0.37, -2.058)
    GGblock3.Orientation    = Vector3.new(37.547, 86.861, 176.758)
    GGblock3.Size           = Vector3.new(0.05, 0.05, 1.222)
    GGblock3.Transparency   = 1
    GGblock3.Parent         = tool

    local GGBall1           = Instance.new("Part")
    GGBall1.Name            = "GGBall1"
    GGBall1.Shape           = Enum.PartType.Ball
    GGBall1.CanCollide      = false
    GGBall1.Material        = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGBall1.BrickColor      = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGBall1.Size            = Vector3.new(0.224, 0.224, 0.224)
    GGBall1.Position        = Vector3.new(0.051, 0.699, -2.106)
    GGBall1.Transparency    = 1
    GGBall1.Parent          = tool

    local GGBall2           = Instance.new("Part")
    GGBall2.Name            = "GGBall2"
    GGBall2.Shape           = Enum.PartType.Ball
    GGBall2.CanCollide      = false
    GGBall2.Material        = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGBall2.BrickColor      = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGBall2.Size            = Vector3.new(0.224, 0.224, 0.224)
    GGBall2.Position        = Vector3.new(-0.93, -0.765, -2.03)
    GGBall2.Transparency    = 1
    GGBall2.Parent          = tool

    local GGBall3           = Instance.new("Part")
    GGBall3.Name            = "GGBall3"
    GGBall3.Shape           = Enum.PartType.Ball
    GGBall3.CanCollide      = false
    GGBall3.Material        = Enum.Material.Neon
    GGBall3.BrickColor      = BrickColor.new("Pastel Blue")
    GGBall3.Size            = Vector3.new(0.224, 0.224, 0.224)
    GGBall3.Position        = Vector3.new(0.931, -0.743, -2.03)
    GGBall3.Transparency    = 1
    GGBall3.Parent          = tool

    -- ── Sounds ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local BShoot        = Instance.new("Sound", H)
    BShoot.Name         = "BShoot"
    BShoot.SoundId      = "rbxassetid://182981554"
    local OShoot        = Instance.new("Sound", H)
    OShoot.Name         = "OShoot"
    OShoot.SoundId      = "rbxassetid://142774034"

    -- ── Flashlight ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local light         = Instance.new("SpotLight", H)
    light.Name          = "Flashlight"
    light.Angle         = 45
    light.Brightness    = 2
    light.Range         = 60
    light.Enabled       = false

    -- ── WeldConstraints ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    local function wc(a, b)
        local w = Instance.new("WeldConstraint", tool)
        w.Part0 = a; w.Part1 = b
    end
    wc(H, MeshPart)
    wc(H, cylinder1)
    wc(H, cylinder2)
    wc(H, GGblock1)
    wc(H, GGblock2)
    wc(H, GGblock3)
    wc(H, GGBall1)
    wc(H, GGBall2)
    wc(H, GGBall3)

    -- ── Grip position (rig-type aware) ────────────────────────────────
    local char = LP.Character
    local isR6 = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
        and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.R6
    tool.GripPos = isR6 and Vector3.new(0.35, 0.25, 0.25) or Vector3.new(0.2, 0.25, -0.1)

    return tool
end


-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  GUI ROOT
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local gui
do
    local g = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    g.Name = "PortalGunUI"; g.ResetOnSpawn = false; g.IgnoreGuiInset = true

    local function tryParent(target)
        if not target then return false end
        local ok = pcall(function() g.Parent = target end)
        return ok and g.Parent == target
    end

    if gethui then
        local ok, h = pcall(gethui)
        if ok and h then tryParent(h) end
    end
    if not g.Parent then
        local ok, cg = pcall(function() return game:GetService("CoreGui") end)
        if ok then tryParent(cg) end
    end
    if not g.Parent then
        local pg = LP:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui") or LP:WaitForChild("PlayerGui", 8)
        tryParent(pg)
    end
    gui = g
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  SURFACE VALIDATION
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function isValidSurface(result)
    if not result then return false end
    local inst = result.Instance

    if inst:IsA("Terrain") then
    elseif inst:IsA("BasePart") then
        if not inst.CanCollide  then return false end
        if inst.Transparency >= 1 then return false end
    else
        return false
    end

    if CFG.flatTolerance > 0 then
        local n = result.Normal
        local flat = math.abs(n.X) > CFG.flatTolerance
                  or math.abs(n.Y) > CFG.flatTolerance
                  or math.abs(n.Z) > CFG.flatTolerance
        if not flat then return false end
    end
    return true
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PORTAL CFRAME
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function portalCF(result)
    local n   = result.Normal
    local pos = result.Position + n * CFG.surfaceOffset
    local up  = math.abs(n:Dot(Vector3.new(0,1,0))) > 0.99
                and Vector3.new(0,0,-1) or Vector3.new(0,1,0)
    local cf  = CFrame.lookAt(pos, pos + n, up)
    if portalTilt ~= 0 then
        cf = cf * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(portalTilt), 0, 0)
    end
    if portalRotation ~= 0 then
        cf = cf * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(portalRotation))
    end
    return cf
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  RAYCAST
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local RPARAMS = RaycastParams.new()
RPARAMS.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude

local function doRaycast()
    local hrp = getHRP()
    if not hrp then return nil end
    local ex = { LP.Character }
    if portals.blue   and portals.blue.folder   then table.insert(ex, portals.blue.folder)   end
    if portals.orange and portals.orange.folder then table.insert(ex, portals.orange.folder) end
    RPARAMS.FilterDescendantsInstances = ex
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        return Workspace:Raycast(Cam.CFrame.Position, Cam.CFrame.LookVector * CFG.range, RPARAMS)
    end)
    return ok and result or nil
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PORTAL VISUALS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function makePortalPart(color)
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    local pw, ph, pd = CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight, CFG.portalDepth

    local folder = Instance.new("Folder")
    folder.Name  = "PortalFolder_"..color
    folder.Parent= Workspace

    local function makePart(name, mat, c, tr, sx, sy)
        local p        = Instance.new("Part")
        p.Name         = name; p.Anchored = true; p.CanCollide = false
        p.CanTouch     = false; p.CastShadow = false
        p.Material     = mat; p.Color = c; p.Transparency = tr
        p.Size         = Vector3.new(sx * pw, sy * ph, pd); p.Parent = folder
        local m        = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
        m.MeshType     = Enum.MeshType.Sphere; m.Scale = Vector3.new(1,1,0.05); m.Parent = p
        return p
    end

    local ring    = makePart("Ring",    Enum.Material.Neon,           col,                    0,    1.00, 1.00)
    local shimmer = makePart("Shimmer", Enum.Material.Neon,           col,                    0.55, 0.90, 0.90)
    local halo    = makePart("Halo",    Enum.Material.Neon,           col,                    0.78, 1.18, 1.18)

    -- ── Portal screen — flat invisible carrier for the ViewportFrame ──────
    -- Replaces the old solid black "Void" disk.
    local screen        = Instance.new("Part")
    screen.Name         = "PortalScreen"; screen.Anchored = true; screen.CanCollide = false
    screen.CanTouch     = false; screen.CastShadow = false; screen.Transparency = 1
    screen.Size         = Vector3.new(pw * 0.80, ph * 0.80, 0.05); screen.Parent = folder

    -- SurfaceGui on the player-facing (+Z = LookVector) side of the screen part
    local surfGui               = Instance.new("SurfaceGui")
    surfGui.Face                = Enum.NormalId.Front
    surfGui.SizingMode          = Enum.SurfaceGuiSizingMode.PixelsPerStud
    surfGui.PixelsPerStud       = 50
    surfGui.ClipsDescendants    = true
    surfGui.AlwaysOnTop         = false
    surfGui.Parent              = screen

    -- ViewportFrame — renders the linked portal's camera view
    local vpf                   = Instance.new("ViewportFrame")
    vpf.Size                    = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    vpf.BackgroundColor3        = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
    vpf.BackgroundTransparency  = 0
    -- Subtle tint so the empty viewport reads as a coloured void rather than
    -- plain black — will look correct once world objects are added to vpf.
    local dimCol                = Color3.new(col.R * 0.18, col.G * 0.18, col.B * 0.18)
    vpf.BackgroundColor3        = dimCol
    vpf.ImageColor3             = Color3.fromRGB(210, 210, 210)
    vpf.Parent                  = surfGui

    -- Dedicated camera for this portal's viewport
    local vpCam                 = Instance.new("Camera")
    vpCam.FieldOfView           = 70
    vpCam.Parent                = vpf
    vpf.CurrentCamera           = vpCam

    local light           = Instance.new("PointLight")
    light.Brightness      = CFG.lightBrightness; light.Range = 20
    light.Color           = col; light.Parent = ring

    local att = Instance.new("Attachment"); att.Parent = ring
    local pe              = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
    pe.Color              = ColorSequence.new(col)
    pe.LightEmission      = 1; pe.LightInfluence = 0
    pe.Size               = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0.35),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,0)})
    pe.Speed              = NumberRange.new(2,6); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(180,0)
    pe.Rotation           = NumberRange.new(0,360); pe.RotSpeed = NumberRange.new(-200,200)
    pe.Lifetime           = NumberRange.new(0.4,1.0); pe.Rate = 70; pe.Parent = att

    return { folder=folder, part=ring, shimmer=shimmer, halo=halo, screen=screen, vpf=vpf, vpCam=vpCam, light=light, emitter=pe }
end

local function setPortalCFrames(d, cf)
    d.part.CFrame    = cf
    d.screen.CFrame  = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.03)   -- screen sits just inside the portal face
    d.shimmer.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.02)
    d.halo.CFrame    = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.06)
end

local function animateOpen(d, cf)
    local pw, ph, pd = CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight, CFG.portalDepth
    setPortalCFrames(d, cf)
    for _, part in ipairs({d.part, d.shimmer, d.halo}) do
        part.Size = Vector3.new(0.1, 0.1, pd)
    end
    d.screen.Size = Vector3.new(0.1, 0.1, 0.05)
    tw(d.part,    CFG.openTime, {Size=Vector3.new(pw,         ph,        pd)})
    tw(d.screen,  CFG.openTime, {Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.80,    ph*0.80,   0.05)})
    tw(d.shimmer, CFG.openTime, {Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.90,    ph*0.90,   pd)})
    tw(d.halo,    CFG.openTime, {Size=Vector3.new(pw*1.18,    ph*1.18,   pd), Transparency=0.78})
end

local function animateClose(d, cb)
    if not d then if cb then cb() end; return end
    d.emitter.Rate = 0
    local pd = CFG.portalDepth
    for _, part in ipairs({d.part, d.shimmer}) do
        tw(part, CFG.closeTime, {Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,pd)})
    end
    tw(d.screen, CFG.closeTime, {Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.05)})
    tw(d.halo, CFG.closeTime, {Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,pd), Transparency=1})
    safeDelay(CFG.closeTime + 0.05, function()
        pcall(function() d.folder:Destroy() end)
        if cb then cb() end
    end)
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  REFRESH MODEL VISUALS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _modelParts = {}

local function refreshPortalVisuals()
    -- Mel skin: when both portals are placed the body fill goes nearly black
    -- (only the shimmer ring retains the portal color — the iconic Portal 2 look).
    local bothOpen = SKIN == "mel" and portals.blue ~= nil and portals.orange ~= nil
    local MEL_BLACK = Color3.fromRGB(17, 17, 17)  -- BrickColor "Really black"

    for _, ck in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
        local d = portals[ck]
        if d then
            local col = ck=="blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
            -- Fill: black when both portals are linked (Mel skin), otherwise portal color
            d.part.Color    = (bothOpen) and MEL_BLACK or col
            d.shimmer.Color = col   -- ring always stays portal color
            d.halo.Color    = col;  d.light.Color   = col
            d.light.Brightness = CFG.lightBrightness
            d.emitter.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
            local pw, ph, pd = CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight, CFG.portalDepth
            d.part.Size    = Vector3.new(pw,       ph,       pd)
            d.screen.Size  = Vector3.new(pw*0.80,  ph*0.80,  0.05)
            d.shimmer.Size = Vector3.new(pw*0.90,  ph*0.90,  pd)
            d.halo.Size    = Vector3.new(pw*1.18,  ph*1.18,  pd)
        end
    end
    if _modelParts.blueNeon then
        for _, p in ipairs(_modelParts.blueNeon) do
            pcall(function() p.Color = CFG.blueColor end)
        end
    end
    if _modelParts.orangeNeon then
        for _, p in ipairs(_modelParts.orangeNeon) do
            pcall(function() p.Color = CFG.orangeColor end)
        end
    end
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PREVIEW GHOST
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function ensurePreview()
    if prevPart and prevPart.Parent then return end
    prevPart             = Instance.new("Part")
    prevPart.Name        = "PortalPreview"; prevPart.Anchored = true
    prevPart.CanCollide  = false; prevPart.CanTouch = false; prevPart.CastShadow = false
    prevPart.Transparency = 0.55; prevPart.Parent = Workspace
    prevPart.Size        = Vector3.new(CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight, CFG.portalDepth)
    local m              = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
    m.MeshType           = Enum.MeshType.Sphere; m.Scale = Vector3.new(1,1,0.05); m.Parent = prevPart
    prevSelect           = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
    prevSelect.Adornee   = prevPart; prevSelect.SurfaceTransparency = 1
    prevSelect.LineThickness = 0.04; prevSelect.Parent = prevPart
end

local function updatePreview(result)
    ensurePreview()
    if not gunEnabled then prevPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(0,-9999,0); return end
    local col = selColor=="blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    if result and isValidSurface(result) then
        prevPart.Size        = Vector3.new(CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight, CFG.portalDepth)
        prevPart.CFrame      = portalCF(result)
        prevPart.Color       = col
        prevPart.Transparency = 0.45
        prevSelect.Color3    = col
    else
        prevPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(0,-9999,0)
    end
end

-- Forward-declared
local VFX

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  VFX MODULE
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
VFX = {}

local function vfxAttachment(parentPart)
    local att = Instance.new("Attachment")
    att.Parent = parentPart
    return att
end

local function vfxBurstEmitter(att, color, opts)
    opts = opts or {}
    local pe = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
    pe.Parent         = att
    pe.Color          = ColorSequence.new(color)
    pe.LightEmission  = opts.lightEmission or 1
    pe.LightInfluence = 0
    pe.Size           = opts.size or NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, opts.startSize or 0.4),
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0),
    })
    pe.Transparency   = opts.transparency or NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.1),
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
    })
    pe.Speed          = opts.speed or NumberRange.new(4, 12)
    pe.SpreadAngle    = opts.spread or Vector2.new(180, 180)
    pe.Rotation       = NumberRange.new(0, 360)
    pe.RotSpeed       = NumberRange.new(-180, 180)
    pe.Lifetime       = opts.lifetime or NumberRange.new(0.3, 0.9)
    pe.Rate           = 0
    pe.Enabled        = false
    pe.Acceleration   = opts.accel or Vector3.new(0, -2, 0)
    pe.EmissionDirection = opts.direction or Enum.NormalId.Front
    return pe
end

local function vfxEmitBurst(pe, count)
    pcall(function() pe:Emit(count or 18) end)
end

local function vfxScheduleCleanup(inst, delaySec)
    safeDelay(delaySec or 1.4, function()
        pcall(function() inst:Destroy() end)
    end)
end

function VFX.muzzleFlash(color)
    local char = LP.Character
    if not char then return end
    local tool = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") or LP.Backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
    local emitterPart = tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Emitter", true)
    local originPart  = emitterPart or getHRP()
    if not originPart then return end

    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor

    local flash = Instance.new("Part")
    flash.Name = "VFX_MuzzleFlash"; flash.Anchored = true; flash.CanCollide = false
    flash.CanTouch = false; flash.CastShadow = false
    flash.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; flash.Color = col
    flash.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball; flash.Size = Vector3.new(0.55, 0.55, 0.55)
    flash.CFrame = originPart.CFrame; flash.Parent = Workspace

    local light = Instance.new("PointLight")
    light.Color = col; light.Range = 14; light.Brightness = 4; light.Parent = flash

    tw(flash, 0.18, {Size = Vector3.new(1.6, 1.6, 1.6), Transparency = 1})
    tw(light, 0.18, {Brightness = 0})

    local att = vfxAttachment(flash)
    local pe  = vfxBurstEmitter(att, col, {
        startSize = 0.5, speed = NumberRange.new(8, 18),
        lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.5), spread = Vector2.new(360, 360),
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(pe, 22)
    vfxScheduleCleanup(flash, 0.6)
end

function VFX.onPortalOpen(portalData, cf, color)
    if not portalData or not portalData.part then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor

    local ring = Instance.new("Part")
    ring.Name = "VFX_OpenRing"; ring.Anchored = true; ring.CanCollide = false
    ring.CanTouch = false; ring.CastShadow = false
    ring.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; ring.Color = col; ring.Transparency = 0.25
    ring.Size = Vector3.new(0.2, 0.2, CFG.portalDepth); ring.CFrame = cf; ring.Parent = Workspace
    local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
    mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere; mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.02); mesh.Parent = ring

    tw(ring, 0.4, {
        Size = Vector3.new(CFG.portalWidth * 1.6, CFG.portalHeight * 1.6, CFG.portalDepth),
        Transparency = 1,
    })
    vfxScheduleCleanup(ring, 0.6)

    local swirlFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
    swirlFolder.Name = "VFX_Swirl"; swirlFolder.Parent = Workspace
    local sparkCount = 10
    for i = 1, sparkCount do
        local ang = (i / sparkCount) * math.pi * 2
        local rad = math.max(CFG.portalWidth, CFG.portalHeight) * 0.55
        local localPos = Vector3.new(math.cos(ang) * rad, math.sin(ang) * rad, 0)
        local spark = Instance.new("Part")
        spark.Name = "Spark"; spark.Anchored = true; spark.CanCollide = false
        spark.CanTouch = false; spark.CastShadow = false
        spark.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; spark.Color = col
        spark.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball; spark.Size = Vector3.new(0.14, 0.14, 0.14)
        spark.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(localPos); spark.Parent = swirlFolder
        tw(spark, 0.35, {CFrame = cf, Transparency = 1, Size = Vector3.new(0.03, 0.03, 0.03)})
    end
    vfxScheduleCleanup(swirlFolder, 0.7)
end

function VFX.onPortalClose(portalData, color)
    if not portalData or not portalData.part then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    local pos = portalData.part.Position

    local puff = Instance.new("Part")
    puff.Name = "VFX_ClosePuff"; puff.Anchored = true; puff.CanCollide = false
    puff.CanTouch = false; puff.CastShadow = false
    puff.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; puff.Color = col; puff.Transparency = 0.2
    puff.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
    puff.Size = Vector3.new(CFG.portalWidth * 0.4, CFG.portalHeight * 0.4, CFG.portalWidth * 0.4)
    puff.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos); puff.Parent = Workspace
    tw(puff, 0.3, {Size = Vector3.new(0.05, 0.05, 0.05), Transparency = 1})

    local att = vfxAttachment(puff)
    local pe  = vfxBurstEmitter(att, col, {
        startSize = 0.35, speed = NumberRange.new(3, 9),
        lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.3, 0.7), accel = Vector3.new(0, -4, 0),
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(pe, 16)
    vfxScheduleCleanup(puff, 0.9)
end

function VFX.onTeleport(fromData, toData, hrp)
    if not hrp then return end
    local function flashAt(cf, col)
        local p = Instance.new("Part")
        p.Name = "VFX_TeleFlash"; p.Anchored = true; p.CanCollide = false
        p.CanTouch = false; p.CastShadow = false
        p.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; p.Color = col
        p.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball; p.Size = Vector3.new(1.2, 1.2, 1.2)
        p.Transparency = 0.1; p.CFrame = cf; p.Parent = Workspace
        tw(p, 0.28, {Size = Vector3.new(3.2, 3.2, 3.2), Transparency = 1})
        vfxScheduleCleanup(p, 0.5)
    end
    if fromData and fromData.cf then flashAt(fromData.cf, CFG.blueColor) end
    if toData and toData.cf then flashAt(toData.cf, CFG.orangeColor) end

    local trailPart = Instance.new("Part")
    trailPart.Name = "VFX_TeleTrailAnchor"; trailPart.Size = Vector3.new(0.2, 0.2, 0.2)
    trailPart.Transparency = 1; trailPart.Anchored = false
    trailPart.CanCollide = false; trailPart.CanTouch = false; trailPart.CastShadow = false
    trailPart.CFrame = hrp.CFrame; trailPart.Parent = Workspace

    local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint")
    weld.Part0 = hrp; weld.Part1 = trailPart; weld.Parent = trailPart

    local a0 = Instance.new("Attachment"); a0.Parent = trailPart
    local a1 = Instance.new("Attachment"); a1.Position = Vector3.new(0, 0, 1.5); a1.Parent = trailPart
    local trail = Instance.new("Trail")
    trail.Attachment0 = a0; trail.Attachment1 = a1; trail.Lifetime = 0.5
    trail.MinLength = 0; trail.FaceCamera = true
    trail.Color = ColorSequence.new(CFG.blueColor, CFG.orangeColor)
    trail.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.2), NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
    })
    trail.WidthScale = NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 1), NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0),
    })
    trail.Parent = trailPart

    safeDelay(0.7, function() pcall(function() trail.Enabled = false end) end)
    vfxScheduleCleanup(trailPart, 1.4)
end

function VFX.startIdlePulse(emitterPart)
    if not emitterPart then return end
    local light = emitterPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("PointLight")
    if not light then return end
    local baseBrightness = light.Brightness
    safeSpawn(function()
        local t = 0
        while emitterPart and emitterPart.Parent do
            t = t + 0.05
            local pulse = baseBrightness + math.sin(t * 3) * (baseBrightness * 0.35)
            pcall(function() light.Brightness = math.max(0.2, pulse) end)
            safeWait(0.05)
        end
    end)
end

function VFX.attachAmbientRim(portalData, color)
    if not portalData or not portalData.part then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    local att = vfxAttachment(portalData.part)
    local pe  = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
    pe.Parent = att; pe.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
    pe.LightEmission = 0.6; pe.LightInfluence = 0
    pe.Size = NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.12), NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0.02),
    })
    pe.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.4), NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
    })
    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(0.4, 1.2); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(360, 360)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(1.2, 2.2); pe.Rate = 6
    portalData.ambientEmitter = pe
end

function VFX.impactScorch(result, color)
    if not result or not result.Position then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    local normal = result.Normal or Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
    local decalPart = Instance.new("Part")
    decalPart.Anchored = true; decalPart.CanCollide = false; decalPart.CanQuery = false
    decalPart.CanTouch = false; decalPart.CastShadow = false; decalPart.Transparency = 1
    decalPart.Size = Vector3.new(1.6, 1.6, 0.05); decalPart.Name = "PortalScorch"
    local look = normal.Magnitude > 0 and normal or Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
    decalPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(result.Position + look * 0.03, result.Position + look)
    decalPart.Parent = workspace

    local decal = Instance.new("Decal")
    decal.Face = Enum.NormalId.Front; decal.Color3 = col; decal.Transparency = 0.35
    decal.Texture = "rbxasset://textures/particles/smoke_main.dds"; decal.Parent = decalPart
    local decal2 = decal:Clone(); decal2.Face = Enum.NormalId.Back; decal2.Parent = decalPart

    local ringAtt = vfxAttachment(decalPart)
    local ringPe  = vfxBurstEmitter(ringAtt, col, {
        startSize = 0.6, speed = NumberRange.new(1, 3), spread = Vector2.new(360, 360),
        lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.4, 0.7), lightEmission = 0.4,
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(ringPe, 8)
    tw(decal, 1.6, {Transparency = 1}); tw(decal2, 1.6, {Transparency = 1})
    vfxScheduleCleanup(decalPart, 1.9)
end

function VFX.spawnBeamTrail(fromPos, toPos, color, opts)
    opts = opts or {}
    local col = color == "blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    local a0 = Instance.new("Part")
    a0.Anchored = true; a0.CanCollide = false; a0.CanQuery = false
    a0.Transparency = 1; a0.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2)
    a0.CFrame = CFrame.new(fromPos); a0.Parent = workspace
    local a1 = Instance.new("Part")
    a1.Anchored = true; a1.CanCollide = false; a1.CanQuery = false
    a1.Transparency = 1; a1.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2)
    a1.CFrame = CFrame.new(toPos); a1.Parent = workspace

    local att0 = vfxAttachment(a0); local att1 = vfxAttachment(a1)
    local beam = Instance.new("Beam")
    beam.Attachment0 = att0; beam.Attachment1 = att1
    beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
    beam.Width0 = opts.width or 0.35; beam.Width1 = (opts.width or 0.35) * 0.15
    beam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({
        NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.15), NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1),
    })
    beam.LightEmission = 1; beam.FaceCamera = true; beam.Segments = 12; beam.Parent = a0
    tw(beam, opts.fadeTime or 0.35, {Width0 = 0, Width1 = 0})
    vfxScheduleCleanup(a0, (opts.fadeTime or 0.35) + 0.2)
    vfxScheduleCleanup(a1, (opts.fadeTime or 0.35) + 0.2)
end

-- ── MEGA VFX EXPANSION PACK ──────────────────────────────────────────

function VFX.lightningArcs(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(150, 220, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 120)
    local cf  = portalData.part.CFrame
    local w, h = portalData.part.Size.X, portalData.part.Size.Y
    for i = 1, 4 do
        local ang = math.rad(math.random(0, 360))
        local rx  = math.cos(ang) * w * 0.48; local ry = math.sin(ang) * h * 0.48
        local basePos = cf * CFrame.new(rx, ry, 0)
        local a0 = Instance.new("Part"); a0.Anchored = true; a0.CanCollide = false; a0.CanQuery = false
        a0.Transparency = 1; a0.Size = Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1); a0.CFrame = basePos; a0.Parent = workspace
        local att0 = vfxAttachment(a0)
        local a1 = Instance.new("Part"); a1.Anchored = true; a1.CanCollide = false; a1.CanQuery = false
        a1.Transparency = 1; a1.Size = Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1)
        a1.CFrame = basePos * CFrame.new(math.random(-15,15)/10, math.random(-15,15)/10, math.random(-4,4)/10)
        a1.Parent = workspace; local att1 = vfxAttachment(a1)
        local ok, beam = pcall(Instance.new, "Beam")
        if ok then
            beam.Attachment0 = att0; beam.Attachment1 = att1
            beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(col); beam.Width0 = 0.12; beam.Width1 = 0.02
            beam.FaceCamera = true; beam.LightEmission = 1; beam.Segments = 3
            beam.CurveSize0 = math.random(-15,15)/10; beam.CurveSize1 = math.random(-15,15)/10
            beam.Parent = att0; tw(beam, 0.18, {Width0 = 0, Width1 = 0})
        end
        vfxScheduleCleanup(a0, 0.4); vfxScheduleCleanup(a1, 0.4)
    end
end

function VFX.emberShower(cf, color)
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(180, 220, 255) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 160, 60)
    local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
    part.Transparency = 1; part.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2); part.CFrame = cf; part.Parent = workspace
    local att = vfxAttachment(part)
    local pe = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter"); pe.Parent = att; pe.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
    pe.LightEmission = 0.6
    pe.Size = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.12),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 0)})
    pe.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 0.2),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 1)})
    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(1, 3); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(60, 60)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(1.2, 2.2); pe.Acceleration = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0); pe.Rate = 0
    pcall(function() pe:Emit(30) end); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 2.5)
end

function VFX.shockwaveGround(pos, color)
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(0,150,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,140,0)
    local ok, ring = pcall(Instance.new, "Part"); if not ok then return end
    ring.Anchored = true; ring.CanCollide = false; ring.CanQuery = false
    ring.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; ring.Color = col
    ring.Size = Vector3.new(0.4, 0.05, 0.4); ring.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos); ring.Parent = workspace
    local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Cylinder; mesh.Parent = ring
    tw(ring, 0.5, {Size = Vector3.new(9, 0.05, 9), Transparency = 1}); vfxScheduleCleanup(ring, 0.6)
end

function VFX.energyTendrils(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(60,160,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,150,40)
    local cf  = portalData.part.CFrame
    for i = 1, 6 do
        local ang = math.rad((360/6) * i + math.random(-10,10))
        local dir = Vector3.new(math.cos(ang), math.sin(ang), 0)
        local a0 = Instance.new("Part"); a0.Anchored = true; a0.CanCollide = false; a0.CanQuery = false
        a0.Transparency = 1; a0.Size = Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1); a0.CFrame = cf; a0.Parent = workspace
        local att0 = vfxAttachment(a0)
        local a1 = Instance.new("Part"); a1.Anchored = true; a1.CanCollide = false; a1.CanQuery = false
        a1.Transparency = 1; a1.Size = Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1)
        a1.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(dir * 2.4); a1.Parent = workspace; local att1 = vfxAttachment(a1)
        local ok, beam = pcall(Instance.new, "Beam")
        if ok then
            beam.Attachment0 = att0; beam.Attachment1 = att1; beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
            beam.Width0 = 0.03; beam.Width1 = 0.22; beam.CurveSize0 = 0.6; beam.CurveSize1 = -0.6
            beam.LightEmission = 0.7; beam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.3); beam.Parent = att0
            safeDelay(0.25, function() pcall(function() tw(beam, 0.3, {Width0 = 0, Width1 = 0}) end) end)
        end
        vfxScheduleCleanup(a0, 0.7); vfxScheduleCleanup(a1, 0.7)
    end
end

function VFX.starburst(pos, color)
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(200,235,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,220,170)
    local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
    part.Transparency = 1; part.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2); part.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos); part.Parent = workspace
    local att = vfxAttachment(part)
    local pe = vfxBurstEmitter(att, col, {
        startSize = 0.5, speed = NumberRange.new(14, 22),
        spread = Vector2.new(360, 360), lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.25, 0.5), lightEmission = 1,
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(pe, 26); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 0.8)
end

function VFX.glyphRing(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(120,200,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,180,90)
    local cf  = portalData.part.CFrame
    local ring = Instance.new("Part"); ring.Anchored = true; ring.CanCollide = false; ring.CanQuery = false
    ring.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; ring.Color = col; ring.Transparency = 0.35
    ring.Size = Vector3.new(portalData.part.Size.X * 1.3, portalData.part.Size.Y * 1.3, 0.05)
    ring.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,-0.08); ring.Parent = workspace
    local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
    mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.02); mesh.Parent = ring
    local spin = 0; local conn
    conn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not ring.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
        spin = spin + dt * 40
        ring.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,-0.08) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(spin))
    end)
    tw(ring, 0.4, {Transparency = 1})
    safeDelay(1.2, function() pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end) end)
    vfxScheduleCleanup(ring, 1.3)
end

function VFX.distortionHaze(portalData)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local cf = portalData.part.CFrame
    local haze = Instance.new("Part"); haze.Anchored = true; haze.CanCollide = false; haze.CanQuery = false
    haze.Material = Enum.Material.ForceField; haze.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
    haze.Transparency = 0.85; haze.Size = portalData.part.Size * Vector3.new(0.95, 0.95, 1)
    haze.CFrame = cf; haze.Parent = workspace
    local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
    mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1,1,0.05); mesh.Parent = haze; vfxScheduleCleanup(haze, 2.5)
end

function VFX.portalWindGust(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(210,235,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,225,190)
    local cf = portalData.part.CFrame
    local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
    part.Transparency = 1; part.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2); part.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,1.2)
    part.Parent = workspace; local att = vfxAttachment(part)
    local pe = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter"); pe.Parent = att; pe.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
    pe.LightEmission = 0.5
    pe.Size = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0.15),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,0)})
    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(8,12); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(6,6)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.4,0.7); pe.Rate = 0
    pcall(function() pe:Emit(18) end); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 1.2)
end

function VFX.rimLightning(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    for i = 1, 2 do
        safeDelay(i * 0.08, function() pcall(function() VFX.lightningArcs(portalData, color) end) end)
    end
end

function VFX.teleportShatter(hrp, color)
    if not hrp then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(180,220,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,200,150)
    local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
    part.Transparency = 1; part.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2); part.CFrame = hrp.CFrame; part.Parent = workspace
    local att = vfxAttachment(part)
    local pe = vfxBurstEmitter(att, col, {
        startSize = 0.18, speed = NumberRange.new(6, 14), spread = Vector2.new(360, 360),
        lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.3, 0.6), lightEmission = 0.6,
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(pe, 22); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 0.8)
end

function VFX.vortexSwirlLoop(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end

    local att = vfxAttachment(portalData.part)

    pe.LightEmission = 0.8; pe.LightInfluence = 0
    pe.Size = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0.22),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,0)})
    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(3,5); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(180,180)
    pe.Rotation = NumberRange.new(0,360); pe.RotSpeed = NumberRange.new(-260,260)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.5,0.9); pe.Rate = 26; portalData._swirlEmitter = pe
end

function VFX.colorCycleAura(portalData)
    if not (portalData and portalData.halo) then return end
    local t = 0; local conn
    conn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not (portalData.halo and portalData.halo.Parent) then conn:Disconnect(); return end
        t = t + dt * 0.15; portalData.halo.Color = Color3.fromHSV(t % 1, 0.6, 1)
    end)
    portalData._colorCycleConn = conn
end

function VFX.floatingSparkMotes(portalData, color)

    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(0.4,1.0); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(180,180)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(2,4); pe.Rate = 6; portalData._moteEmitter = pe
end

function VFX.impactCrackDecals(result, color)
    if not result then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(90,180,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,150,60)
    for i = 1, 4 do
        local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
        part.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; part.Color = col
        part.Size = Vector3.new(0.03, math.random(4,10)/10, 0.03)
        local ang = math.rad(math.random(0,360))
        part.CFrame = CFrame.new(result.Position + result.Normal * 0.05,
            result.Position + result.Normal * 0.05 + result.Normal) * CFrame.Angles(math.pi/2, 0, ang)
        part.Transparency = 0.2; part.Parent = workspace
        tw(part, 0.6, {Transparency = 1}); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 0.7)
    end
end

function VFX.portalCoronaFlare(cf, color)
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(200,235,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,225,180)
    for _, rot in ipairs({0, 90}) do
        local flare = Instance.new("Part"); flare.Anchored = true; flare.CanCollide = false; flare.CanQuery = false
        flare.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; flare.Color = col
        flare.Size = Vector3.new(3.4, 0.05, 0.05)
        flare.CFrame = cf * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(rot)); flare.Transparency = 0.15; flare.Parent = workspace
        tw(flare, 0.35, {Size = Vector3.new(0.05,0.05,0.05), Transparency = 1}); vfxScheduleCleanup(flare, 0.5)
    end
end

function VFX.groundScorchRing(pos, color)
    local ring = Instance.new("Part"); ring.Anchored = true; ring.CanCollide = false; ring.CanQuery = false
    ring.Material = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic; ring.Color = Color3.fromRGB(20,20,20)
    ring.Transparency = 0.4; ring.Size = Vector3.new(2.6, 0.02, 2.6)
    ring.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos - Vector3.new(0,0.02,0)); ring.Parent = workspace
    local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Cylinder; mesh.Parent = ring
    safeDelay(4, function() tw(ring, 1.5, {Transparency = 1}) end); vfxScheduleCleanup(ring, 5.6)
end

function VFX.ambientFireflies(portalData, color)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(150,230,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,210,120)
    local part = portalData.part
    for i = 1, 3 do
        local orbitRadius = math.random(15,30)/10; local speed = math.random(6,14)/10
        local phase = math.random() * math.pi * 2
        local fly = Instance.new("Part"); fly.Anchored = true; fly.CanCollide = false; fly.CanQuery = false
        fly.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; fly.Color = col; fly.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
        fly.Size = Vector3.new(0.08,0.08,0.08); fly.Parent = workspace
        local light = Instance.new("PointLight"); light.Color = col; light.Range = 4; light.Brightness = 1; light.Parent = fly
        local t = 0; local conn
        conn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
            if not (part.Parent and fly.Parent) then
                pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end); pcall(function() fly:Destroy() end); return
            end
            t = t + dt * speed
            fly.CFrame = part.CFrame * CFrame.new(math.cos(t + phase) * orbitRadius, math.sin(t * 1.3 + phase) * orbitRadius * 0.6, 0.15)
        end)
        safeDelay(3, function() pcall(function() conn:Disconnect() end); pcall(function() fly:Destroy() end) end)
    end
end

function VFX.screenVignettePulse(color)
    local ok, cc = pcall(Instance.new, "ColorCorrectionEffect"); if not ok then return end
    cc.TintColor = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(180,220,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,210,170)
    cc.Saturation = 0.15; cc.Brightness = 0.05; cc.Parent = Lighting
    tw(cc, 0.3, {Brightness = 0, Saturation = 0}); safeDelay(0.4, function() pcall(function() cc:Destroy() end) end)
end

function VFX.rippleField(cf, color)
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(60,170,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,150,50)
    for i = 1, 3 do
        safeDelay(i * 0.12, function()
            local ring = Instance.new("Part"); ring.Anchored = true; ring.CanCollide = false; ring.CanQuery = false
            ring.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; ring.Color = col; ring.Transparency = 0.3
            ring.Size = Vector3.new(0.6, 0.6, 0.05); ring.CFrame = cf; ring.Parent = workspace
            local mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); mesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            mesh.Scale = Vector3.new(1,1,0.02); mesh.Parent = ring
            tw(ring, 0.5, {Size = Vector3.new(5,5,0.05), Transparency = 1}); vfxScheduleCleanup(ring, 0.6)
        end)
    end
end

function VFX.energyBeamPillar(cf, color)

    local pillar = Instance.new("Part"); pillar.Anchored = true; pillar.CanCollide = false; pillar.CanQuery = false
    pillar.Material = Enum.Material.Neon; pillar.Color = col; pillar.Transparency = 0.35
    pillar.Size = Vector3.new(0.3, 0.1, 0.3); pillar.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,0.02); pillar.Parent = workspace
    tw(pillar, 0.25, {Size = Vector3.new(0.3, 40, 0.3)})
    safeDelay(0.3, function() tw(pillar, 0.4, {Transparency = 1}) end); vfxScheduleCleanup(pillar, 0.8)
end

    local ghost = Instance.new("Part"); ghost.Anchored = true; ghost.CanCollide = false; ghost.CanQuery = false
    ghost.Material = Enum.Material.ForceField; ghost.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)

    tw(ghost, 0.4, {Transparency = 1, Size = Vector3.new(2.6,5.6,2.6)}); vfxScheduleCleanup(ghost, 0.5)
end

function VFX.dustKickup(pos)
    local part = Instance.new("Part"); part.Anchored = true; part.CanCollide = false; part.CanQuery = false
    part.Transparency = 1; part.Size = Vector3.new(0.2,0.2,0.2)
    part.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos - Vector3.new(0,2.9,0)); part.Parent = workspace
    local att = vfxAttachment(part)
    local pe = vfxBurstEmitter(att, Color3.fromRGB(140,130,110), {
        startSize = 0.5, speed = NumberRange.new(2, 6), spread = Vector2.new(360, 0),
        lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.4, 0.8), lightEmission = 0, direction = Enum.NormalId.Top,
    })
    vfxEmitBurst(pe, 14); vfxScheduleCleanup(part, 1)
end

function VFX.auraTrailOnPlayer(hrp, color, duration)
    if not hrp then return end
    local col = color == "blue" and Color3.fromRGB(100,190,255) or Color3.fromRGB(255,160,60)
    local att = vfxAttachment(hrp)
    local pe = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter"); pe.Parent = att; pe.Color = ColorSequence.new(col)
    pe.LightEmission = 0.5
    pe.Size = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0.18),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,0)})
    pe.Transparency = NumberSequence.new({NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0.3),NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1)})
    pe.Speed = NumberRange.new(0.5,1.5); pe.SpreadAngle = Vector2.new(30,30)
    pe.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.5,0.9); pe.Rate = 40
    safeDelay(duration or 1.5, function()
        pe.Rate = 0; safeDelay(1, function() pcall(function() att:Destroy() end) end)
    end)
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PLACE PORTAL
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local fireCooldown   = false
local recoilT        = 0     -- seconds of recoil kick remaining
local reloadActive   = false
local reloadProgress = 0
local RELOAD_DUR     = 1.15  -- total reload animation length in seconds

local function triggerReload()
    if reloadActive or not toolEquipped then return end
    reloadActive   = true
    reloadProgress = 0
end

local function easeInOut(t)
    t = math.clamp(t, 0, 1)
    return t < 0.5 and 2*t*t or -1 + (4 - 2*t)*t
end

local function placePortal(color)
    if not gunEnabled then return end
    if fireCooldown then return end
    local hrp = getHRP(); if not hrp then return end

    recoilT = 0.22   -- kick arms back for 0.22 s
    playSound(CFG.sndFire, hrp)
    local result = doRaycast()
    if not result or not isValidSurface(result) then return end

    fireCooldown = true; safeDelay(0.15, function() fireCooldown = false end)

    local cf = portalCF(result)
    if portals[color] then
        local old = portals[color]; portals[color] = nil
        playSound(CFG.sndClose, old.part); animateClose(old)
        pcall(function() VFX.onPortalClose(old, color) end)
    end
    local d = makePortalPart(color)
    d.cf = cf; portals[color] = d
    animateOpen(d, cf); playSound(CFG.sndCreate, d.part)
    pcall(function() VFX.onPortalOpen(d, cf, color) end)
    pcall(function() VFX.muzzleFlash(color) end)
    pcall(function() VFX.impactScorch(result, color) end)
    pcall(function() VFX.spawnBeamTrail(hrp.Position, result.Position, color, {width = 0.25, fadeTime = 0.3}) end)

    if CFG.vfxLightning   then pcall(function() VFX.lightningArcs(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxEmbers      then pcall(function() VFX.emberShower(cf, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxShockwave   then pcall(function() VFX.shockwaveGround(result.Position, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxTendrils    then pcall(function() VFX.energyTendrils(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxStarburst   then pcall(function() VFX.starburst(result.Position, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxGlyphs      then pcall(function() VFX.glyphRing(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxHaze        then pcall(function() VFX.distortionHaze(d) end) end
    if CFG.vfxWindGust    then pcall(function() VFX.portalWindGust(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxRimArcs     then pcall(function() VFX.rimLightning(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxVortexLoop  then pcall(function() VFX.vortexSwirlLoop(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxColorCycle  then pcall(function() VFX.colorCycleAura(d) end) end
    if CFG.vfxFloatMotes  then pcall(function() VFX.floatingSparkMotes(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxCrackDecals then pcall(function() VFX.impactCrackDecals(result, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxCoronaFlare then pcall(function() VFX.portalCoronaFlare(cf, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxScorchRing  then pcall(function() VFX.groundScorchRing(result.Position, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxFireflies   then pcall(function() VFX.ambientFireflies(d, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxVignette    then pcall(function() VFX.screenVignettePulse(color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxRipple      then pcall(function() VFX.rippleField(cf, color) end) end
    if CFG.vfxBeamPillar  then pcall(function() VFX.energyBeamPillar(cf, color) end) end
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  CLOSE ALL PORTALS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function closePortals()
    for _, color in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
        if portals[color] then
            local d = portals[color]; portals[color] = nil
            playSound(CFG.sndClose, d.part); animateClose(d)
            pcall(function() VFX.onPortalClose(d, color) end)
        end
    end
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  TELEPORTATION
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function cameraShake()
    if CFG.shakeAmt <= 0 then return end
    local steps = 10; local dt = CFG.shakeDur / steps
    for i = 1, steps do
        local s = CFG.shakeAmt * (1 - i/steps)
        pcall(function()
            Cam.CFrame = Cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(
                (math.random()-0.5)*2*s, (math.random()-0.5)*2*s, 0)
        end)
        safeWait(dt)
    end
end

local function teleportPlayer(fromData, toData)
    local hrp = getHRP(); if not hrp then return end
    local fromCF = fromData.cf; local toCF = toData.cf
    local worldUp = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
    local relPos  = fromCF:PointToObjectSpace(hrp.Position)
    local exitPos = toCF:PointToWorldSpace(Vector3.new(-relPos.X, relPos.Y, 0))
    local exitNormal = toCF.LookVector
    exitPos = exitPos + exitNormal * 2.5
    local flatNormal = Vector3.new(exitNormal.X, 0, exitNormal.Z)
    local exitLookDir
    if flatNormal.Magnitude > 0.15 then
        exitLookDir = flatNormal.Unit
    else
        local portalUp = toCF.UpVector; local flatUp = Vector3.new(portalUp.X, 0, portalUp.Z)
        if flatUp.Magnitude > 0.15 then
            exitLookDir = flatUp.Unit
        else
            local cur = hrp.CFrame.LookVector; local flatCur = Vector3.new(cur.X, 0, cur.Z)
            exitLookDir = flatCur.Magnitude > 0.01 and flatCur.Unit or Vector3.new(0,0,-1)
        end
    end
    local exitCF = CFrame.lookAt(exitPos, exitPos + exitLookDir, worldUp)
    local vel    = hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity
    local locVel = fromCF:VectorToObjectSpace(vel)
    local exitVel = toCF:VectorToWorldSpace(
        Vector3.new(-locVel.X, locVel.Y, -locVel.Z) * CFG.velocityMult)
    hrp.CFrame = exitCF; hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = exitVel
    playSound(CFG.sndTeleport, hrp); safeSpawn(cameraShake)
    pcall(function() VFX.onTeleport(fromData, toData, hrp) end)
    if CFG.screenFlash then
        local ok, cc = pcall(Instance.new, "ColorCorrectionEffect")
        if ok then
            cc.Brightness = 0.45; cc.Parent = Lighting
            tw(cc, 0.35, {Brightness=0})
            safeDelay(0.4, function() pcall(function() cc:Destroy() end) end)
        end
    end
    local exitColor = fromData and fromData == portals.blue and "orange" or "blue"
    if CFG.vfxShatter    then pcall(function() VFX.teleportShatter(hrp, exitColor) end) end
    if CFG.vfxGhostTrail then pcall(function() VFX.teleportGhostTrail(hrp) end) end
    if CFG.vfxDustKick   then pcall(function() VFX.dustKickup(hrp.Position) end) end
    if CFG.vfxPlayerAura then pcall(function() VFX.auraTrailOnPlayer(hrp, exitColor, 2.0) end) end
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  HEARTBEAT — teleport detection
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if not gunEnabled then return end
    local now = tick(); local hrp = getHRP(); if not hrp then return end
    if now - lastTeleport >= CFG.cooldown and portals.blue and portals.orange then
        local function check(enter, exit)
            local rel = enter.cf:PointToObjectSpace(hrp.Position)
            local hw  = CFG.portalWidth  * 0.5; local hh = CFG.portalHeight * 0.5
            if (rel.X/hw)^2 + (rel.Y/hh)^2 < 1 and math.abs(rel.Z) < 3.5 then
                lastTeleport = now; teleportPlayer(enter, exit); return true
            end
            return false
        end
        if not check(portals.blue, portals.orange) then check(portals.orange, portals.blue) end
    end
end)

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  GUI HELPERS
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function corner(inst, radius)
    local c = Instance.new("UICorner"); c.CornerRadius = radius or UDim.new(0,10); c.Parent = inst
end
local function stroke(inst, thickness, color, trans)
    local s = Instance.new("UIStroke"); s.Thickness = thickness or 1.5
    s.Color = color or Color3.new(1,1,1); s.Transparency = trans or 0.7; s.Parent = inst
end
local function makeLabel(parent, text, size, color, font, align, zIndex)
    local l = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    l.BackgroundTransparency = 1; l.Text = text; l.TextSize = size or 13
    l.TextColor3 = color or Color3.new(1,1,1); l.Font = font or Enum.Font.GothamBold
    l.TextXAlignment = align or Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
    l.ZIndex = zIndex or 1; l.Parent = parent; return l
end
local function makeBtn(parent, text, bg, pos, sz, zIndex)
    local b = Instance.new("TextButton")
    b.Size = sz or UDim2.new(0,80,0,40); b.Position = pos or UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
    b.BackgroundColor3 = bg or Color3.fromRGB(40,40,70); b.BorderSizePixel = 0
    b.Text = text; b.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1); b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    b.TextSize = 13; b.ZIndex = zIndex or 2; b.Parent = parent
    corner(b, UDim.new(0,10)); return b
end
local function makeDraggable(panel, handle)
    local drag, ds, sp = false, nil, nil
    handle.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
        if uiLocked then return end
        local ut = inp.UserInputType
        if ut == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or ut == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            drag = true; ds = inp.Position; sp = panel.Position
            inp.Changed:Connect(function()
                if inp.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then drag = false end
            end)
        end
    end)
    handle.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
        if not drag then return end
        local ut = inp.UserInputType
        if ut == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or ut == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            local d = inp.Position - ds
            panel.Position = UDim2.new(sp.X.Scale, sp.X.Offset+d.X, sp.Y.Scale, sp.Y.Offset+d.Y)
        end
    end)
end
local function addMinimizeButton(panel, titleBar, minBtn)
    local fullSize = panel.Size; local barHeight = titleBar.Size.Y.Offset
    local minimized = false; local hidden = {}
    minBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        minimized = not minimized
        if minimized then
            for _, child in ipairs(panel:GetChildren()) do
                if child ~= titleBar and child:IsA("GuiObject") then
                    hidden[child] = child.Visible; child.Visible = false
                end
            end
            tw(panel, 0.18, {Size = UDim2.new(fullSize.X.Scale, fullSize.X.Offset, 0, barHeight)})
            minBtn.Text = "▢"
        else
            tw(panel, 0.18, {Size = fullSize})
            for child, wasVisible in pairs(hidden) do
                if child.Parent then child.Visible = wasVisible end
            end
            hidden = {}; minBtn.Text = "—"
        end
    end)
end

-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  RENDER STEPPED — HUD updates
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
--  PORTAL CAMERA TRANSFORM  (runs inside RenderStepped below)
--
--  For each placed portal, the linked ViewportFrame camera is updated so
--  it matches what you would see from the exit portal:
--
--    1. Express the player camera's CFrame in the entrance portal's local
--       space  →  relCF
--    2. Flip 180° around the portal's Y axis so the camera looks OUT
--       through the exit instead of INTO it  →  flipCF * relCF
--    3. Transform the result into world space via the exit portal's CFrame.
--
--  Portal A's viewport shows Portal B's outward view, and vice-versa.
-- ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _PORTAL_CAM_FLIP = CFrame.Angles(0, math.pi, 0)

local function updatePortalCameras()
    local blue   = portals.blue
    local orange = portals.orange
    -- Both portals must exist and their vpCams must still be valid.
    if not (blue and orange) then return end
    if not (blue.vpCam and blue.vpCam.Parent) then return end
    if not (orange.vpCam and orange.vpCam.Parent) then return end

    local playerCamCF = Cam.CFrame

    -- Blue portal's viewport → shows the view from inside the orange portal
    pcall(function()
        local relCF = blue.cf:ToObjectSpace(playerCamCF)
        blue.vpCam.CFrame = orange.cf * _PORTAL_CAM_FLIP * relCF
        blue.vpCam.FieldOfView = Cam.FieldOfView
    end)

    -- Orange portal's viewport → shows the view from inside the blue portal
    pcall(function()
        local relCF = orange.cf:ToObjectSpace(playerCamCF)
        orange.vpCam.CFrame = blue.cf * _PORTAL_CAM_FLIP * relCF
        orange.vpCam.FieldOfView = Cam.FieldOfView
    end)
end

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
    local result = doRaycast(); updatePreview(result)
    -- Update each portal's viewport camera every render frame
    pcall(updatePortalCameras)
    if not gunEnabled then return end
    local cc = selColor=="blue" and CFG.blueColor or CFG.orangeColor
    xhInner.BackgroundColor3 = cc; xhOuter.BackgroundColor3 = cc
    blueDot.BackgroundTransparency = portals.blue   and 0.0 or 0.8
    orngDot.BackgroundTransparency = portals.orange and 0.0 or 0.8
    blueDot.BackgroundColor3 = CFG.blueColor; orngDot.BackgroundColor3 = CFG.orangeColor
    if selColor=="blue" then
        crosshairLbl.Text = "● BLUE"; crosshairLbl.TextColor3 = CFG.blueColor
    else
        crosshairLbl.Text = "● ORANGE"; crosshairLbl.TextColor3 = CFG.orangeColor
    end
    if portalRotation ~= 0 or portalTilt ~= 0 then
        rotBadge.Visible = true
        rotLabel.Text = "↻ " .. tostring(portalRotation) .. "°  ↕ " .. tostring(portalTilt) .. "°"
    else
        rotBadge.Visible = false
    end
end)

toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    gunEnabled = not gunEnabled
    toggleBtn.Text = gunEnabled and "● ON" or "○ OFF"
    toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = gunEnabled and Color3.fromRGB(30,160,60) or Color3.fromRGB(120,40,40)
    if not gunEnabled then
        if prevPart then prevPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(0,-9999,0) end
        xhInner.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100,100,100)
        xhOuter.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100,100,100)
    end
end)

local TAB_NAMES = {"Colors", "Size", "Advanced", "VFX"}
local tabBtns = {}; local tabPages = {}

local tabBar = Instance.new("Frame")
tabBar.Size = UDim2.new(1,-14,0,34); tabBar.Position = UDim2.new(0,7,0,50)
tabBar.BackgroundTransparency = 1; tabBar.ZIndex = 31; tabBar.Parent = settingsPanel

local function makePage()
    local sf = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
    sf.Size = UDim2.new(1,-14,1,-96); sf.Position = UDim2.new(0,7,0,88)
    sf.BackgroundTransparency = 1; sf.BorderSizePixel = 0
    sf.ScrollBarThickness = 4; sf.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60,130,255)
    sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0); sf.Visible = false; sf.ZIndex = 31; sf.Parent = settingsPanel
    local layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout"); layout.Padding = UDim.new(0,6); layout.Parent = sf
    layout:GetPropertyChangedSignal("AbsoluteContentSize"):Connect(function()
        sf.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,layout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 10)
    end)
    return sf
end

for i, name in ipairs(TAB_NAMES) do
    local btn = makeBtn(tabBar, name, Color3.fromRGB(28,28,50), UDim2.new(0,(i-1)*136,0,2), UDim2.new(0,130,0,30), 32)
    corner(btn, UDim.new(0,8)); tabBtns[name] = btn; tabPages[name] = makePage()
end

local activeTab = ""
local function switchTab(name)
    if activeTab == name then return end; activeTab = name
    for n, btn in pairs(tabBtns) do
        btn.BackgroundColor3 = (n==name) and Color3.fromRGB(0,85,185) or Color3.fromRGB(28,28,50)
        btn.TextColor3 = (n==name) and Color3.new(1,1,1) or Color3.fromRGB(170,170,200)
    end
    for n, page in pairs(tabPages) do page.Visible = (n==name) end
end
for name, btn in pairs(tabBtns) do btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() switchTab(name) end) end
switchTab("Colors")

-- ── Widget helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function sectionLbl(parent, text)
    local l = makeLabel(parent, text, 11, Color3.fromRGB(90,155,255), Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 32)
    l.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,20)
end

local function makeSlider(parent, labelText, minV, maxV, initV, fmt, onChange)
    fmt = fmt or "%.1f"
    local container = Instance.new("Frame"); container.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,52)
    container.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20,20,38); container.BorderSizePixel = 0
    container.ZIndex = 32; container.Parent = parent; corner(container, UDim.new(0,8))
    local nl = makeLabel(container, labelText, 12, Color3.fromRGB(210,210,230), Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 33)
    nl.Size = UDim2.new(0.6,0,0,18); nl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,4)
    local vl = makeLabel(container, string.format(fmt, initV), 12, Color3.fromRGB(140,210,255), Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Right, 33)
    vl.Size = UDim2.new(0.35,0,0,18); vl.Position = UDim2.new(0.65,-6,0,4)
    local track = Instance.new("Frame"); track.Size = UDim2.new(1,-20,0,8); track.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,32)
    track.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(38,38,62); track.BorderSizePixel = 0; track.ZIndex = 33; track.Parent = container
    corner(track, UDim.new(0.5,0))
    local fill = Instance.new("Frame"); fill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,115,255)
    fill.BorderSizePixel = 0; fill.ZIndex = 34; fill.Parent = track; corner(fill, UDim.new(0.5,0))
    local knob = Instance.new("Frame"); knob.Size = UDim2.new(0,14,0,14)
    knob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1); knob.BorderSizePixel = 0; knob.ZIndex = 35; knob.Parent = track
    corner(knob, UDim.new(0.5,0))
    local cur = initV
    local function setValue(v)
        v = clamp(v, minV, maxV); cur = v; local pct = (v-minV)/(maxV-minV)
        fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct,0,1,0); knob.Position = UDim2.new(pct,-7,0.5,-7)
        vl.Text = string.format(fmt, v); if onChange then onChange(v) end
    end
    setValue(initV)
    local dragging = false
    local function onInp(inp)
        local ap = track.AbsolutePosition; local as = track.AbsoluteSize
        setValue(lerp(minV, maxV, clamp((inp.Position.X-ap.X)/as.X, 0, 1)))
    end
    track.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
        local ut = inp.UserInputType
        if ut==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or ut==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging=true; onInp(inp)
            inp.Changed:Connect(function() if inp.UserInputState==Enum.UserInputState.End then dragging=false end end)
        end
    end)
    track.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
        if not dragging then return end
        local ut = inp.UserInputType
        if ut==Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or ut==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then onInp(inp) end
    end)
    return container, setValue
end

local function makeSwatchRow(parent, presets, setColor)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame"); row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,38)
    row.BackgroundTransparency = 1; row.ZIndex = 32; row.Parent = parent
    for i, p in ipairs(presets) do
        local sw = Instance.new("TextButton"); sw.Size = UDim2.new(0,32,0,32)
        sw.Position = UDim2.new(0,(i-1)*36+4,0,3); sw.BackgroundColor3 = p.color
        sw.BorderSizePixel = 0; sw.Text = ""; sw.ZIndex = 33; sw.Parent = row
        corner(sw, UDim.new(0.5,0)); stroke(sw, 2, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.6)
        sw.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() setColor(p.color); refreshPortalVisuals() end)
    end
end

local function makeRGBSliders(parent, getColor, setColor)
    local con = Instance.new("Frame"); con.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,106)
    con.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18,18,34); con.BorderSizePixel = 0; con.ZIndex = 32; con.Parent = parent
    corner(con, UDim.new(0,8))
    local CHANNELS = {{"R","R",Color3.fromRGB(255,90,90)},{"G","G",Color3.fromRGB(90,220,90)},{"B","B",Color3.fromRGB(90,140,255)}}
    for i, ch in ipairs(CHANNELS) do
        local ltr, key, lcol = ch[1], ch[2], ch[3]; local yOff = (i-1)*32+10
        local lbl = makeLabel(con, ltr, 12, lcol, Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, 33)
        lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0,14,0,20); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,8,0,yOff+4)
        local track = Instance.new("Frame"); track.Size = UDim2.new(1,-72,0,8)
        track.Position = UDim2.new(0,26,0,yOff+10); track.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(38,38,62)
        track.BorderSizePixel = 0; track.ZIndex = 33; track.Parent = con; corner(track,UDim.new(0.5,0))
        local fill = Instance.new("Frame"); fill.BackgroundColor3 = lcol
        fill.BorderSizePixel = 0; fill.ZIndex = 34; fill.Parent = track; corner(fill,UDim.new(0.5,0))
        local knob = Instance.new("Frame"); knob.Size = UDim2.new(0,12,0,12)
        knob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1); knob.BorderSizePixel = 0; knob.ZIndex = 35; knob.Parent = track
        corner(knob,UDim.new(0.5,0))
        local vlbl = makeLabel(con, "0", 11, Color3.fromRGB(180,180,210), Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Right, 33)
        vlbl.Size = UDim2.new(0,34,0,18); vlbl.Position = UDim2.new(1,-40,0,yOff+6)
        local function set(v)
            v = clamp(math.floor(v+0.5), 0, 255); local pct = v/255
            fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct,0,1,0); knob.Position = UDim2.new(pct,-6,0.5,-6); vlbl.Text = tostring(v)
            local c = getColor()
            setColor(Color3.new(key=="R" and v/255 or c.R, key=="G" and v/255 or c.G, key=="B" and v/255 or c.B))
            refreshPortalVisuals()
        end
        set(getColor()[key] * 255)
        local dragging = false
        local function onInp(inp)
            local ap = track.AbsolutePosition; local as = track.AbsoluteSize
            set(clamp((inp.Position.X-ap.X)/as.X, 0, 1)*255)
        end
        track.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
            local ut = inp.UserInputType
            if ut==Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or ut==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                dragging=true; onInp(inp)
                inp.Changed:Connect(function() if inp.UserInputState==Enum.UserInputState.End then dragging=false end end)
            end
        end)
        track.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
            if not dragging then return end
            local ut = inp.UserInputType
            if ut==Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or ut==Enum.UserInputType.Touch then onInp(inp) end
        end)
    end
    return con
end

local function makeToggle(parent, label, getV, setV)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame"); row.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,42)
    row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20,20,38); row.BorderSizePixel = 0; row.ZIndex = 32; row.Parent = parent
    corner(row, UDim.new(0,8))
    local lbl = makeLabel(row, label, 12, Color3.fromRGB(210,210,230), Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 33)
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.7,0,1,0); lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)
    local btn = makeBtn(row, "", Color3.fromRGB(40,180,60), UDim2.new(1,-70,0.5,-14), UDim2.new(0,60,0,28), 33)
    corner(btn, UDim.new(0,6))
    local function refresh()
        local on = getV(); btn.Text = on and "ON" or "OFF"
        btn.BackgroundColor3 = on and Color3.fromRGB(40,180,60) or Color3.fromRGB(120,40,40)
    end
    refresh(); btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() setV(not getV()); refresh() end)
end

local function sep(parent)
    local f = Instance.new("Frame"); f.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,1)
    f.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45,45,75); f.BorderSizePixel = 0; f.Parent = parent
end

    makeToggle(p, "⚡ Lightning Arcs",       function() return CFG.vfxLightning   end, function(on) CFG.vfxLightning=on   end)
