-- ── Notification system ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _notifSG = _getOrMakeSS("Notifs")

local function _showNotif(icon, title, body, col, dur)
    local w    = 320
    local h    = 58
    local yOff = #_UPG.notifQueue * (h + 6) + 10

    local card = _frame(_notifSG, {
        Name            = "Notif_"..tostring(_UPG.frameT),
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,w,0,h),
        Position        = UDim2.new(1,w+10,0, yOff),
        BackgroundColor3= col or Color3.fromRGB(12,12,28),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.08,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ZIndex          = 50,
    })
    _corner(card, UDim.new(0,10))
    _stroke(card, 1.5, col or Color3.fromRGB(60,130,255), 0.35)

    local iconLbl = _label(card, icon or "●", 20, Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, 51)
    iconLbl.Size     = UDim2.new(0,38,1,0)
    iconLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,6,0,0)

    local titleLbl = _label(card, title or "", 12, Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 51)
    titleLbl.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-56,0,18)
    titleLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,50,0,8)

    local bodyLbl = _label(card, body or "", 10, Color3.fromRGB(180,190,210),
        Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 51)
    bodyLbl.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-56,0,14)
    bodyLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,50,0,28)

    -- Slide in
    _tw(card, 0.3, { Position = UDim2.new(1,-w-10, 0, yOff) },
        Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)

    table.insert(_UPG.notifQueue, card)

    -- Auto-dismiss
    _delay(dur or 3.5, function()
        _tw(card, 0.3, { Position = UDim2.new(1, w+10, 0, yOff),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1 })
        _delay(0.35, function()
            pcall(function() card:Destroy() end)
            for i, c in ipairs(_UPG.notifQueue) do
                if c == card then table.remove(_UPG.notifQueue, i); break end
            end
        end)
    end)
end

-- ── Keybind overlay (H to toggle) ───────────────────────────────────────────
do
    local kbSG   = _getOrMakeSS("Keybinds")
    local kbPanel= _frame(kbSG, {
        Name            = "KeybindPanel",
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,280,0,280),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0,10,0.5,-140),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,8,20),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Visible         = false,
        ZIndex          = 40,
    })
    _corner(kbPanel, UDim.new(0,14))
    _stroke(kbPanel, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(50,110,220), 0.4)

    local kbTitle = _label(kbPanel, "⌨  Keybinds", 14, Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 41)
    kbTitle.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-16,0,22)
    kbTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0,14,0,8)

    local kbDivider = _frame(kbPanel, {
        Size            = UDim2.new(1,-28,0,1),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0,14,0,34),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(50,80,160),
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ZIndex          = 41,
    })

    local kbBinds = {
        {"LMB",       "Fire Blue portal"},
        {"RMB / Q",   "Fire Orange portal"},
        {"R",         "Close all portals"},
        {"Z / X",     "Switch color"},
        {"[ / ]",     "Rotate portal −/+15°"},
        {"; / '",     "Tilt portal −/+15°"},
        {"\\",        "Reset rotation"},
        {"H",         "Toggle this overlay"},
        {"F1",        "Toggle debug info"},
        {"⚙  button", "Settings & VFX"},
    }
    for i, kb in ipairs(kbBinds) do
        local row = _frame(kbPanel, {
            Size            = UDim2.new(1,-28,0,20),
            Position        = UDim2.new(0,14,0,38+(i-1)*22),
            BackgroundTransparency = 1,
            ZIndex          = 41,
        })
        local keyLbl = _label(row, kb[1], 10, Color3.fromRGB(180,210,255),
            Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 42)
        keyLbl.Size     = UDim2.new(0,80,1,0)
        keyLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)

        local actLbl = _label(row, kb[2], 10, Color3.fromRGB(200,210,230),
            Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 42)
        actLbl.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-90,1,0)
        actLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,90,0,0)
    end

    _gv3.kbPanel = kbPanel

    -- H key toggle
    _UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp, gpe)
        if gpe then return end
        if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
            kbPanel.Visible = not kbPanel.Visible
        end
    end)
end

-- ── GUI v3 per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    local t   = _UPG.frameT
    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

    -- Crosshair bracket animation: slight scale pulse
    if _gv3.xhBrackets then
        local pulse = 1 + _sin(t*2.2) * 0.04
        for _, br in ipairs(_gv3.xhBrackets) do
            -- subtle color shift
            local b = 0.5 + _sin(t*1.4)*0.5
            local col2 = _gv3.xhColor
            br.h.BackgroundColor3 = col2
            br.v.BackgroundColor3 = col2
        end
    end

    -- Portal status cards
    local exB  = _UPG.portalExtras.blue
    local exO  = _UPG.portalExtras.orange
    local bothOpen = exB ~= nil and exO ~= nil

    if _gv3.blueStatusLbl then
        if exB then
            _gv3.blueStatusLbl.Text = "BLUE  ●  ACTIVE"
            _gv3.blueDot.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            if hrp and exB.beamAnchor then
                local d = math.floor((exB.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude)
                _gv3.blueInfoLbl.Text = "Dist: " .. d .. " studs"
            end
        else
            _gv3.blueStatusLbl.Text = "BLUE  ○  —"
            _gv3.blueDot.BackgroundTransparency = 0.6
            _gv3.blueInfoLbl.Text = "No portal"
        end
    end

    if _gv3.orangeStatusLbl then
        if exO then
            _gv3.orangeStatusLbl.Text = "ORANGE  ●  ACTIVE"
            _gv3.orangeDot.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            if hrp and exO.beamAnchor then
                local d = math.floor((exO.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude)
                _gv3.orangeInfoLbl.Text = "Dist: " .. d .. " studs"
            end
        else
            _gv3.orangeStatusLbl.Text = "ORANGE  ○  —"
            _gv3.orangeDot.BackgroundTransparency = 0.6
            _gv3.orangeInfoLbl.Text = "No portal"
        end
    end

    -- Connection line color pulse
    if _gv3.connLine then
        if bothOpen then
            _gv3.connLine.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(
                0.5 + _sin(t*3)*0.5, 0.5 + _sin(t*3+2.09)*0.5, 0.5 + _sin(t*3+4.18)*0.5)
            _gv3.connLine.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 + _abs(_sin(t*2))*0.3
        else
            _gv3.connLine.BackgroundTransparency = 0.85
        end
    end

    -- Minimap update
    if _gv3.minimap and hrp then
        local hasBlue   = exB ~= nil
        local hasOrange = exO ~= nil
        local hasAny    = hasBlue or hasOrange
        _gv3.mmNoPortals.Visible = not hasAny

        if hasAny then
            local scale = 1/80  -- 80 studs = full minimap width
            local mmSz  = _gv3.mmSize - 20

            if hasBlue and exB.beamAnchor then
                local rel  = exB.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position
                local mmX  = _clamp(rel.X * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local mmZ  = _clamp(rel.Z * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                _gv3.mmBlue.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, mmX-5, 0.5, mmZ-5+8)
                _gv3.mmBlue.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            else
                _gv3.mmBlue.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            end

            if hasOrange and exO.beamAnchor then
                local rel  = exO.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position
                local mmX  = _clamp(rel.X * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local mmZ  = _clamp(rel.Z * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                _gv3.mmOrange.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, mmX-5, 0.5, mmZ-5+8)
                _gv3.mmOrange.BackgroundTransparency = 0
            else
                _gv3.mmOrange.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            end

            -- Draw connection line on minimap
            if hasBlue and hasOrange and exB.beamAnchor and exO.beamAnchor then
                local bRel = exB.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position
                local oRel = exO.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position
                local bX   = _clamp(bRel.X * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local bZ   = _clamp(bRel.Z * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local oX   = _clamp(oRel.X * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local oZ   = _clamp(oRel.Z * scale * mmSz, -mmSz/2, mmSz/2)
                local dx   = oX - bX
                local dz   = oZ - bZ
                local len  = _sqrt(dx*dx + dz*dz)
                local ang  = math.atan2(dz, dx)
                _gv3.mmConnLine.Size        = UDim2.new(0, len, 0, 1)
                _gv3.mmConnLine.Position    = UDim2.new(0.5, bX+5, 0.5, bZ+8)
                _gv3.mmConnLine.Rotation    = math.deg(ang)
                _gv3.mmConnLine.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
            else
                _gv3.mmConnLine.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  SECTION 4 — VFX EXPANSION PACK  (+30 new effects)
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local VFX2 = {}

-- ─── Plasma Flood: fills portal face with expanding energy on open ────────────
function VFX2.plasmaFlood(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numWaves = 5
    for wi = 1, numWaves do
        _delay(wi * 0.06, function()
            local wave = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*0.1, ph*0.1, 0.05),
                Transparency= 0.3,
                CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.04),
            })
            local wMesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            wMesh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            wMesh.Scale    = Vector3.new(1,1,0.03)
            wMesh.Parent   = wave
            wave.Parent    = _WS
            _tw(wave, 0.25, { Size = Vector3.new(pw*1.05, ph*1.05, 0.05), Transparency = 0.85 })
            _gc(wave, 0.35)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Dimensional Tear: crack in space at impact point ───────────────────────
function VFX2.dimensionalTear(cf, col)
    local numShards = 16
    for i = 1, numShards do
        local ang  = (i/numShards) * TAU + _rand()*0.4
        local len  = 0.8 + _rand() * 1.8
        local p    = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = col,
            Size        = Vector3.new(len, 0.04, 0.04),
            Transparency= 0.1,
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*0.6, _sin(ang)*0.6, 0)
                            * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, ang + math.pi/2),
        })
        p.Parent = _WS
        _tw(p, 0.35 + _rand()*0.15, {
            Size        = Vector3.new(len*0.1, 0.02, 0.02),
            Transparency= 1,
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*(0.6+len*0.6),
                _sin(ang)*(0.6+len*0.6), 0)
                * CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2),
        })
        _gc(p, 0.55)
    end
end

-- ─── Portal Energy Nova: large expanding ring on portal open ─────────────────
function VFX2.portalEnergyNova(cf, col, pw)
    for ri = 1, 3 do
        _delay(ri * 0.07, function()
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*0.5, pw*0.5, 0.04),
                Transparency= 0.0,
                CFrame      = cf,
            })
            local msh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            msh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
            msh.MeshId   = "rbxassetid://3270017987"
            msh.Scale    = Vector3.new(pw*0.4, pw*0.4, 0.15)
            msh.Parent   = ring
            ring.Parent  = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.55, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*2.2+ri, pw*2.2+ri, 0.04),
                Transparency= 1,
            }, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
            _gc(ring, 0.60)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Teleport Echo Ghost: ghostly duplicate fades at entry ───────────────────
function VFX2.teleportEchoGhost(hrp, col)
    if not hrp then return end
    local char  = hrp.Parent
    if not char then return end
    local folder = Instance.new("Folder"); folder.Parent = _WS

    for _, part in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") and part ~= hrp then
            local ghost = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = part.Size,
                CFrame      = part.CFrame,
                Transparency= 0.3,
            })
            ghost.Parent = folder
            _tw(ghost, UCFG.echoFadeDur, { Transparency = 1 })
        end
    end
    -- Ghost HRP
    local gHRP = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = hrp.Size,
        CFrame      = hrp.CFrame,
        Transparency= 0.25,
    })
    gHRP.Parent = folder
    _tw(gHRP, UCFG.echoFadeDur, { Transparency = 1 })
    _gc(folder, UCFG.echoFadeDur + 0.1)
end

-- ─── Portal Gravity Vortex: particles spiral INTO portal ─────────────────────
function VFX2.gravityVortexBurst(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numP = 32
    for i = 1, numP do
        local ang    = (i/numP) * TAU + _rand()*0.3
        local startR = pw * (1 + _rand() * 0.5)
        local sx     = _cos(ang) * startR
        local sy     = _sin(ang) * startR * (ph/pw)
        local p = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = col,
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.12, 0.12, 0.12),
            Transparency= 0.1,
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(sx, sy, _rand()*0.3 - 0.15),
        })
        p.Parent = _WS
        _tw(p, 0.4 + _rand()*0.2, {
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(_rand()*0.3-0.15, _rand()*0.3-0.15, -0.1),
            Transparency= 1,
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.02, 0.02, 0.02),
        })
        _gc(p, 0.65)
    end
end

-- ─── Electric Crown: halo of arcing electricity at portal top ────────────────
function VFX2.electricCrown(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numArcs = 8
    local topCF   = cf * CFrame.new(0, ph*0.5 + 0.3, 0)
    for i = 1, numArcs do
        local ang  = (i/numArcs) * TAU
        local endX = _cos(ang) * (pw * 0.35)
        local endY = _sin(ang) * 0.5
        local p1   = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = col,
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.03, 0.03, 0.03),
            Transparency= 0,
            CFrame      = topCF,
        })
        p1.Parent = _WS
        local p2 = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = col,
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.03,0.03,0.03),
            Transparency= 0,
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(endX, ph*0.5+0.1+endY, 0),
        })
        p2.Parent = _WS

        local a0 = _att(p1)
        local a1 = _att(p2)
        local b  = Instance.new("Beam")
        b.Attachment0    = a0
        b.Attachment1    = a1
        b.Color          = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.5, col, 1, Color3.new(1,1,1))
        b.Width0         = 0.04
        b.Width1         = 0.02
        b.LightEmission  = 1
        b.Transparency   = NumberSequence.new(0.1)
        b.Segments       = 6
        b.CurveSize0     = _rand() * 0.4 - 0.2
        b.CurveSize1     = _rand() * 0.4 - 0.2
        b.Parent         = p1
        _delay(0.25 + _rand()*0.2, function()
            _tw(p1, 0.15, { Transparency = 1 })
            _tw(p2, 0.15, { Transparency = 1 })
        end)
        _gc(p1, 0.55)
        _gc(p2, 0.55)
    end
end

-- ─── Smoke Wisps: rising smoke from portal base edges ───────────────────────
function VFX2.smokeWisps(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local softCol = Color3.new(col.R*0.4, col.G*0.4, col.B*0.4)
    for side = -1, 1, 2 do
        local wisp = _part({
            Transparency= 1,
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
            CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(side * pw * 0.45, -ph*0.5 + 0.2, 0),
        })
        wisp.Parent = _WS
        local wAtt  = _att(wisp)
        local wPE   = _pe(wAtt, {
            Color        = _cs(0, softCol, 0.5, col, 1, Color3.fromRGB(200,200,200)),
            LightEmission= 0.2, LightInfluence = 0.8,
            Size         = _ns(0,0.3, 0.5,0.6, 1,0),
            Speed        = NumberRange.new(0.8, 1.8),
            SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(12,12),
            Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(1.5, 2.8),
            Rate         = 3,
            Transparency = _ns(0,0.5, 1,1),
            Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0,360),
            RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-60,60),
        })
        _delay(4, function() wPE.Rate = 0 end)
        _gc(wisp, 7)
    end
end

-- ─── Holographic Rings: sci-fi expanding rings around portal ────────────────
function VFX2.holographicRings(cf, col, pw)
    local numRings = 5
    for ri = 1, numRings do
        _delay(ri * 0.09, function()
            local r = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*0.6+ri*0.1, pw*0.6+ri*0.1, 0.02),
                Transparency= 0.25,
                CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,-0.06*(ri)),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
            rm.MeshId   = "rbxassetid://3270017987"
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(pw*0.5+ri*0.08, pw*0.5+ri*0.08, 0.06)
            rm.Parent   = r
            r.Parent    = _WS
            _tw(r, 0.45, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*1.8+ri*0.2, pw*1.8+ri*0.2, 0.02),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(r, 0.5)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Quantum Flicker: portal briefly flickers on placement ──────────────────
function VFX2.quantumFlicker(portalData, times)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    times = times or 5
    _spawn(function()
        for i = 1, times do
            portalData.part.Transparency = 0.8
            task.wait(0.04)
            portalData.part.Transparency = 0.0
            task.wait(0.05 + _rand()*0.04)
        end
    end)
end

-- ─── Ion Charge: crackling static pre-fire effect on gun barrel ──────────────
function VFX2.ionCharge(emitterPart, col)
    if not emitterPart then return end
    local numIons = 8
    for i = 1, numIons do
        _delay(i * 0.025, function()
            local p = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(0.05,0.05,0.05),
                Transparency= 0,
                CFrame      = emitterPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(
                    _rand()*0.4-0.2, _rand()*0.4-0.2, _rand()*0.2),
            })
            p.Parent = _WS
            _tw(p, 0.18, {
                CFrame      = emitterPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(
                    _cos(i)*0.6, _sin(i)*0.6, 0.3),
                Transparency= 1,
                Size        = Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01),
            })
            _gc(p, 0.22)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Energy Orb Projectile: glowing orb fired toward target ─────────────────
function VFX2.energyOrbProjectile(startPos, endPos, col, onArrive)
    local dist   = (endPos - startPos).Magnitude
    local dir    = (endPos - startPos).Unit
    local speed  = 80
    local dur    = dist / speed

    local orb = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = Vector3.new(0.35, 0.35, 0.35),
        Transparency= 0,
        CFrame      = CFrame.new(startPos),
    })
    local orbLight = Instance.new("PointLight")
    orbLight.Brightness = 6
    orbLight.Range      = 10
    orbLight.Color      = col
    orbLight.Parent     = orb

    local orbAtt = _att(orb)
    local orbPE  = _pe(orbAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col, 1, col),
        LightEmission= 1, LightInfluence=0,
        Size         = _ns(0, 0.25, 1, 0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(3,6),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(150,150),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(0.15, 0.3),
        Rate         = 40,
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0,360),
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-360,360),
    })
    orb.Parent = _WS

    -- Animate movement
    _tw(orb, dur, { CFrame = CFrame.new(endPos) }, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In)

    _delay(dur, function()
        orbPE.Rate = 0
        _tw(orb, 0.12, { Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01), Transparency=1 })
        _gc(orb, 0.2)
        if onArrive then onArrive() end
    end)

    return orb
end

-- ─── Muzzle Flash: gun barrel muzzle flash ──────────────────────────────────
function VFX2.muzzleFlash(emitterPart, col)
    if not emitterPart then return end
    local flashCF = emitterPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.7)

    -- Star flash
    for i = 1, 4 do
        local ang = (i/4)*TAU + math.pi/8
        local star = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = Color3.new(1,1,1),
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.5, 0.05, 0.05),
            Transparency= 0,
            CFrame      = flashCF * CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang),
        })
        star.Parent = _WS
        _tw(star, 0.12, { Size=Vector3.new(0.02,0.02,0.02), Transparency=1 })
        _gc(star, 0.15)
    end

    -- Core glow
    local glow = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = Vector3.new(0.35, 0.35, 0.35),
        Transparency= 0,
        CFrame      = flashCF,
    })
    glow.Parent = _WS
    _tw(glow, 0.12, { Size=Vector3.new(0.02,0.02,0.02), Transparency=1 })
    _gc(glow, 0.15)
end

-- ─── Impact Shockwave: ground-level ring on placement ───────────────────────
function VFX2.impactShockwave(cf, col, pw)
    local numRings = 3
    for ri = 1, numRings do
        _delay(ri * 0.05, function()
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*0.3, pw*0.3*0.15, 0.05),
                Transparency= 0.1,
                CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0, -0.1, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.pi/2,0,0),
            })
            ring.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.4, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*2.5+ri, pw*2.5*0.15+ri, 0.05),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(ring, 0.45)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Color Shift Ripple: color wave across portal face ──────────────────────
function VFX2.colorShiftRipple(portalData, col)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local cf = portalData.part.CFrame
    local pw = portalData.part.Size.X
    local ph = portalData.part.Size.Y
    for ri = 1, 6 do
        _delay(ri * 0.06, function()
            local r = ri / 6
            local ripple = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = Color3.fromHSV((ri/6)*0.2, 0.6, 1),
                Size        = Vector3.new(pw*r, ph*r, 0.02),
                Transparency= 0.5,
                CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.05),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(1,1,0.02)
            rm.Parent   = ripple
            ripple.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ripple, 0.3, { Transparency = 1 })
            _gc(ripple, 0.35)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Portal Breath Animation: slow expand/contract ───────────────────────────
-- (handled by main RenderStepped loop via extras.rings)

-- ─── Neon Grid Flicker: grid lines pulse on activate ────────────────────────
function VFX2.neonGridFlicker(extras, times)
    if not (extras and extras.gridParts) then return end
    _spawn(function()
        for tick = 1, (times or 3) do
            for _, gp in ipairs(extras.gridParts) do
                gp.Transparency = 0.4
            end
            task.wait(0.06)
            for _, gp in ipairs(extras.gridParts) do
                gp.Transparency = 0.92
            end
            task.wait(0.08)
        end
    end)
end

-- ─── Surface Burn Ring: temporary scorched ring on placement ─────────────────
function VFX2.surfaceBurnRing(cf, col, pw)
    local burn = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic,
        Color       = Color3.fromRGB(15,15,15),
        Size        = Vector3.new(pw*1.2, pw*1.2, 0.02),
        Transparency= 0.2,
        CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0, 0, 0.08),
    })
    local msh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
    msh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Cylinder
    msh.Scale    = Vector3.new(0.01, 1, 1)
    msh.Parent   = burn
    burn.Parent  = _WS
    _tw(burn, 8, { Transparency = 1 })
    _gc(burn, 8.5)

    -- Neon ring on top of burn
    local nRing = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = Vector3.new(pw*1.25, pw*1.25, 0.02),
        Transparency= 0.5,
        CFrame      = cf * CFrame.new(0,0,0.06),
    })
    local nMsh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
    nMsh.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
    nMsh.MeshId   = "rbxassetid://3270017987"
    nMsh.Scale    = Vector3.new(pw*1.0, pw*1.0, 0.06)
    nMsh.Parent   = nRing
    nRing.Parent  = _WS
    _tw(nRing, 4, { Transparency = 1 })
    _gc(nRing, 4.5)
end

-- ─── Teleport Speed Trail: motion blur trail on teleport ─────────────────────
function VFX2.teleportSpeedTrail(hrp, col, duration)
    if not hrp then return end
    duration = duration or 0.35
    local steps = 8
    for si = 1, steps do
        _delay(si * (duration/steps), function()
            if not hrp.Parent then return end
            local ghost = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = hrp.Size,
                Transparency= 0.25 + si*0.09,
                CFrame      = hrp.CFrame,
            })
            ghost.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ghost, 0.4, { Transparency = 1 })
            _gc(ghost, 0.45)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Portal Heartbeat: periodic light/size pulse ────────────────────────────
local function _startHeartbeat(colorKey)
    local conn
    local lastBeat = 0
    conn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
        if not (ex and ex.folder and ex.folder.Parent) then
            conn:Disconnect(); return
        end
        local t    = _UPG.frameT
        local tSec = t % UCFG.heartbeatPeriod
        -- Two-beat pattern
        local beat = (tSec < 0.12 or (tSec > 0.22 and tSec < 0.34))
        local bStr = beat and 1 or 0
        -- Apply to outer halo brightness
        if ex.outerHalo then
            ex.outerHalo.Transparency = 0.88 - bStr * 0.1
        end
        -- Apply to corner arc lights
        for _, cd in ipairs(ex.cornerArcs) do
            local light = cd.part:FindFirstChildOfClass("PointLight")
            if light then
                light.Brightness = 3 + bStr * 2
            end
        end
    end)
    return conn
end

-- ─── Ambient Dust: floating dust motes near portal ──────────────────────────
function VFX2.ambientDust(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local dustPart = _part({
        Transparency= 1,
        Size        = Vector3.new(pw*2, ph*2, pw*2),
        CFrame      = cf,
    })
    dustPart.Parent = _WS
    local dAtt  = _att(dustPart)
    local dustPE= _pe(dAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.fromRGB(200,220,255), 0.5, col, 1, Color3.fromRGB(200,200,200)),
        LightEmission= 0.1, LightInfluence = 0.9,
        Size         = _ns(0,0.06, 0.5,0.04, 1,0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.6),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(180,180),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(3,6),
        Rate         = 5,
        Transparency = _ns(0,0.5, 1,1),
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0,360),
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-30,30),
    })
    _delay(6, function() dustPE.Rate = 0 end)
    _gc(dustPart, 12)
end

-- ─── Portal Aura Pulse: expanding translucent sphere ────────────────────────
function VFX2.portalAuraPulse(cf, col)
    for i = 1, 4 do
        _delay(i * 0.08, function()
            local aura = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(0.5,0.5,0.5),
                Transparency= 0.4,
                CFrame      = cf,
            })
            local am = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            am.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            am.Parent   = aura
            aura.Parent = _WS

                Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
            _gc(aura, 0.65)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Exit Shockwave: burst on exit from portal ───────────────────────────────
function VFX2.exitShockwave(cf, col)
    VFX2.portalEnergyNova(cf, col, 4)
    VFX2.electricCrown(cf, col, 4, 6)
    _doFlash(col, 0.28, 0.3)
end

-- ─── Entry Vortex: spiral on entry into portal ───────────────────────────────
function VFX2.entryVortex(cf, col, pw, ph)
    VFX2.gravityVortexBurst(cf, col, pw, ph)
    _doChroma = _spawn(function()
        _doChromaticAberration(0.2)
    end)
end

-- ─── Floating Runes: mystical symbol particle trail ──────────────────────────
function VFX2.floatingRunes(cf, col, count)
    count = count or 10
    local runeChars = {"⊕","⊗","◈","⬡","⬢","⬣","◆","◇","⟁","⟂","⎔","⎗"}
    for i = 1, count do
        local ang = (i/count)*TAU + _rand()*0.5
        local r   = 1.5 + _rand() * 1.5
        local yOff= (_rand()-0.5)*2
        local rp  = Instance.new("Part")
        rp.Anchored   = true; rp.CanCollide = false; rp.Size = Vector3.new(0.8,0.8,0.1)
        rp.Transparency= 1; rp.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*r, yOff, _sin(ang)*0.5)
        rp.Parent = _WS
        local bb = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
        bb.Size  = UDim2.new(0,30,0,30)
        bb.AlwaysOnTop = false
        bb.Parent = rp
        local rl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        rl.Size              = UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
        rl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        rl.Text              = runeChars[_rand(1,#runeChars)]
        rl.TextColor3        = col
        rl.TextStrokeColor3  = Color3.new(1,1,1)
        rl.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
        rl.Font              = Enum.Font.Fantasy
        rl.TextSize          = 20
        rl.Parent            = bb
        _delay(0.3 + i*0.08, function()
            _tw(rl, 0.8 + _rand()*0.3, { TextTransparency=1, TextStrokeTransparency=1 })
        end)
        _gc(rp, 2.5)
    end
end

-- ─── Lightning Storm Inside Portal: random arcs inside portal face ───────────
function VFX2.interiorLightningStorm(cf, col, pw, ph, numArcs)
    numArcs = numArcs or 10
    for i = 1, numArcs do
        _delay(_rand() * 0.4, function()
            local startX = (_rand()-0.5) * pw * 0.9
            local startY = (_rand()-0.5) * ph * 0.9
            local endX   = (_rand()-0.5) * pw * 0.9
            local endY   = (_rand()-0.5) * ph * 0.9
            local p1 = _part({
                Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                CFrame= cf * CFrame.new(startX, startY, -0.05),
            })
            local p2 = _part({
                Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                CFrame= cf * CFrame.new(endX, endY, -0.05),
            })
            p1.Parent = _WS; p2.Parent = _WS
            local a1  = _att(p1); local a2 = _att(p2)
            local bolt = Instance.new("Beam")
            bolt.Attachment0    = a1
            bolt.Attachment1    = a2
            bolt.Color          = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col, 1, Color3.new(1,1,1))
            bolt.Width0         = 0.04 + _rand()*0.04
            bolt.Width1         = 0.04 + _rand()*0.04
            bolt.LightEmission  = 1
            bolt.Transparency   = NumberSequence.new(0.0)
            bolt.Segments       = 8
            bolt.FaceCamera     = true
            bolt.CurveSize0     = (_rand()-0.5)*1.2
            bolt.CurveSize1     = (_rand()-0.5)*1.2
            bolt.Parent         = p1
            _delay(0.06 + _rand()*0.08, function()
                _tw(p1, 0.12, { Transparency=1 })
                _tw(p2, 0.12, { Transparency=1 })
            end)
            _gc(p1, 0.25)
            _gc(p2, 0.25)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Rim Lightning Cascade: multiple sequential arcs around portal rim ────────
function VFX2.rimLightningCascade(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numArcs = 12
    for i = 1, numArcs do
        _delay(i * 0.04, function()
            local ang0 = (i-1)/numArcs * TAU
            local ang1 = i/numArcs * TAU
            local ex0  = Vector3.new(_cos(ang0)*pw*0.5, _sin(ang0)*ph*0.5, 0)
            local ex1  = Vector3.new(_cos(ang1)*pw*0.5, _sin(ang1)*ph*0.5, 0)
            local p1 = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(ex0) })
            local p2 = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(ex1) })
            p1.Parent=_WS; p2.Parent=_WS
            local a1=_att(p1); local a2=_att(p2)
            local bolt=Instance.new("Beam")
            bolt.Attachment0=a1; bolt.Attachment1=a2
            bolt.Color=_cs(0,col,0.5,Color3.new(1,1,1),1,col)
            bolt.Width0=0.06; bolt.Width1=0.06
            bolt.LightEmission=1; bolt.Segments=4
            bolt.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0)
            bolt.Parent=p1
            _delay(0.12, function()
                _tw(p1,0.1,{Transparency=1}); _tw(p2,0.1,{Transparency=1})
            end)
            _gc(p1, 0.25); _gc(p2, 0.25)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── Teleport Warp Bubble: sphere that expands then pops on teleport ─────────
function VFX2.teleportWarpBubble(hrp, col)
    if not hrp then return end
    local bubble = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.ForceField,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = Vector3.new(4,4,4),
        Transparency= 0.5,
        CFrame      = hrp.CFrame,
    })
    local bm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
    bm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere; bm.Parent = bubble
    bubble.Parent = _WS
    _tw(bubble, 0.2, { Size=Vector3.new(8,8,8), Transparency=0.85 })
    _delay(0.22, function()
        _tw(bubble, 0.12, { Size=Vector3.new(0.5,0.5,0.5), Transparency=1 })
        _gc(bubble, 0.15)
    end)
end

-- ─── Neon Tracer: thin neon line from gun to portal site ────────────────────
function VFX2.neonTracer(startPos, endPos, col)
    local mid     = (startPos + endPos) / 2
    local dist    = (endPos - startPos).Magnitude
    local dir     = (endPos - startPos).Unit
    local tracer  = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = col,
        Size        = Vector3.new(0.04, 0.04, dist),
        Transparency= 0.15,
        CFrame      = CFrame.new(mid, endPos),
    })
    tracer.Parent = _WS
    _tw(tracer, 0.25, { Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,dist) })
    _gc(tracer, 0.30)
end

-- ─── Portal Proximity Pull Particles: particles drift toward portal ──────────
function VFX2.proximityPullParticles(cf, col, radius)
    local pp = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(radius*2,radius*2,radius*2), CFrame=cf })
    pp.Parent = _WS
    local pAtt = _att(pp)
    local pPE  = _pe(pAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.3, col, 1, col),
        LightEmission= 0.5, LightInfluence=0.5,
        Size         = _ns(0,0.18, 0.7,0.10, 1,0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(2, 5),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(360,360),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(0.5, 1.2),
        Rate         = 22,
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-200,200),
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0,360),
    })
    _delay(3, function() pPE.Rate = 0 end)
    _gc(pp, 6)
end

-- ─── Teleport screen-space combo ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX2.fullTeleportFX(hrp, entryColor, exitColor)
    -- Screen effects
    _doFlash(entryColor, 0.6, 0.35)
    _doChromaticAberration(0.22)
    _doSpeedLines(entryColor, 0.16)
    _vignetteFlash(0.7, 0.5)
    -- World effects
    if hrp then
        VFX2.teleportEchoGhost(hrp, entryColor)
        VFX2.teleportSpeedTrail(hrp, exitColor, 0.4)
        VFX2.teleportWarpBubble(hrp, exitColor)
    end
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  SECTION 5 — AUDIO SYSTEM v2
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local AUDIO2 = {}

-- Sound ID library (all free Roblox audio assets)
local SFX = {
    portalOpenBlue   = "rbxassetid://171399373",
    portalOpenOrange = "rbxassetid://171399373",
    portalClose      = "rbxassetid://182981587",
    portalFireBlue   = "rbxassetid://182981554",
    portalFireOrange = "rbxassetid://182981587",
    teleportEnter    = "rbxassetid://232806289",
    teleportExit     = "rbxassetid://232806289",
    ambientHum       = "rbxassetid://1843645492",
    electricArc      = "rbxassetid://240764183",
    whoosh           = "rbxassetid://1369158409",
    deepBoom         = "rbxassetid://131961136",
    shimmer          = "rbxassetid://180200963",
    heartbeat        = "rbxassetid://303570791",
    energyBuild      = "rbxassetid://169445572",
    cosmicDrone      = "rbxassetid://282666306",
    staticCrackle    = "rbxassetid://240764183",
    portalTear       = "rbxassetid://130776445",
    implosion        = "rbxassetid://157878578",
}

local function _playAt(id, pos, vol, pitch, rollOff)
    local p = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=CFrame.new(pos or Vector3.new(0,0,0)) })
    p.Parent = _WS
    local s  = Instance.new("Sound")
    s.SoundId           = id
    s.Volume            = vol or 0.7
    s.PlaybackSpeed     = pitch or 1
    s.RollOffMaxDistance= rollOff or 60
    s.RollOffMode       = Enum.RollOffMode.Linear
    s.Parent            = p
    s:Play()
    s.Ended:Connect(function() pcall(function() p:Destroy() end) end)
    _delay(8, function() pcall(function() p:Destroy() end) end)
    return s
end

local function _playGlobal(id, vol, pitch)
    local s = Instance.new("Sound")
    s.SoundId      = id
    s.Volume       = vol or 0.7
    s.PlaybackSpeed= pitch or 1
    s.Parent       = _SS
    s:Play()
    s.Ended:Connect(function() pcall(function() s:Destroy() end) end)
    return s
end

function AUDIO2.onPortalFire(color, pos)
    if not UCFG.audioPositional then return end
    local id    = color == "blue" and SFX.portalFireBlue or SFX.portalFireOrange
    local pitch = color == "blue" and 1.0 or 0.85
    _playAt(id, pos, 0.8, pitch)
    _playAt(SFX.electricArc, pos, 0.4, 1.2 + _rand()*0.3)
end

function AUDIO2.onPortalOpen(color, pos)
    local id    = color == "blue" and SFX.portalOpenBlue or SFX.portalOpenOrange
    local pitch = color == "blue" and 1.05 or 0.88
    _playAt(id, pos, 0.85, pitch)
    _delay(0.1, function() _playAt(SFX.whoosh, pos, 0.5, 0.9) end)
    _delay(0.25, function() _playAt(SFX.shimmer, pos, 0.4, 1.1) end)
end

function AUDIO2.onPortalClose(color, pos)
    _playAt(SFX.portalClose, pos, 0.7, 1.0)
    _delay(0.08, function() _playAt(SFX.implosion, pos, 0.55, 1.4) end)
end

function AUDIO2.onTeleportEnter(pos)
    _playAt(SFX.teleportEnter, pos, 0.9, 1.0)
    _playAt(SFX.whoosh, pos, 0.6, 1.3)
    _playGlobal(SFX.staticCrackle, 0.4, 1.5)
end

function AUDIO2.onTeleportExit(pos)
    _playAt(SFX.teleportExit, pos, 0.85, 0.85)
    _delay(0.05, function() _playGlobal(SFX.shimmer, 0.5, 0.95) end)
end

function AUDIO2.onElectricArc(pos)
    _playAt(SFX.electricArc, pos, 0.35, 0.9 + _rand()*0.4)
end

-- Proximity hum management
local _proxHum = nil

_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    if not UCFG.audioProximity then return end
    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end

    local nearestDist = 999
    for _, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
            local d = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
            if d < nearestDist then nearestDist = d end
        end
    end

    if nearestDist < 35 then
        if not _proxHum then
            local s     = Instance.new("Sound")
            s.SoundId   = SFX.ambientHum
            s.Volume    = 0
            s.Looped    = true
            s.PlaybackSpeed = 1.05
            s.Parent    = _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or _SS
            s:Play()
            _proxHum    = s
        end
        local t    = _clamp(1 - nearestDist/35, 0, 1)
        _proxHum.Volume       = _lerp(_proxHum.Volume, UCFG.ambientHumVol * t * 0.8, dt * 3)
        _proxHum.PlaybackSpeed= 1.0 + t * 0.15
    else
        if _proxHum then
            _proxHum.Volume = _lerp(_proxHum.Volume, 0, dt * 4)
            if _proxHum.Volume < 0.005 then
                pcall(function() _proxHum:Stop(); _proxHum:Destroy() end)
                _proxHum = nil
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  SECTION 6 — PORTAL INTERACTION PHYSICS & PORTAL TIMER
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── Portal Stability Meter ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _portalStability = { blue = 1, orange = 1 }
local _portalAge       = { blue = 0, orange = 0 }
local PORTAL_MAX_AGE   = 300  -- seconds before portal weakens (0 = no limit)

_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if ex then
            _portalAge[ck] = (_portalAge[ck] or 0) + dt
            if PORTAL_MAX_AGE > 0 then
                local age = _portalAge[ck]
                local stab= _clamp(1 - (age / PORTAL_MAX_AGE), 0.2, 1)
                _portalStability[ck] = stab
                -- Visual instability: rings flicker as stability drops
                if stab < 0.5 then
                    local flickerChance = (0.5 - stab) * 0.4
                    if _rand() < flickerChance * dt * 10 then
                        for _, rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
                            rd.part.Transparency = _rand() * 0.6
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Gravity Pull: objects near portal experience mild visual drift ───────────
-- (particles handled by extras.gravityPE; here we do a HRP-awareness check)
_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    if not UCFG.showGravityWell then return end
    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end

    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if not (ex and ex.beamAnchor) then continue end
        local portalPos = ex.beamAnchor.Position
        local dist      = (portalPos - hrp.Position).Magnitude
        -- Only visual feedback, no actual force
        if dist < UCFG.gravityWellRadius and dist > 0.5 then
            -- Update gravity PE facing
            if ex.gravityPart then
                local toPortal = (portalPos - hrp.Position).Unit
                ex.gravityPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position + toPortal * 3, portalPos)
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Portal event hooks: inject into original script's placePortal & closePortals
-- These use spawn-safe pcall wrapping so they never break the original logic.

-- We wrap the original's closing logic by listening to portal table changes.
local _lastPortalState = { blue = false, orange = false }

_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    -- Detect portal opens: portals table from original scope
    for _, ck in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
        local pData = pcall and (function()
            local ok, pd = pcall(function() return portals and portals[ck] end)
            return ok and pd or nil
        end)() or nil

        if pData ~= nil then
            local nowOpen = (pData ~= nil) and (pData ~= false)
            local wasOpen = _lastPortalState[ck]

            if nowOpen and not wasOpen then
                -- Portal just opened
                _lastPortalState[ck] = true
                _portalAge[ck] = 0
                _spawn(function()
                    local ok2, err = pcall(function()
                        local col  = ck=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                                                 or  (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
                        local cf2  = pData.part and pData.part.CFrame
                        local pw2  = (CFG and CFG.portalWidth)  or 4
                        local ph2  = (CFG and CFG.portalHeight) or 6
                        if cf2 then
                            pData.cf = cf2
                            _onPortalPlaced(ck, pData, CFG or { blueColor=col, orangeColor=col, portalWidth=pw2, portalHeight=ph2 })
                            -- Fire VFX
                            VFX2.plasmaFlood(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            VFX2.dimensionalTear(cf2, col)
                            VFX2.portalEnergyNova(cf2, col, pw2)
                            VFX2.holographicRings(cf2, col, pw2)
                            VFX2.electricCrown(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            VFX2.smokeWisps(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            VFX2.surfaceBurnRing(cf2, col, pw2)
                            VFX2.interiorLightningStorm(cf2, col, pw2, ph2, 14)
                            VFX2.rimLightningCascade(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            VFX2.cosmicDust(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            VFX2.portalAuraPulse(cf2, col)
                            VFX2.floatingRunes(cf2, col, 8)
                            VFX2.impactShockwave(cf2, col, pw2)
                            VFX2.ambientDust(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
                            _startHeartbeat(ck)
                            -- Notification
                            local icon = ck=="blue" and "🔵" or "🟠"
                            local name = ck=="blue" and "Blue" or "Orange"
                            _showNotif(icon, name .. " Portal Opened",
                                "Portal placed · ".. math.floor(pw2).."×"..math.floor(ph2) .." studs",
                                ck=="blue" and Color3.fromRGB(0,60,140) or Color3.fromRGB(120,50,0))
                            -- Audio
                            AUDIO2.onPortalOpen(ck, cf2.Position)
                        end
                    end)
                end)

            elseif not nowOpen and wasOpen then
                -- Portal just closed
                _lastPortalState[ck] = false
                _spawn(function()
                    pcall(function()
                        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[ck]
                        if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
                            local closePos = ex.beamAnchor.Position
                            AUDIO2.onPortalClose(ck, closePos)
                        end
                        _onPortalClosed(ck)
                        local icon = ck=="blue" and "🔵" or "🟠"
                        local name = ck=="blue" and "Blue" or "Orange"
                        _showNotif(icon, name .. " Portal Closed", "Portal removed", Color3.fromRGB(40,40,60))
                    end)
                end)
            end
        end
    end
end)

        local sp = settingsSG:FindFirstChild("PortalSettings", true)

            { key="showEdgeTendrils", label="Edge Tendrils" },
            { key="showNeonGrid",     label="Neon Grid Overlay" },
            { key="showDepthSpiral",  label="Depth Spiral" },
            { key="showCornerArcs",   label="Corner Lightning Nodes" },
            { key="showGravityWell",  label="Gravity Well Effect" },
            { key="showCrossBeam",    label="Cross-Portal Beam" },
            { key="showBreathing",    label="Portal Breathing" },
            { key="ssFX_chromatic",   label="Chromatic Aberration" },
            { key="ssFX_vignette",    label="Vignette" },
            { key="ssFX_scanlines",   label="Scanlines" },
            { key="ssFX_colorLeak",   label="Color Leak" },
            { key="ssFX_speedLines",  label="Speed Lines (Teleport)" },

        for _, row in ipairs(toggleRows) do

            rowFrame.BackgroundColor3  = Color3.fromRGB(18,18,36)

            rowFrame.ZIndex            = 32
            rowFrame.Parent            = fxPage
            _corner(rowFrame, UDim.new(0,8))

            local lbl = _label(rowFrame, row.label, 12, Color3.fromRGB(200,210,235),
                Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 33)
            lbl.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-80,1,0)
            lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,12,0,0)

            local val = UCFG[row.key]
            local toggleF = Instance.new("TextButton")
            toggleF.Size             = UDim2.new(0,50,0,22)
            toggleF.Position         = UDim2.new(1,-60,0.5,-11)

    for i, k in ipairs(lineKeys) do

    _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)

        dbgLines["BluePortal"].Text   = "Blue: "   .. ((_UPG.portalExtras.blue   and "ACTIVE") or "—")
        dbgLines["OrangePortal"].Text = "Orange: " .. ((_UPG.portalExtras.orange and "ACTIVE") or "—")
        dbgLines["Stability"].Text    = "Stab B:"  .. math.floor((_portalStability.blue or 1)*100)
            .. "% O:" .. math.floor((_portalStability.orange or 1)*100) .. "%"
        local ne = 0
        for _ in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do ne=ne+1 end
        dbgLines["Extras"].Text  = "Extras: " .. ne
        dbgLines["SFX"].Text     = "ProxHum: " .. (_proxHum and "ON" or "OFF")
        dbgLines["Beams"].Text   = "CrossBeam: " .. (_crossBeamInst and "ON" or "OFF")
        dbgLines["Heartbeat"].Text= "Age B:" .. math.floor(_portalAge.blue or 0)
            .. "s O:" .. math.floor(_portalAge.orange or 0) .. "s"
    end)
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  SECTION 9 — COOLDOWN ARC & CROSSHAIR UPDATE
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    local t = _UPG.frameT

    -- Cooldown arc — reads original's lastFire and CFG.cooldown if available
    if _gv3.arcSegs then
        local cooldownPct = 1.0
        pcall(function()
            if lastFire then
                local elapsed = tick() - lastFire
                local cd      = CFG and CFG.cooldown or 0.8
                cooldownPct   = _clamp(elapsed / cd, 0, 1)
            end
        end)
        local numSegs = _gv3.arcNumSegs or 24
        local col2    = cooldownPct >= 1
            and Color3.fromRGB(0,200,80)
            or  Color3.fromRGB(0, 130, 255)
        for i, seg in ipairs(_gv3.arcSegs) do
            local thresh = i / numSegs
            seg.BackgroundColor3       = col2
            seg.BackgroundTransparency = thresh <= cooldownPct and 0.35 or 0.88
        end
        if _gv3.arcLabel then
            _gv3.arcLabel.Text = cooldownPct >= 1 and "READY" or
                string.format("%.0f%%", cooldownPct*100)
        end
    end

    -- Crosshair color sync with selected portal
    pcall(function()
        if selColor then
            local col3 = selColor == "blue"
                and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                or  (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
            _gv3.xhColor = col3
            if _gv3.xhDot then
                _gv3.xhDot.BackgroundColor3 = col3
            end
            if _gv3.xhHitRing then
                local stroke2 = _gv3.xhHitRing:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
                if stroke2 then stroke2.Color = col3 end
            end
        end
    end)
end)

--  PORTAL GUN v3  ·  ULTRA UPGRADE PATCH  ·  PART II
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── VFX3 namespace (additional effects) ─────────────────────────────────────
local VFX3 = {}



-- ─── portalSolarFlare: Bright streaks that shoot outward like a solar flare ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalSolarFlare(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numFlares = 12
    for i = 1, numFlares do
        local ang  = (i/numFlares)*TAU + _rand()*0.3
        local len  = pw * (0.8 + _rand() * 1.4)
        local w    = 0.06 + _rand() * 0.08
        _delay(i*0.03, function()
            local p = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(len, w, w), Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=cf * CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*pw*0.5, _sin(ang)*ph*0.5, 0)
                    * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, ang + math.pi/2) })
            p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p, 0.4, { Size=Vector3.new(0.02,0.02,0.02),
                Transparency=1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*(pw*0.5+len), _sin(ang)*(ph*0.5+len),0)
                    *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2) })
            _gc(p, 0.45)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── portalEnergyTendrilWave: Wave of energy tendrils that ripple outward ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalEnergyTendrilWave(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local arms = 16
    for i = 1, arms do
        local baseAng = (i/arms)*TAU
        for seg = 1, 7 do
            local st  = seg/7
            local ang  = baseAng + _sin(st*math.pi)*0.4
            local r    = pw*(0.5 + st*0.8)
            local p    = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(0.06*(1-st*0.7), 0.06*(1-st*0.7), 0.06),
                Transparency=0.15 + st*0.7,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*r, _sin(ang)*r*(ph/pw), -0.05) })
            p.Parent=_WS
            _delay(0.05+i*0.02+seg*0.01, function()
                _tw(p, 0.3, { Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01) })
            end)
            _gc(p, 0.55)
        end
    end
end


-- ─── portalPlasmaArc: Large arcing plasma beam between two points near the portal ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalPlasmaArc(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numArcs = 6
    for ai = 1, numArcs do
        _delay(ai*0.05, function()
            local ang0 = _rand()*TAU
            local ang1 = ang0 + math.pi + (_rand()-0.5)*1.2
            local r0   = pw*(0.3 + _rand()*0.25)
            local r1   = pw*(0.3 + _rand()*0.25)
            local p0   = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang0)*r0, _sin(ang0)*r0*(ph/pw), -0.08) })
            local p1   = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang1)*r1, _sin(ang1)*r1*(ph/pw), -0.08) })
            p0.Parent=_WS; p1.Parent=_WS
            local a0, a1 = _att(p0), _att(p1)
            local b = Instance.new("Beam")
            b.Attachment0=a0; b.Attachment1=a1
            b.Color=_cs(0,Color3.new(1,1,1),0.3,col,0.7,col,1,Color3.new(1,1,1))
            b.Width0=0.08+_rand()*0.06; b.Width1=0.04+_rand()*0.04
            b.LightEmission=1; b.Segments=12
            b.CurveSize0=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.6; b.CurveSize1=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.6
            b.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0); b.FaceCamera=false; b.Parent=p0
            _delay(0.18+_rand()*0.12, function()
                _tw(p0,0.1,{Transparency=1}); _tw(p1,0.1,{Transparency=1})
            end)
            _gc(p0,0.35); _gc(p1,0.35)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── portalRippleWave: Concentric ripple waves spreading out from portal center ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalRippleWave(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numRipples = 8
    for ri = 1, numRipples do
        _delay(ri*0.07, function()
            local t = ri/numRipples
            local rp = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.2*t, ph*0.2*t, 0.02),
                Transparency=0.2, CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.04) })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere; rm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.02); rm.Parent=rp
            rp.Parent=_WS
            _tw(rp, 0.45+t*0.15, { Size=Vector3.new(pw*1.6, ph*1.6, 0.02), Transparency=1 })
            _gc(rp, 0.65)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── portalStarBurst: Multi-pointed starburst explosion of neon rays ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalStarBurst(cf, col, pw)
    local points = 8
    for pi2 = 1, points do
        for layer = 1, 2 do
            local ang = (pi2/points)*TAU + (layer-1)*math.pi/points
            local len = pw * (0.6 + layer*0.3 + _rand()*0.3)
            local p   = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(len, 0.06-layer*0.01, 0.06-layer*0.01),
                Transparency=0, CFrame=cf*CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang) })
            p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p, 0.3+layer*0.05, { Size=Vector3.new(0.02,0.02,0.02), Transparency=1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*len,_sin(ang)*len,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang) })
            _gc(p, 0.4)
        end
    end
end


-- ─── portalVoidRift: Dark rift that opens in space, opposite of normal portal colors ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalVoidRift(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local darkCol = Color3.new(1-col.R*0.7, 1-col.G*0.7, 1-col.B*0.7)
    local numParts = 18
    for i = 1, numParts do
        local ang = (i/numParts)*TAU
        local r   = pw*0.5
        local p   = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=darkCol,
            Size=Vector3.new(0.08, ph*0.15, 0.04),
            Transparency=0.2,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*r, _sin(ang)*r*(ph/pw), -0.1)
                *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2) })
        p.Parent=_WS
        _tw(p, 0.4, { Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01), Transparency=1,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*(r+pw*0.4), _sin(ang)*(r+ph*0.4)*(ph/pw), -0.1)
                *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2) })
        _gc(p, 0.5)
    end
end


-- ─── portalLightPillar: Vertical column of light rising from portal base ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalLightPillar(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local pillar = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
        Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.3, 0.1, pw*0.3), Transparency=0.3,
        CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0, -ph*0.5, 0) })
    local pm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); pm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Cylinder
    pm.Scale=Vector3.new(0.01,1,1); pm.Parent=pillar; pillar.Parent=_WS
    _tw(pillar, 0.4, { Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.3, ph*3, pw*0.3), Transparency=0.85 })
    _tw(pillar, 1.5, { Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.1, ph*3, pw*0.1), Transparency=1 })
    _gc(pillar, 2)
    -- Particles rising through pillar
    local pAtt = _att(pillar)
    local pPE  = _pe(pAtt, { Color=_cs(0,col,0.5,Color3.new(1,1,1),1,col),
        LightEmission=0.8, Size=_ns(0,0.12,0.5,0.08,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(3,6), SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(8,8),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.8,1.8), Rate=20,
        Direction=Vector3.new(0,1,0) })
    _delay(2, function() pPE.Rate=0 end); _gc(pillar, 4)
end


-- ─── portalFractureLines: Crack-like fracture lines radiating from portal edge ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalFractureLines(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numLines = 14
    local brightCol = Color3.new(
        math.min(1,col.R+0.4), math.min(1,col.G+0.4), math.min(1,col.B+0.4))
    for i = 1, numLines do
        local ang    = (i/numLines)*TAU + (_rand()-0.5)*0.4
        local segs   = 3 + _rand(0,2)
        local prevX  = _cos(ang)*pw*0.5
        local prevY  = _sin(ang)*ph*0.5
        for s = 1, segs do
            local branchAng = ang + (_rand()-0.5)*0.7
            local segLen    = 0.4 + _rand()*0.8
            local endX = prevX + _cos(branchAng)*segLen
            local endY = prevY + _sin(branchAng)*segLen
            local midX = (prevX+endX)/2; local midY=(prevY+endY)/2
            local dist = _sqrt((endX-prevX)^2+(endY-prevY)^2)
            local ang2 = math.atan2(endY-prevY, endX-prevX)
            local seg = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=brightCol,
                Size=Vector3.new(dist, 0.03, 0.03), Transparency=0.05,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(midX,midY,-0.09)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang2) })
            seg.Parent=_WS
            _tw(seg, 0.5+s*0.08, { Transparency=1 })
            _gc(seg, 0.65)
            prevX=endX; prevY=endY
        end
    end
end


-- ─── portalQuantumTunnel: Visual tunnel effect suggesting depth beyond portal ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalQuantumTunnel(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numRings = 8
    local tunnelDepth = pw * 3
    for ri = 1, numRings do
        local t  = ri/numRings
        local rz = -t * tunnelDepth * 0.15
        local rs = 1 - t*0.65
        local ring = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(pw*rs, ph*rs, 0.03), Transparency=0.2+t*0.5,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,rz) })
        local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
        rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh; rm.MeshId="rbxassetid://3270017987"
        rm.Scale=Vector3.new(pw*rs*0.85, ph*rs*0.85, 0.08); rm.Parent=ring
        ring.Parent=_WS
        _delay(0.1, function()
            _tw(ring, 0.5+ri*0.06, { Transparency=0.7+t*0.3 })
        end)
        _delay(3.5, function() _tw(ring,0.5,{Transparency=1}) end)
        _gc(ring, 4.5)
    end
end


-- ─── portalAngelHalo: Glowing halo ring above the portal ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function VFX3.portalAngelHalo(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local halo = _part({ Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
        Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.9, pw*0.9, 0.04), Transparency=0.2,
        CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0, ph*0.6+0.5, 0)*CFrame.Angles(math.pi/12,0,0) })
    local hm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); hm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
    hm.MeshId="rbxassetid://3270017987"; hm.Scale=Vector3.new(pw*0.75,pw*0.75,0.12); hm.Parent=halo
    halo.Parent=_WS
    local conn; local ang=0
    conn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not (halo and halo.Parent) then conn:Disconnect(); return end
        ang=ang+dt*1.2; halo.CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,ph*0.6+0.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.pi/12,ang,0)
        halo.Transparency=0.2+_sin(ang*2)*0.1
    end)
    _delay(4, function()
        if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
        _tw(halo,0.5,{Transparency=1}); _gc(halo,0.6)
    end)
end



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PARTICLE PRESET LIBRARY  — 60 pre-built emitter configurations
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local ParticlePresets = {}

-- ─── Builder helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function _preset(name, def)
    ParticlePresets[name] = def
end

local function applyPreset(presetName, parent, col)
    local def = ParticlePresets[presetName]
    if not def then return nil end
    local att = _att(parent)
    local pe  = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
    pe.Color        = def.color or (col and ColorSequence.new(col)) or ColorSequence.new(Color3.new(1,1,1))
    pe.LightEmission= def.lightEmission or 0
    pe.LightInfluence=def.lightInfluence or 1
    pe.Size         = def.size         or _ns(0,0.1,1,0)
    pe.Speed        = def.speed        or NumberRange.new(2,4)
    pe.SpreadAngle  = def.spread       or Vector2.new(90,90)
    pe.Lifetime     = def.lifetime     or NumberRange.new(1,2)
    pe.Rate         = def.rate         or 10
    pe.Rotation     = def.rotation     or NumberRange.new(0,360)
    pe.RotSpeed     = def.rotSpeed     or NumberRange.new(-90,90)
    pe.Transparency = def.transparency or _ns(0,0,1,1)
    if def.texture then pe.Texture=def.texture end
    if def.accelerate then pe.Acceleration=def.accelerate end
    if def.drag then pe.Drag=def.drag end
    pe.Parent = att
    return pe
end

ParticlePresets.register = applyPreset

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL ART PRESETS  — 20 curated color schemes for blue/orange portals
--  Apply with: PortalArt.apply("SchemeName")
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local PortalArt = {}
local _artSchemes = {}

local function _defArt(name, bR,bG,bB, oR,oG,oB, desc)
    _artSchemes[name] = {
        blue   = Color3.fromRGB(bR, bG, bB),
        orange = Color3.fromRGB(oR, oG, oB),
        desc   = desc,
    }
end

_defArt("Classic", 0,130,255, 255,120,0, "Original Portal aesthetic")
_defArt("Inferno", 255,50,0, 255,200,0, "Volcanic fire theme")
_defArt("Arctic", 160,230,255, 200,240,255, "Ice and snow — both cool")
_defArt("Neon", 0,255,128, 255,0,255, "Cyberpunk neon vibes")
_defArt("Void", 80,0,160, 20,0,80, "Dark space — ominous")
_defArt("Forest", 40,180,60, 180,120,20, "Nature earth tones")
_defArt("Sunset", 255,100,0, 255,200,100, "Golden hour warm")
_defArt("Ocean", 0,100,200, 0,200,200, "Deep sea blue-teal")
_defArt("Galactic", 100,0,255, 255,100,200, "Space nebula purple-pink")
_defArt("Toxic", 100,255,0, 200,255,50, "Radioactive neon green")
_defArt("Crimson", 200,0,50, 255,80,80, "Blood crimson red")
_defArt("Hologram", 0,200,255, 200,0,255, "Sci-fi holographic")
_defArt("Gold", 255,200,0, 200,140,0, "Metallic warm gold")
_defArt("Platinum", 200,220,240, 160,180,200, "Silver cool platinum")
_defArt("Sakura", 255,150,180, 255,100,140, "Cherry blossom pink")
_defArt("Midnight", 20,20,80, 60,20,100, "Deep midnight dark")
_defArt("Biohazard", 160,255,80, 80,200,0, "Toxic biohazard green")
_defArt("Solar", 255,220,50, 255,150,0, "Solar energy warm")
_defArt("Candy", 255,100,200, 100,200,255, "Sweet candy colors")
_defArt("Thunder", 255,255,100, 200,200,50, "Lightning storm yellow")

function PortalArt.apply(schemeName)
    local scheme = _artSchemes[schemeName]
    if not scheme then
        warn("[PortalArt] Unknown scheme: " .. tostring(schemeName))
        return false
    end
    pcall(function()
        if CFG then
            CFG.blueColor   = scheme.blue
            CFG.orangeColor = scheme.orange
            if type(refreshPortalVisuals) == "function" then
                refreshPortalVisuals()
            end
        end
    end)
    _showNotif("🎨", "Art Scheme: " .. schemeName, scheme.desc,
        Color3.fromRGB(40,20,80), 3)
    return true
end

function PortalArt.getSchemes()
    local list = {}
    for name, sch in pairs(_artSchemes) do
        table.insert(list, { name=name, blue=sch.blue, orange=sch.orange, desc=sch.desc })
    end
    table.sort(list, function(a,b) return a.name < b.name end)
    return list
end

function PortalArt.random()
    local schemes = PortalArt.getSchemes()
    if #schemes == 0 then return end
    local picked = schemes[_rand(1, #schemes)]
    PortalArt.apply(picked.name)
end

        local galPanel = _frame(galSG, {
            Name            = "ArtGalleryPanel",

        })
        _corner(galPanel, UDim.new(0,14))
        _stroke(galPanel, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(100,40,180), 0.4)

        local galTitle = _label(galPanel, "🎨  Portal Art Gallery", 14,

        local schemeScroll = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        schemeScroll.Size                = UDim2.new(1,-14,1,-60)

        schemeScroll.BackgroundTransparency=1; schemeScroll.BorderSizePixel=0
        schemeScroll.ScrollBarThickness  = 4
        schemeScroll.ScrollBarImageColor3= Color3.fromRGB(100,40,180)
        schemeScroll.CanvasSize          = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
        schemeScroll.ZIndex              = 36; schemeScroll.Parent = galPanel

        schemeGrid.CellPadding = UDim2.new(0,6,0,6)

            local card = _frame(schemeScroll, {
