        randBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            PortalArt.random()
        end)

        -- Toggle gallery
        galBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            galPanel.Visible = not galPanel.Visible
        end)
    end)
end)



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL GUN ANIMATION STATE MACHINE v2
--  States: Idle, Aiming, Firing, Reloading, Holstering, Drawing, Teleporting
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local AnimSM = {}
AnimSM.currentState  = "Idle"
AnimSM.previousState = "Idle"
AnimSM.stateTime     = 0
AnimSM.transitions   = {}
AnimSM.onEnter       = {}
AnimSM.onExit        = {}
AnimSM.onUpdate      = {}

-- ─── State definitions ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

AnimSM.states = {
    "Idle",
    "Aiming",
    "Firing",
    "Reloading",
    "Holstering",
    "Drawing",
    "Teleporting",
    "PortalOpen",
    "PortalClose",
    "Scanning",
}

-- ─── Transition table ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
AnimSM.transitions = {
    Idle         = { Aiming=true, Holstering=true, Drawing=true },
    Aiming       = { Idle=true, Firing=true, Reloading=true },
    Firing       = { Aiming=true, Idle=true, PortalOpen=true },
    Reloading    = { Aiming=true, Idle=true },
    Holstering   = { Idle=true },
    Drawing      = { Idle=true, Aiming=true },
    Teleporting  = { Idle=true },
    PortalOpen   = { Aiming=true, Idle=true },
    PortalClose  = { Idle=true },
    Scanning     = { Aiming=true, Idle=true },
}

-- ─── State machine step ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function AnimSM.transition(newState)
    local current = AnimSM.currentState
    if current == newState then return false end
    local allowed = AnimSM.transitions[current]
    if not (allowed and allowed[newState]) then return false end

    if AnimSM.onExit[current] then
        pcall(AnimSM.onExit[current])
    end

    AnimSM.previousState = current
    AnimSM.currentState  = newState
    AnimSM.stateTime     = 0

    if AnimSM.onEnter[newState] then
        pcall(AnimSM.onEnter[newState])
    end

    return true
end

_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    AnimSM.stateTime = AnimSM.stateTime + dt
    local fn = AnimSM.onUpdate[AnimSM.currentState]
    if fn then pcall(fn, dt, AnimSM.stateTime) end
end)

-- ─── State behaviors ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

-- IDLE: gentle weapon sway
AnimSM.onEnter["Idle"] = function()
    -- nothing special on enter idle
end
AnimSM.onUpdate["Idle"] = function(dt, t)
    -- Idle sway handled by existing arm code
end

-- FIRING: trigger recoil, flash, and VFX chain
AnimSM.onEnter["Firing"] = function()
    local emPart = nil
    pcall(function()
        local char = _LP.Character
        if char then
            local tool = char:FindFirstChild("Mel's Portal Gun")
            if tool then emPart = tool:FindFirstChild("Emitter", true) end
        end
    end)
    if emPart then
        local col = pcall and (function()
            local ok, c = pcall(function()
                return selColor=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                    or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
            end)
            return ok and c or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
        end)() or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
        VFX2.muzzleFlash(emPart, col)
        VFX2.ionCharge(emPart, col)
    end
    _delay(0.12, function()
        pcall(function() AnimSM.transition("Aiming") end)
    end)
end

-- TELEPORTING: full screen FX
AnimSM.onEnter["Teleporting"] = function()
    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    local col  = Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    pcall(function()
        col = selColor=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor) or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor) or col
    end)
    VFX2.fullTeleportFX(hrp, col, col)
    _delay(0.4, function()
        pcall(function() AnimSM.transition("Idle") end)
    end)
end

-- PORTAL_OPEN: plays on new portal creation
AnimSM.onEnter["PortalOpen"] = function()
    _delay(0.35, function()
        pcall(function() AnimSM.transition("Aiming") end)
    end)
end

-- SCANNING: crosshair expands while scanning for surface
AnimSM.onEnter["Scanning"] = function()
    if _gv3.xhHitRing then
        _tw(_gv3.xhHitRing, 0.2, { Size=UDim2.new(0,50,0,50), Position=UDim2.new(0.5,-25,0.5,-25) })
    end
end
AnimSM.onExit["Scanning"] = function()
    if _gv3.xhHitRing then
        _tw(_gv3.xhHitRing, 0.2, { Size=UDim2.new(0,28,0,28), Position=UDim2.new(0.5,-14,0.5,-14) })
    end
end

-- ─── Public API ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function AnimSM.fire()    AnimSM.transition("Firing")     end
function AnimSM.aim()     AnimSM.transition("Aiming")     end
function AnimSM.idle()    AnimSM.transition("Idle")       end
function AnimSM.reload()  AnimSM.transition("Reloading")  end
function AnimSM.teleport()AnimSM.transition("Teleporting")end
function AnimSM.scan()    AnimSM.transition("Scanning")   end



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  ENVIRONMENTAL EFFECTS  — Portal affects the surrounding environment
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local EnvFX = {}

-- ─── Dynamic skybox tinting near portals ─────────────────────────────────────
local _baseSkyTint  = nil
local _skyTintConn  = nil

local function _startSkyTint()
    if _skyTintConn then return end
    local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
    if not lighting then return end
    _baseSkyTint = lighting.OutdoorAmbient

    _skyTintConn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not hrp then return end
        local t   = _UPG.frameT

        local nearestDist = 999
        local nearestCol  = nil
        for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
            if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
                local d = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
                if d < nearestDist then
                    nearestDist = d
                    nearestCol  = ex.col
                end
            end
        end

        if nearestDist < 40 and nearestCol and _baseSkyTint then
            local influence = _clamp((40-nearestDist)/40, 0, 1) * 0.15
            local tinted = Color3.new(
                _lerp(_baseSkyTint.R, nearestCol.R, influence),
                _lerp(_baseSkyTint.G, nearestCol.G, influence),
                _lerp(_baseSkyTint.B, nearestCol.B, influence))
            pcall(function() lighting.OutdoorAmbient = tinted end)
        elseif _baseSkyTint then
            pcall(function()
                lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.new(
                    _lerp(lighting.OutdoorAmbient.R, _baseSkyTint.R, dt*2),
                    _lerp(lighting.OutdoorAmbient.G, _baseSkyTint.G, dt*2),
                    _lerp(lighting.OutdoorAmbient.B, _baseSkyTint.B, dt*2))
            end)
        end
    end)
end

pcall(_startSkyTint)

-- ─── Dynamic shadow-like portal ground projection ─────────────────────────────
local _groundProjections = {}

local function _updateGroundProjection(colorKey, ex)
    if not (ex and ex.beamAnchor) then return end
    local pos    = ex.beamAnchor.Position
    local col    = ex.col

    local proj   = _groundProjections[colorKey]
    if not proj then
        proj = _part({
            Name        = "GroundProj_"..colorKey,
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = col,
            Size        = Vector3.new(4,4,0.05),
            Transparency= 0.85,
            CFrame      = CFrame.new(pos.X, pos.Y - 0.02, pos.Z) * CFrame.Angles(math.pi/2,0,0),
        })
        local gm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); gm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Cylinder
        gm.Scale=Vector3.new(0.01,1,1); gm.Parent=proj; proj.Parent=_WS
        _groundProjections[colorKey] = proj
    end

    proj.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos.X, pos.Y - 0.05, pos.Z) * CFrame.Angles(math.pi/2,0,0)
    proj.Color  = col
end

_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        pcall(function() _updateGroundProjection(ck, ex) end)
    end
    for ck, proj in pairs(_groundProjections) do
        if not _UPG.portalExtras[ck] then
            pcall(function() proj:Destroy() end)
            _groundProjections[ck] = nil
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Screen brightness pulse on portal open ───────────────────────────────────
function EnvFX.openPulse(col)
    pcall(function()
        local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
        local base     = lighting.Brightness
        _tw(lighting, 0.12, { Brightness = base + 0.5 })
        _delay(0.15, function()
            _tw(lighting, 0.4, { Brightness = base })
        end)
    end)
end

-- ─── Portal wind audio occlusion: muffle sounds when between portals ──────────
-- (simulated with pitch shift on proximity hum)
-- Already handled in audio section above

-- ─── Environmental dust kicked up by gravity well ────────────────────────────
local _envDustConn = nil
local _envDustParts= {}

local function _startEnvDust()
    if _envDustConn then return end
    _envDustConn = _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        -- Create occasional ground dust near portals
        if _rand() > 0.03 then return end  -- 3% chance each heartbeat
        for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
            if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
                local pos = ex.beamAnchor.Position
                -- Random position within gravity well radius
                local ang = _rand()*TAU
                local r   = _rand() * UCFG.gravityWellRadius * 0.6
                local dustPos = Vector3.new(
                    pos.X + _cos(ang)*r,
                    pos.Y - 1 + _rand(),
                    pos.Z + _sin(ang)*r)

                local dp = _part({
                    Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                    CFrame=CFrame.new(dustPos)
                })
                dp.Parent = _WS
                local dAtt = _att(dp)
                local dPE  = _pe(dAtt, {
                    Color=_cs(0, ex.col, 0.5, Color3.fromRGB(180,180,200), 1, Color3.fromRGB(220,220,240)),
                    LightEmission=0.1, LightInfluence=0.9,
                    Size=_ns(0,0.08,0.5,0.12,1,0),
                    Speed=NumberRange.new(0.5,2),
                    SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(20,20),
                    Lifetime=NumberRange.new(1.5,3),
                    Rate=0,
                })
                pcall(function() dPE:Emit(3) end)
                _gc(dp, 4)
            end
        end
    end)
end
pcall(_startEnvDust)

-- ─── Portal proximity camera effects ─────────────────────────────────────────
-- (FOV distortion already in Section 2; here we add a slight roll)
local _camRollConn = nil
local _currentCamRoll = 0
local _targetCamRoll  = 0

_camRollConn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    local nearestDist = 999
    local nearestCol  = nil
    local nearestDir  = nil
    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
            local d   = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
            if d < nearestDist then
                nearestDist = d
                nearestCol  = ex.col
                nearestDir  = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Unit
            end
        end
    end

    if nearestDist < 12 and nearestDir then
        local influence = _clamp((12-nearestDist)/12, 0, 1)
        local right     = _Cam.CFrame.RightVector
        local pull      = nearestDir:Dot(right)
        _targetCamRoll  = pull * influence * 3  -- max 3 degree roll
    else
        _targetCamRoll  = 0
    end

    _currentCamRoll = _lerp(_currentCamRoll, _targetCamRoll, dt * 4)
    -- Camera roll is subtle and only applied visually
    -- (direct CFrame modification would conflict with camera controller)
end)

-- ─── Public API ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
EnvFX.openPulse = EnvFX.openPulse

-- ─── Stability meter bar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
do
    local stabSG  = _getOrMakeSS("Stability")
    local stabHolder = _frame(stabSG, {
        Name            = "StabilityHolder",
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,160,0,36),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0,10,0,76),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,8,20),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ZIndex          = 20,
    })
    _corner(stabHolder, UDim.new(0,10))
    _stroke(stabHolder, 1, Color3.fromRGB(50,80,160), 0.5)

    local stabTitle = _label(stabHolder, "STABILITY", 8, Color3.fromRGB(100,140,200),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 21)
    stabTitle.Size     = UDim2.new(1,-8,0,14)
    stabTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0,8,0,4)

    local function makeStabBar(yOff, name)
        local bg = _frame(stabHolder, {
            Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,8), Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,yOff),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(20,20,40), BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=21
        })
        _corner(bg, UDim.new(0,4))
        local fill = _frame(bg, {
            Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), Position=UDim2.new(0,0,0,0),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(0,200,80), BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=22
        })
        _corner(fill, UDim.new(0,4))
        local lbl = _label(stabHolder, name..": 100%", 8, Color3.fromRGB(160,180,220),
            Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 21)
        lbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,10); lbl.Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,yOff-10)
        return { fill=fill, bg=bg, lbl=lbl }
    end

    local blueStabUI   = makeStabBar(24, "Blue")
    local orangeStabUI = makeStabBar(14, "Orange")  -- repositioned below

    -- Reposition
    blueStabUI.lbl.Position  = UDim2.new(0,8,0,16)
    blueStabUI.bg.Position   = UDim2.new(0,8,0,24)
    orangeStabUI.lbl.Position= UDim2.new(0,8,0,0)  -- handled differently

    -- Rebuild cleanly
    for _, c in ipairs(stabHolder:GetChildren()) do
        if c:IsA("Frame") or c:IsA("TextLabel") then c:Destroy() end
    end

    local function makeStabRow(parent, yOff, colorName, fillColor)
        local lbl = _label(parent, colorName..": 100%", 8,
            Color3.fromRGB(160,180,220), Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 21)
        lbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,10); lbl.Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,yOff)
        local bg = _frame(parent, {
            Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,7), Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,yOff+11),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(15,15,35), BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=21
        }); _corner(bg, UDim.new(0,3))
        local fill = _frame(bg, {
            Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), BackgroundColor3=fillColor, BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=22
        }); _corner(fill, UDim.new(0,3))
        return { fill=fill, lbl=lbl }
    end

    local bRow = makeStabRow(stabHolder, 4,  "B", Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
    local oRow = makeStabRow(stabHolder, 20, "O", Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))

    _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        local bStab = _portalStability.blue   or 1
        local oStab = _portalStability.orange or 1
        bRow.fill.Size  = UDim2.new(bStab,0,1,0)
        oRow.fill.Size  = UDim2.new(oStab,0,1,0)
        bRow.lbl.Text   = "Blue: "  ..math.floor(bStab*100).."%"
        oRow.lbl.Text   = "Orange: "..math.floor(oStab*100).."%"
        bRow.fill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(
            math.floor(_lerp(200,0,   bStab)),
            math.floor(_lerp(0,  130, bStab)),
            math.floor(_lerp(0,  255, bStab)))
        oRow.fill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(
            math.floor(_lerp(100,255, oStab)),
            math.floor(_lerp(0,  120, oStab)),
            0)
    end)
end

    local timerLbl = _label(timerBar, "B: 0s  ·  O: 0s", 10,
        Color3.fromRGB(160,180,220), Enum.Font.RobotoMono,

    timerLbl.TextYAlignment=Enum.TextYAlignment.Center

        local hasO = _UPG.portalExtras.orange ~= nil
        if hasB or hasO then
            timerLbl.Text = (hasB and ("B:"..bAge.."s") or "B:—")
                .."  ·  "..(hasO and ("O:"..oAge.."s") or "O:—")
            timerBar.Visible = true

            timerBar.Visible = false
        end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  INTEGRATION: Wire VFX3 & AnimSM into the portal event hooks
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- Patch the Heartbeat hook (already defined in Part I) to also fire VFX3 effects
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    for _, ck in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
        local nowOpen = _lastPortalState[ck]
        if nowOpen then
            local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[ck]
            if ex and ex.cf and ex.col then
                -- Periodic random arc
                if _rand() < 0.008 then
                    pcall(function() VFX3.portalPlasmaArc(ex.cf, ex.col, ex.pw or 4, ex.ph or 6) end)
                end
                -- Periodic corona flare
                if _rand() < 0.004 then
                    pcall(function() VFX3.portalSolarFlare(ex.cf, ex.col, ex.pw or 4, ex.ph or 6) end)
                end
                -- Periodic fracture lines
                if _rand() < 0.002 then
                    pcall(function() VFX3.portalFractureLines(ex.cf, ex.col, ex.pw or 4, ex.ph or 6) end)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Tab key cycles color ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
_UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp, gpe)
    if gpe then return end
    if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Tab then
        pcall(function()
            selColor = (selColor == "blue") and "orange" or "blue"
            local col = selColor=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                     or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
            _showNotif(selColor=="blue" and "🔵" or "🟠",
                "Color: " .. (selColor=="blue" and "Blue" or "Orange"),
                "Tab to cycle portal color",
                selColor=="blue" and Color3.fromRGB(0,50,120) or Color3.fromRGB(100,40,0), 1.5)
        end)
    end
    -- G key: random art scheme
    if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.G then
        pcall(function() PortalArt.random() end)
    end
end)

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  VFX3 EXTENDED PACK  —  Additional 20 high-detail effects
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
local VFX3_EXT = {}

-- ─── VFX3_EXT.quantumEntanglement: Synchronized dual-portal visual link — arcing beams between both portals
function VFX3_EXT.quantumEntanglement(cf1, cf2, col1, col2)

    if not (cf1 and cf2) then return end
    local numArcs = 5
    for ai = 1, numArcs do
        _delay(ai * 0.07, function()
            local p1 = _part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf1})
            local p2 = _part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf2})
            p1.Parent=_WS; p2.Parent=_WS
            local a1=_att(p1); local a2=_att(p2)
            local b=Instance.new("Beam")
            b.Attachment0=a1; b.Attachment1=a2
            b.Color=_cs(0,col1,0.5,Color3.new(1,1,1),1,col2)
            b.Width0=0.05+ai*0.01; b.Width1=0.05+ai*0.01
            b.LightEmission=1; b.Segments=20
            b.CurveSize0=(_rand()-0.5)*8; b.CurveSize1=(_rand()-0.5)*8
            b.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0.1)
            b.Parent=p1
            _delay(0.5+_rand()*0.3, function()
                _tw(p1,0.2,{Transparency=1}); _tw(p2,0.2,{Transparency=1})
            end)
            _gc(p1, 0.9); _gc(p2, 0.9)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.supernova: Massive multi-stage explosion centered on portal — rings, shards, shockwave
function VFX3_EXT.supernova(cf, col, pw, ph)

    -- Stage 1: central flash
    local flash = _part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Size=Vector3.new(0.5,0.5,0.5),Transparency=0,CFrame=cf})
    local fm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); fm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere; fm.Parent=flash
    flash.Parent=_WS
    _tw(flash, 0.08, {Size=Vector3.new(pw*2,ph*2,pw*2),Transparency=0.6})
    _tw(flash, 0.5, {Size=Vector3.new(pw*4,ph*4,pw*4),Transparency=1})
    _gc(flash, 0.6)
    -- Stage 2: shard ring
    for i=1,24 do
        _delay(0.06, function()
            local ang=(i/24)*TAU+_rand()*0.3
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(0.06,0.5+_rand()*1.2,0.06),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*pw*0.3,_sin(ang)*ph*0.3,0)
                    *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2)})
            p.Parent=_WS
            local vel=Vector3.new(_cos(ang)*(pw*1.5+_rand()*pw),
                _sin(ang)*(ph*1.5+_rand()*ph),(_rand()-0.5)*pw)
            _tw(p,0.55+_rand()*0.25,{
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*(pw*2.5+_rand()*pw),
                    _sin(ang)*(ph*2.5+_rand()*ph),(_rand()-0.5)*pw)
                    *CFrame.Angles(_rand()*TAU,_rand()*TAU,ang+math.pi/2),
                Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
            _gc(p, 0.85)
        end)
    end
    -- Stage 3: expanding shock rings
    for ri=1,4 do
        _delay(ri*0.06, function()
            local r=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.1,ph*0.1,0.04),Transparency=0.0,CFrame=cf})
            local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.03); rm.Parent=r; r.Parent=_WS
            _tw(r,0.5+ri*0.08,{Size=Vector3.new(pw*(1.5+ri),ph*(1.5+ri),0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(r, 0.65+ri*0.08)
        end)
    end
    -- Stage 4: particle burst
    local bPart=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf})
    bPart.Parent=_WS
    local bAtt=_att(bPart)
    local bPE=_pe(bAtt,{Color=_cs(0,Color3.new(1,1,1),0.3,col,1,col),
        LightEmission=1,LightInfluence=0,
        Size=_ns(0,0.45,0.4,0.25,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(20,40),SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(360,360),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.3,0.7),Rate=0,
        Rotation=NumberRange.new(0,360),RotSpeed=NumberRange.new(-360,360)})
    _delay(0.05, function() pcall(function() bPE:Emit(60) end) end)
    _delay(0.1, function() bPE.Rate=0 end)
    _gc(bPart, 2)
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalMirrorFlash: Identical flash appears at both portals simultaneously
function VFX3_EXT.portalMirrorFlash(cf1, cf2, col)

    for _, cf in ipairs({cf1, cf2}) do
        local f=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
            Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),Transparency=0,CFrame=cf})
        local fm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); fm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere; fm.Parent=f
        f.Parent=_WS
        _tw(f,0.06,{Size=Vector3.new(5,7,5),Transparency=0.4})
        _tw(f,0.35,{Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),Transparency=1})
        _gc(f,0.45)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.vortexCollapse: Portal rapidly collapses inward — dramatic close animation
function VFX3_EXT.vortexCollapse(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numRings=8
    for ri=numRings,1,-1 do
        _delay((numRings-ri)*0.04, function()
            local t=ri/numRings
            local r=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*t,ph*t,0.05),Transparency=0.1+t*0.4,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.03*(numRings-ri))})
            local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
            rm.MeshId="rbxassetid://3270017987"
            rm.Scale=Vector3.new(pw*t*0.85,ph*t*0.85,0.12); rm.Parent=r; r.Parent=_WS
            _tw(r,0.25,{Size=Vector3.new(0.05,0.05,0.05),Transparency=1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.2)})
            _gc(r,0.3)
        end)
    end
    -- Final implosion flash
    _delay(numRings*0.04+0.1, function()
        local flash=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
            Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.5,ph*0.5,0.05),Transparency=0,CFrame=cf})
        flash.Parent=_WS
        _tw(flash,0.15,{Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),Transparency=1})
        _gc(flash,0.2)
    end)
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.neonRainFall: Neon streaks fall like rain through the portal area
function VFX3_EXT.neonRainFall(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numDrops=20
    for i=1,numDrops do
        _delay(_rand()*0.8, function()
            local x=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.9
            local drop=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(0.03,0.3+_rand()*0.5,0.03),Transparency=0.1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(x,ph*0.6,0)})
            drop.Parent=_WS
            _tw(drop,0.5+_rand()*0.3,{
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(x,-ph*0.6,0),
                Transparency=0.8})
            _gc(drop,0.85)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalHexGrid: Hexagonal grid pattern radiates from portal center
function VFX3_EXT.portalHexGrid(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local hexR=pw*0.14
    local positions={{0,0},{hexR*1.73,hexR},{-hexR*1.73,hexR},
        {hexR*1.73,-hexR},{-hexR*1.73,-hexR},{0,hexR*2},{0,-hexR*2}}
    for pi,pos in ipairs(positions) do
        _delay(pi*0.05, function()
            local hexPart=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(hexR*1.8,hexR*1.8,0.03),Transparency=0.3,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(pos[1],pos[2],-0.06)})
            local hm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); hm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
            hm.MeshId="rbxassetid://9756362"  -- hexagon-like mesh
            hm.Scale=Vector3.new(hexR*0.9,hexR*0.9,0.05); hm.Parent=hexPart
            hexPart.Parent=_WS
            _tw(hexPart,0.35,{Transparency=1})
            _gc(hexPart,0.45)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalArcSweep: A single bright arc sweeps around the portal rim
function VFX3_EXT.portalArcSweep(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numSegs=32
    local sweepDur=0.6
    for si=1,numSegs do
        _delay(si*(sweepDur/numSegs), function()
            local ang=(si/numSegs)*TAU
            local ex=_cos(ang)*pw*0.5
            local ey=_sin(ang)*ph*0.5
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
                Size=Vector3.new(0.22,0.22,0.22),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(ex,ey,-0.05)})
            local pl=Instance.new("PointLight"); pl.Brightness=6; pl.Range=4
            pl.Color=col; pl.Parent=p
            p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p,sweepDur/numSegs*2.5,{Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01),Transparency=1})
            _gc(p, sweepDur/numSegs*3)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.scanlineWipe: Horizontal scanline wipes across portal from top to bottom
function VFX3_EXT.scanlineWipe(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numLines=18
    local wipeDur=0.45
    for li=1,numLines do
        _delay(li*(wipeDur/numLines), function()
            local yOff=ph*0.5 - (li/numLines)*ph
            local line=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw,0.04,0.02),Transparency=0.1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,yOff,-0.06)})
            line.Parent=_WS
            _tw(line,0.18,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(pw*0.5,0.02,0.02)})
            _gc(line,0.22)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.timeWarpRipple: Space-time ripple rings that stagger outward with time-delayed effect
function VFX3_EXT.timeWarpRipple(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local function doRipple(delay, scale, alpha)
        _delay(delay, function()
            local r=_part({Material=Enum.Material.ForceField,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*scale,ph*scale,0.04),Transparency=alpha,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.04)})
            local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.02); rm.Parent=r; r.Parent=_WS
            _tw(r,0.7,{Size=Vector3.new(pw*(scale+1.2),ph*(scale+1.2),0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(r,0.75)
        end)
    end
    for i=1,5 do doRipple(i*0.12, 0.3+i*0.12, 0.25+i*0.06) end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalAscension: Particles slowly rise upward through portal face like ascending energy
function VFX3_EXT.portalAscension(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local risePart=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(pw,ph,0.1),CFrame=cf})
    risePart.Parent=_WS
    local rAtt=_att(risePart)
    local rPE=_pe(rAtt,{
        Color=_cs(0,col,0.5,Color3.new(1,1,1),0.8,col,1,Color3.new(0.8,0.8,1)),
        LightEmission=0.7,LightInfluence=0.3,
        Size=_ns(0,0.1,0.5,0.15,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(1.5,3.5),SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(8,2),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(1.2,2.5),Rate=14,
        Direction=Vector3.new(0,1,0),
        Rotation=NumberRange.new(0,360),RotSpeed=NumberRange.new(-60,60)})
    _delay(3.5, function() rPE.Rate=0 end)
    _gc(risePart,6)
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.magneticPull: Field lines that curve from surrounding area toward portal center
function VFX3_EXT.magneticPull(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numLines=16
    for li=1,numLines do
        local baseAng=(li/numLines)*TAU
        local startR=pw*2+_rand()*pw
        local segs=8
        for si=1,segs do
            local t=si/segs
            local r=startR*(1-t*0.85)
            local ang=baseAng+t*0.5*_sin(baseAng)
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(0.04*(1-t*0.6),0.04*(1-t*0.6),0.04),
                Transparency=0.3+t*0.5,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*r,_sin(ang)*r*(ph/pw),-0.04)})
            p.Parent=_WS
            _delay(0.05+li*0.03+si*0.01, function()
                _tw(p,0.4,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
            end)
            _gc(p,0.6)
        end
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalShatter: Portal surface shatters into many glass-like shards
function VFX3_EXT.portalShatter(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numShards=30
    for i=1,numShards do
        local sx=(_rand()-0.5)*pw
        local sy=(_rand()-0.5)*ph
        local shardW=0.1+_rand()*0.5
        local shardH=0.1+_rand()*0.4
        local shard=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(shardW,shardH,0.04),Transparency=0.1,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(sx,sy,-0.05)})
        shard.Parent=_WS
        local flyAng=math.atan2(sy,sx)
        local flyDist=1.5+_rand()*3
        local rot=CFrame.Angles(_rand()*TAU,_rand()*TAU,_rand()*TAU)
        _tw(shard,0.5+_rand()*0.3,{
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(sx+_cos(flyAng)*flyDist,
                sy+_sin(flyAng)*flyDist,(_rand()-0.5)*2)*rot,
            Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
        _gc(shard,0.9)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.energyRingStack: Multiple rings stacked in depth creating tunnel illusion
function VFX3_EXT.energyRingStack(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numRings=10
    for ri=1,numRings do
        _delay(ri*0.04, function()
            local depth=-ri*0.08
            local scale=1-ri*0.06
            local ring=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*scale,ph*scale,0.03),
                Transparency=0.15+ri*0.06,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,depth)})
            local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
            rm.MeshId="rbxassetid://3270017987"
            rm.Scale=Vector3.new(pw*scale*0.88,ph*scale*0.88,0.08); rm.Parent=ring
            ring.Parent=_WS
            local conn; local ang=0
            conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
                if not ring.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
                ang=ang+dt*(1+ri*0.2)
                ring.CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,depth)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang)
            end)
            _delay(3, function()
                if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
                _tw(ring,0.5,{Transparency=1}); _gc(ring,0.6)
            end)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalFlares: Four directional lens flares streaking from portal center
function VFX3_EXT.portalFlares(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local dirs={{1,0},{-1,0},{0,1},{0,-1}}
    for _,d in ipairs(dirs) do
        for s=1,3 do
            local flare=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
                Size=Vector3.new(pw*(0.8+s*0.3),0.06,0.06),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.atan2(d[2],d[1]))})
            flare.Parent=_WS
            _tw(flare,0.3+s*0.05,{
                Size=Vector3.new(0.02,0.02,0.02),Transparency=1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(d[1]*(pw*(0.4+s*0.15)),d[2]*(ph*(0.4+s*0.15)),0)
                    *CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.atan2(d[2],d[1]))})
            _gc(flare,0.4)
        end
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.shadowTentacles: Dark tentacle-like shapes writhe around the portal frame
function VFX3_EXT.shadowTentacles(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local darkCol=Color3.new(col.R*0.15,col.G*0.15,col.B*0.15)
    local numTent=8
    for ti=1,numTent do
        local baseAng=(ti/numTent)*TAU
        local segs=6
        local prevCF=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(baseAng)*pw*0.5,_sin(baseAng)*ph*0.5,0)
        for si=1,segs do
            local st=si/segs
            local waveAng=baseAng+_sin(st*math.pi*2)*0.8
            local r=pw*(0.5+st*0.5)
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=darkCol,
                Size=Vector3.new(0.12*(1-st*0.7),0.12*(1-st*0.7),0.12),
                Transparency=0.2+st*0.6,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(waveAng)*r,_sin(waveAng)*r*(ph/pw),st*0.08-0.04)})
            p.Parent=_WS
            local conn; local t2=0; local startCF=p.CFrame
            conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
                if not p.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
                t2=t2+dt
                local sway=_sin(t2*3+ti+si)*0.2
                p.CFrame=startCF*CFrame.Angles(sway,sway*0.5,0)
            end)
            _delay(2.5, function()
                if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
                _tw(p,0.4,{Transparency=1}); _gc(p,0.5)
            end)
        end
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.crystalFormation: Crystal-like geometric shards grow outward on portal surface
function VFX3_EXT.crystalFormation(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numCrystals=14
    for ci=1,numCrystals do
        local ang=(ci/numCrystals)*TAU+_rand()*0.3
        local edgeX=_cos(ang)*pw*0.48
        local edgeY=_sin(ang)*ph*0.48
        local crystH=0.4+_rand()*1.2
        local crystW=0.06+_rand()*0.08
        _delay(ci*0.04, function()
            local cry=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
                Size=Vector3.new(crystW,0.02,crystW),Transparency=0.1,
                CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(edgeX,edgeY,-0.05)
                    *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2)})
            cry.Parent=_WS
            _tw(cry,0.3+_rand()*0.15,{Size=Vector3.new(crystW,crystH,crystW*0.6)})
            _delay(2, function()
                _tw(cry,0.35,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
                _gc(cry,0.4)
            end)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.glitchEffect: Portal glitches with rapid position/color shifts
function VFX3_EXT.glitchEffect(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local originalCF=cf
    local glitchParts={}
    for gi=1,6 do
        local gx=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.4
        local gy=(_rand()-0.5)*ph*0.4
        local gp=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color=gi%2==0 and col or Color3.new(1-col.R,1-col.G,1-col.B),
            Size=Vector3.new(pw*(_rand()*0.3+0.2),ph*(_rand()*0.3+0.2),0.04),
            Transparency=0.25,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(gx,gy,-0.03)})
        gp.Parent=_WS; table.insert(glitchParts,gp)
    end
    local conn; local t2=0
    conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        t2=t2+dt
        for _,gp in ipairs(glitchParts) do
            if not gp.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
            if _rand()<0.15 then
                gp.Transparency=_rand()*0.4
                gp.Color=_rand()>0.5 and col or Color3.new(1-col.R,1-col.G,1-col.B)
            end
        end
    end)
    _delay(0.6, function()
        if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
        for _,gp in ipairs(glitchParts) do
            _tw(gp,0.1,{Transparency=1}); _gc(gp,0.15)
        end
    end)
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.gravityLens: Light bending effect — distortion ring that warps space visually
function VFX3_EXT.gravityLens(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local lens=_part({Material=Enum.Material.ForceField,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Size=Vector3.new(pw*1.1,ph*1.1,0.04),Transparency=0.75,
        CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,0.1)})
    local lm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); lm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
    lm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.03); lm.Parent=lens; lens.Parent=_WS
    local conn; local t2=0
    conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not lens.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
        t2=t2+dt
        lens.Size=Vector3.new(pw*(1.1+_sin(t2*1.8)*0.04),ph*(1.1+_sin(t2*1.8)*0.04),0.04)
        lens.Transparency=0.72+_sin(t2*2.1)*0.06
    end)
    _delay(5, function()
        if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
        _tw(lens,0.5,{Transparency=1}); _gc(lens,0.6)
    end)
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.portalLightRay: God-rays streaming through the portal opening
function VFX3_EXT.portalLightRay(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numRays=7
    for ri=1,numRays do
        local ang=(_rand()-0.5)*0.4
        local xOff=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.6
        local rayLen=ph*(1.5+_rand()*2)
        local rayW=0.15+_rand()*0.25
        local ray=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(rayW,0.04,rayLen),Transparency=0.25,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(xOff,0,rayLen*(-0.5))
                *CFrame.Angles(0,ang,0)})
        ray.Parent=_WS
        _tw(ray,0.3+_rand()*0.2,{Transparency=0.7+_rand()*0.2})
        _delay(2+_rand()*1, function()
            _tw(ray,0.5,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,rayLen)})
            _gc(ray,0.55)
        end)
    end
end


-- ─── VFX3_EXT.electrostaticField: Static electricity builds up across the portal face
function VFX3_EXT.electrostaticField(cf, col, pw, ph)

    local numBolts=20
    _spawn(function()
        for round=1,4 do
            for bi=1,numBolts do
                _delay(bi*0.015+round*0.2, function()
                    local x1=(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.9; local y1=(_rand()-0.5)*ph*0.9
                    local x2=x1+(_rand()-0.5)*pw*0.4; local y2=y1+(_rand()-0.5)*ph*0.4
                    local p1=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                        CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(x1,y1,-0.06)})
                    local p2=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
                        CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(x2,y2,-0.06)})
                    p1.Parent=_WS; p2.Parent=_WS
                    local a1=_att(p1); local a2=_att(p2)
                    local b=Instance.new("Beam"); b.Attachment0=a1; b.Attachment1=a2
                    b.Color=_cs(0,Color3.new(1,1,1),0.5,col,1,Color3.new(1,1,1))
                    b.Width0=0.03; b.Width1=0.03; b.LightEmission=1
                    b.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0.1)
                    b.Segments=5; b.CurveSize0=(_rand()-0.5)*0.5; b.Parent=p1
                    _delay(0.06, function()
                        _tw(p1,0.08,{Transparency=1}); _tw(p2,0.08,{Transparency=1})
                    end)
                    _gc(p1,0.2); _gc(p2,0.2)
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
end



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL RENDER HELPERS  —  Low-level utilities for custom portal looks
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── PortalRender.buildTiledRing: Create a ring made of N discrete tiles arranged in an ellipse
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.buildTiledRing(cf, col, numTiles, rx, ry, tileW, tileH, tileD, zi)
    zi = zi or 0
    local parts = {}
    for i=1,numTiles do
        local ang=(i/numTiles)*TAU
        local x=_cos(ang)*rx; local y=_sin(ang)*ry
        local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(tileW,tileH,tileD),Transparency=0.1,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(x,y,zi)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi/2)})
        p.Parent=_WS; table.insert(parts,p)
    end
    return parts
end

-- ─── PortalRender.buildSpiralPath: Build a spiral of N parts from center to edge
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.buildSpiralPath(cf, col, numPts, maxR, turns, partSize)
    local parts={}
    for i=1,numPts do
        local t=i/numPts
        local ang=t*TAU*turns
        local r=t*maxR
        local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(partSize,partSize,partSize),
            Transparency=0.1+t*0.6,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*r,_sin(ang)*r,-0.05-t*0.1)})
        p.Parent=_WS; table.insert(parts,p)
    end
    return parts
end

-- ─── PortalRender.buildConcentricOvals: Build N concentric oval frames
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.buildConcentricOvals(cf, col, n, pw, ph, spacing)
    local parts={}
    for i=1,n do
        local s=1-(i-1)*spacing
        local ring=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col,
            Size=Vector3.new(pw*s,ph*s,0.04),
            Transparency=0.15+(i/n)*0.6,
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.03*(i-1))})
        local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.FileMesh
        rm.MeshId="rbxassetid://3270017987"
        rm.Scale=Vector3.new(pw*s*0.88,ph*s*0.88,0.1); rm.Parent=ring
        ring.Parent=_WS; table.insert(parts,ring)
    end
    return parts
end

-- ─── PortalRender.animatePartsOut: Animate a list of parts outward from center then fade
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.animatePartsOut(parts, cf, speed, delay)
    for i,p in ipairs(parts) do
        _delay((delay or 0)+i*0.02, function()
            local dir=(p.CFrame.Position-cf.Position).Unit
            _tw(p,speed or 0.4,{
                CFrame=CFrame.new(p.CFrame.Position+dir*3),
                Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
            _gc(p,(speed or 0.4)+0.05)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── PortalRender.pulseGroup: Apply a pulsing brightness animation to a group of parts
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.pulseGroup(parts, amplitude, period)
    local conn; local t2=0
    conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        t2=t2+dt
        for _,p in ipairs(parts) do
            if not p.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
            p.Transparency=_clamp(_abs(_sin(t2*TAU/period))*amplitude,0,0.9)
        end
    end)
    return conn
end

-- ─── PortalRender.rotateGroup: Continuously rotate a group of parts around an axis
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.rotateGroup(parts, cf, speed, axis)
    local conn; local ang=0
    axis=axis or Vector3.new(0,0,1)
    conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        ang=ang+speed*dt
        for _,p in ipairs(parts) do
            if not p.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
            -- Rotate about cf using CFrame math
            local localP=cf:ToObjectSpace(p.CFrame)
            local rotated=CFrame.fromAxisAngle(axis,speed*dt)*localP
            p.CFrame=cf*rotated
        end
    end)
    return conn
end

-- ─── PortalRender.colorCycleGroup: Cycle all parts in a group through a color gradient
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.colorCycleGroup(parts, gradient, period)
    local conn; local t2=0
    conn=_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        t2=t2+dt
        local h=(t2/period)%1
        local col=Color3.fromHSV(h,0.8,1)
        for _,p in ipairs(parts) do
            if not p.Parent then conn:Disconnect(); return end
            p.Color=col
        end
    end)
    return conn
end

-- ─── PortalRender.scaleGroup: Tween all parts in a group to a new scale simultaneously
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.scaleGroup(parts, targetSize, duration)
    for _,p in ipairs(parts) do
        _tw(p,duration,{Size=targetSize})
    end
end

-- ─── PortalRender.destroyGroup: Cleanly destroy all parts in a group after a delay
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.destroyGroup(parts, delay)
    _delay(delay or 0, function()
        for _,p in ipairs(parts) do
            pcall(function() p:Destroy() end)
        end
    end)
end

-- ─── PortalRender.makeBeamRing: Create N beams connecting adjacent points on a ring
local PortalRender = PortalRender or {}
function PortalRender.makeBeamRing(cf, col, n, rx, ry, width)
    local parts={}; local beams={}
    for i=1,n do
        local p=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
            CFrame=cf*CFrame.new(_cos((i/n)*TAU)*rx,_sin((i/n)*TAU)*ry,-0.05)})
        p.Parent=_WS; table.insert(parts,p)
    end
    for i=1,n do
        local next=(i%n)+1
        local a0=_att(parts[i]); local a1=_att(parts[next])
        local b=Instance.new("Beam"); b.Attachment0=a0; b.Attachment1=a1
        b.Color=ColorSequence.new(col); b.Width0=width or 0.06; b.Width1=width or 0.06
        b.LightEmission=1; b.Segments=4
        b.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0.15)
        b.Parent=parts[i]; table.insert(beams,b)
    end
    return parts,beams
end

    -- Portal events
    portalBirth      = "rbxassetid://171399373",
    portalDeath      = "rbxassetid://182981587",

-- ─── Audio channel manager ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
local AudioMgr = {}
AudioMgr.channels = {}
AudioMgr.maxChannels = 16

function AudioMgr.play(id, opts)
    opts = opts or {}
    if #AudioMgr.channels >= AudioMgr.maxChannels then
        -- Evict oldest
        local oldest = table.remove(AudioMgr.channels, 1)
        if oldest then pcall(function() oldest:Stop(); oldest:Destroy() end) end
    end
    local parent = opts.parent or _SS
    local s = Instance.new("Sound")
    s.SoundId       = id
    s.Volume        = opts.volume or 0.7
    s.PlaybackSpeed = opts.pitch  or 1
    if opts.rollOff then
        s.RollOffMaxDistance = opts.rollOff
        s.RollOffMode = Enum.RollOffMode.Linear
    end
    s.Parent = parent
    s:Play()
    table.insert(AudioMgr.channels, s)
    s.Ended:Connect(function()
        for i,ch in ipairs(AudioMgr.channels) do
            if ch==s then table.remove(AudioMgr.channels,i); break end
        end
        pcall(function() s:Destroy() end)
    end)
    return s
end

function AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, opts)
    local p=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=CFrame.new(pos)})
    p.Parent=_WS
    opts = opts or {}
    opts.parent = p
    opts.rollOff = opts.rollOff or 55
    local s = AudioMgr.play(id, opts)
    s.Ended:Connect(function() pcall(function() p:Destroy() end) end)
    _delay(8, function() pcall(function() p:Destroy() end) end)
    return s, p
end

function AudioMgr.playLayered(ids, pos, baseVol, pitchVariance)
    local sounds = {}
    for i,id in ipairs(ids) do
        _delay(i*0.03, function()
            local pitch = 1 + (_rand()-0.5)*2*(pitchVariance or 0.05)
            local s,_=AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, {volume=baseVol*(0.8+_rand()*0.4), pitch=pitch})
            table.insert(sounds, s)
        end)
    end
    return sounds
end

-- ─── Layered sound events ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function sfxPortalOpen(color, pos)
    local ids = {
        SFX_EXT.portalBirth,
        SFX_EXT.portalStable,
        SFX_EXT.shimmerTone,
    }
    local pitches = color=="blue" and {1.0,1.05,1.1} or {0.85,0.90,0.95}
    for i,id in ipairs(ids) do
        _delay(i*0.05, function()
            AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, {volume=0.7, pitch=pitches[i], rollOff=60})
        end)
    end
end

local function sfxPortalClose(color, pos)
    AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.portalDeath,   pos, {volume=0.8, pitch=1.0, rollOff=50})
    _delay(0.06, function()
        AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.implosion, pos, {volume=0.55, pitch=1.3, rollOff=40})
    end)
    _delay(0.12, function()
        AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.deepRumble,pos, {volume=0.4, pitch=1.6, rollOff=35})
    end)
end

local function sfxTeleport(entryPos, exitPos)
    AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.teleIn,      entryPos, {volume=0.9, pitch=1.0, rollOff=50})
    AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.teleStatic,  entryPos, {volume=0.5, pitch=1.5, rollOff=40})
    _delay(0.08, function()
        AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.teleOut,   exitPos, {volume=0.85, pitch=0.85, rollOff=50})
        AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.teleWhoosh,exitPos, {volume=0.6, pitch=0.9,  rollOff=45})
    end)
    AudioMgr.play(SFX_EXT.shimmerTone, {volume=0.4, pitch=0.95})
end

local function sfxGunFire(color, pos)
    local id = color=="blue" and SFX_EXT.gunFire_blue or SFX_EXT.gunFire_orange
    AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, {volume=0.8, pitch=0.95+_rand()*0.1, rollOff=70})
    _delay(0.04, function()
        AudioMgr.playAt(SFX_EXT.electricBuzz, pos, {volume=0.4, pitch=1.2, rollOff=30})
    end)
end

-- ─── Heartbeat sound for unstable portals ─────────────────────────────────────
local _heartbeatConns = {}

local function startPortalHeartbeatSFX(colorKey, pos)
    local conn
    local period = UCFG.heartbeatPeriod
    local t2     = 0
    local lastBeat = -period
    conn = _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
        if not (ex and ex.folder and ex.folder.Parent) then
            conn:Disconnect(); return
        end
        t2 = t2 + dt
        local stab = _portalStability[colorKey] or 1
        if stab < 0.7 and t2 - lastBeat > period then
            lastBeat = t2
            local pitch = 0.8 + stab * 0.4
            AudioMgr.play(SFX_EXT.electricBuzz, {volume=0.25*(1-stab)*2, pitch=pitch})
        end
    end)
    _heartbeatConns[colorKey] = conn
end

-- ─── Proximity audio (enhanced version) ──────────────────────────────────────
local _ambientLoops = {}

local function manageAmbientLoop(colorKey, col)
    local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
    if not ex then
        local loop = _ambientLoops[colorKey]
        if loop then
            pcall(function() loop:Stop(); loop:Destroy() end)
            _ambientLoops[colorKey] = nil
        end
        return
    end
    if not _ambientLoops[colorKey] then
        local id = colorKey=="blue" and SFX_EXT.portalHum_blue or SFX_EXT.portalHum_orange
        local s  = Instance.new("Sound")
        s.SoundId      = id
        s.Volume       = 0
        s.Looped       = true
        s.PlaybackSpeed= colorKey=="blue" and 0.95 or 0.82
        if ex.humPart then
            s.Parent = ex.humPart
        else
            s.Parent = _SS
        end
        s:Play()
        _ambientLoops[colorKey] = s
    end
end

_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    manageAmbientLoop("blue",   CFG and CFG.blueColor   or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
    manageAmbientLoop("orange", CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))

    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end

    for ck, loop in pairs(_ambientLoops) do
        if not loop or not loop.Parent then _ambientLoops[ck]=nil; continue end
        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[ck]
        if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
            local dist = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
            local vol  = _clamp((35-dist)/35, 0, 1) * UCFG.ambientHumVol
            loop.Volume = _lerp(loop.Volume, vol, dt*3)
        else
            loop.Volume = _lerp(loop.Volume, 0, dt*4)
        end
    end
end)

print("[PortalGun v3] Extended audio system loaded — "..tostring(#(function()
    local t={} for k in pairs(SFX_EXT) do table.insert(t,k) end return t end()).." sound IDs registered")



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL SHADER SIMULATION  —  Simulates advanced rendering effects in Roblox
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── PortalShader: per-portal visual style presets ───────────────────────────
local PortalShader = {}
PortalShader.presets = {}

local function _defShader(name, fn)
    PortalShader.presets[name] = fn
end

-- ── Shader: "Neon Glow" — Maximum emission, hard neon colors ────────────────
_defShader("NeonGlow", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    local brightCol = Color3.new(math.min(1,col.R+0.3),math.min(1,col.G+0.3),math.min(1,col.B+0.3))
    for _,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
        rd.part.Material    = Enum.Material.Neon
        rd.part.Color       = brightCol
        rd.part.Transparency= 0.05
    end
    if ex.outerHalo then
        ex.outerHalo.Color       = brightCol
        ex.outerHalo.Transparency= 0.75
        ex.outerHalo.Material    = Enum.Material.Neon
    end
end)

-- ── Shader: "Void" — Dark, ominous portal with deep colors ──────────────────
_defShader("Void", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    local darkCol = Color3.new(col.R*0.2, col.G*0.2, col.B*0.2)
    for i,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
        rd.part.Color       = darkCol
        rd.part.Transparency= 0.3 + i*0.05
    end
    if ex.outerHalo then
        ex.outerHalo.Color       = darkCol
        ex.outerHalo.Transparency= 0.92
    end
    for _,od in ipairs(ex.orbits) do
        od.part.Color       = darkCol
        od.part.Transparency= 0.5
    end
end)

-- ── Shader: "Prismatic" — Rainbow color cycling ──────────────────────────────
local _prismConn = nil
_defShader("Prismatic", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    if _prismConn then _prismConn:Disconnect() end
    local t2=0
    _prismConn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not (ex and ex.folder and ex.folder.Parent) then
            _prismConn:Disconnect(); return
        end
        t2=t2+dt
        for i,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
            if rd.part.Parent then
                rd.part.Color=Color3.fromHSV(((t2*0.2+i*0.12))%1, 0.85, 1)
            end
        end
        if ex.outerHalo and ex.outerHalo.Parent then
            ex.outerHalo.Color=Color3.fromHSV((t2*0.15)%1, 0.7, 1)
        end
    end)
end)

-- ── Shader: "Holographic" — Semi-transparent with blue-white tones ───────────
_defShader("Holographic", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    local holoCol = Color3.fromRGB(150,220,255)
    for i,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
        rd.part.Material    = Enum.Material.ForceField
        rd.part.Color       = holoCol
        rd.part.Transparency= 0.4 + i*0.06
    end
    if ex.outerHalo then
        ex.outerHalo.Material    = Enum.Material.ForceField
        ex.outerHalo.Color       = holoCol
        ex.outerHalo.Transparency= 0.82
    end
end)

-- ── Shader: "Crystalline" — High-contrast sharp edges with SmoothPlastic ─────
_defShader("Crystalline", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    for i,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
        rd.part.Material    = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic
        rd.part.Color       = col
        rd.part.Transparency= 0.0 + i*0.1
    end
end)

-- ── Shader: "Plasma" — Flowing plasma look with particle enhancement ──────────
_defShader("Plasma", function(ex, col)
    if not (ex and ex.rings) then return end
    local plasmaCol=Color3.new(math.min(1,col.R+0.15),col.G,math.min(1,col.B+0.15))
    for i,rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
        rd.part.Material    = Enum.Material.Neon
        rd.part.Color       = plasmaCol
        rd.part.Transparency= 0.0 + (i-1)*0.04
    end
    -- Boost particle emitters
    for _,od in ipairs(ex.orbits) do
        local pe = od.part:FindFirstChildOfClass("ParticleEmitter")
        if pe then pe.Rate = pe.Rate * 2 end
    end
end)

-- ── Apply a shader to a portal ───────────────────────────────────────────────
function PortalShader.apply(colorKey, shaderName)
    local fn  = PortalShader.presets[shaderName]
    local ex  = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
    if not fn then warn("[PortalShader] Unknown: "..tostring(shaderName)); return end
    if not ex then return end
    local col = colorKey=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                                  or  (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
    pcall(function() fn(ex, col) end)
    _showNotif("🎛", "Shader: "..shaderName,
        "Applied to "..colorKey.." portal", Color3.fromRGB(20,40,80), 2)
end

function PortalShader.applyBoth(shaderName)
    PortalShader.apply("blue",   shaderName)
    PortalShader.apply("orange", shaderName)
end

function PortalShader.list()
    local names={}
    for k in pairs(PortalShader.presets) do table.insert(names,k) end
    table.sort(names)
    return names
end



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL COMBO SYSTEM  —  Tracks portal usage patterns and fires bonus VFX
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── Combo tracker ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local ComboSys = {}
ComboSys.streak        = 0
ComboSys.lastFireTime  = 0
ComboSys.comboWindow   = 4.0   -- seconds between fires to maintain combo
ComboSys.milestones    = {5, 10, 20, 50, 100}
ComboSys.milestoneDone = {}

-- ─── Combo VFX by level ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local comboEffects = {
    [5]   = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX2.portalAuraPulse(cf, col)
        _showNotif("🔥", "5× Combo!", "Nice shot!", Color3.fromRGB(60,30,0), 2)
    end,
    [10]  = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX2.electricCrown(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX2.portalEnergyNova(cf, col, pw)
        _showNotif("⚡", "10× Combo!", "Sizzling!", Color3.fromRGB(60,60,0), 2.5)
    end,
    [20]  = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX3_EXT.supernova(cf, col, pw, ph)
        _doFlash(col, 0.5, 0.4)
        _showNotif("💥", "20× Combo!", "Unstoppable!", Color3.fromRGB(80,20,0), 3)
    end,
    [50]  = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX3_EXT.supernova(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX2.interiorLightningStorm(cf, col, pw, ph, 25)
        VFX2.holographicRings(cf, col, pw)
        _doFlash(col, 0.7, 0.5)
        _doSpeedLines(col, 0.3)
        _showNotif("🌟", "50× Combo!!", "LEGENDARY!", Color3.fromRGB(80,60,0), 4)
    end,
    [100] = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        for i=1,3 do
            _delay(i*0.1, function()
                VFX3_EXT.supernova(cf, col, pw, ph)
            end)
        end
        VFX3_EXT.quantumEntanglement(cf, cf, col, col)
        _doChromaticAberration(0.5)
        _doSpeedLines(col, 0.4)
        _vignetteFlash(0.9, 0.8)
        _showNotif("👑", "100× COMBO!!!", "PORTAL MASTER", Color3.fromRGB(80,70,0), 5)
    end,
}

function ComboSys.onFire(colorKey)
    local now  = tick()
    local dt2  = now - ComboSys.lastFireTime

    if dt2 > ComboSys.comboWindow then
        ComboSys.streak = 0
        for m in pairs(ComboSys.milestoneDone) do ComboSys.milestoneDone[m]=false end
    end

    ComboSys.streak       = ComboSys.streak + 1
    ComboSys.lastFireTime = now

    -- Check milestones
    for _,m in ipairs(ComboSys.milestones) do
        if ComboSys.streak >= m and not ComboSys.milestoneDone[m] then
            ComboSys.milestoneDone[m] = true
            local fn = comboEffects[m]
            if fn then
                _spawn(function()
                    pcall(function()
                        local ex   = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
                        local col2 = colorKey=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor) or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor)
                            or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
                        if ex and ex.cf then
                            fn(ex.cf, col2, ex.pw or 4, ex.ph or 6)
                        end
                    end)
                end)
            end
        end
    end

    -- Display current streak (only when active combo)
    if ComboSys.streak >= 3 then
        pcall(function()
            if _gv3.arcLabel then
                _gv3.arcLabel.Text = "×"..ComboSys.streak
            end
        end)
    end
end

function ComboSys.getStreak() return ComboSys.streak end

-- ─── Hook into portal fire events ─────────────────────────────────────────────
-- (wired via the Heartbeat portal-state watcher)
local _prevFireCount = 0
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    pcall(function()
        if lastFire and lastFire ~= _prevFireCount then
            _prevFireCount = lastFire
            ComboSys.onFire(selColor or "blue")
        end
    end)
end)



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL PHYSICS SIMULATION  —  Visual-only momentum and gravity simulation
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

-- ─── Portal momentum predictor ───────────────────────────────────────────────
-- Visualizes the predicted exit trajectory as a faint dotted arc
local PortalPhysics = {}
PortalPhysics.previewParts = {}
PortalPhysics.enabled      = true

local function _clearPreviewPath()
    for _, p in ipairs(PortalPhysics.previewParts) do
        pcall(function() p:Destroy() end)
    end
    PortalPhysics.previewParts = {}
end

local function _drawPathArc(startPos, startVel, numPts, gravity)
    _clearPreviewPath()
    if not PortalPhysics.enabled then return end
    gravity = gravity or Vector3.new(0,-workspace.Gravity or -196.2,0)
    local dt2 = 0.06
    local pos  = startPos
    local vel  = startVel
    for i=1,numPts do
        vel = vel + gravity * dt2
        pos = pos + vel * dt2
        local p = _part({
            Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
            Color       = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255),
            Size        = Vector3.new(0.08,0.08,0.08),
            Transparency= 0.3 + (i/numPts)*0.65,
            CFrame      = CFrame.new(pos),
        })
        p.Parent = _WS
        table.insert(PortalPhysics.previewParts, p)
    end
end

-- ─── Momentum preservation helper (visual indicator) ─────────────────────────
local function _showMomentumArrow(exitCF, velocity)
    local arr = _part({
        Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
        Color       = Color3.fromRGB(0,220,100),
        Size        = Vector3.new(0.06, 0.06, velocity.Magnitude * 0.04),
        Transparency= 0.2,
        CFrame      = exitCF * CFrame.new(0,0,-velocity.Magnitude*0.02),
    })
    arr.Parent = _WS
    _tw(arr, 0.8, { Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01) })
    _gc(arr, 0.85)
end

-- ─── Portal gravity simulation — pull particles inward ───────────────────────
local _gravConnections = {}

local function _startGravPull(colorKey)
    if _gravConnections[colorKey] then
        _gravConnections[colorKey]:Disconnect()
    end
    local conn
    conn = _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt2)
        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
        if not (ex and ex.beamAnchor) then
            conn:Disconnect(); _gravConnections[colorKey]=nil; return
        end
        local portalPos = ex.beamAnchor.Position
        local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not hrp then return end
        local dist = (portalPos - hrp.Position).Magnitude
        -- Visual only: just spawn pull particles if close enough
        if dist < UCFG.gravityWellRadius and _rand() < 0.04 then
            local spawnPos = hrp.Position + Vector3.new(
                (_rand()-0.5)*8, (_rand()-0.5)*4, (_rand()-0.5)*8)
            local p = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = ex.col,
                Size        = Vector3.new(0.08,0.08,0.08),
                Transparency= 0.2,
                CFrame      = CFrame.new(spawnPos),
            })
            p.Parent = _WS
            _tw(p, 0.5+_rand()*0.3, {
                CFrame      = CFrame.new(portalPos),
                Transparency= 1,
                Size        = Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01),
            })
            _gc(p, 0.9)
        end
    end)
    _gravConnections[colorKey] = conn
end

-- Start gravity pull for each portal on open
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt2)
    for _, ck in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
        if _UPG.portalExtras[ck] and not _gravConnections[ck] then
            _startGravPull(ck)
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Portal surface geometry analyzer ─────────────────────────────────────────
-- Determines the surface type (wall/floor/ceiling) and reports it in status
local function _analyzeSurface(normal)
    local dot = normal:Dot(Vector3.new(0,1,0))
    if dot > 0.7 then
        return "Floor"
    elseif dot < -0.7 then
        return "Ceiling"
    else
        return "Wall"
    end
end

-- Update status cards with surface type info
_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if ex and ex.cf then
            local normal = ex.cf.LookVector
            local surfType = _analyzeSurface(normal)
            -- Update info label if available
            local infoKey = ck=="blue" and "blueInfoLbl" or "orangeInfoLbl"
            local lbl = _gv3[infoKey]
            if lbl then
                local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                local distStr = "—"
                if hrp and ex.beamAnchor then
                    distStr = tostring(math.floor((ex.beamAnchor.Position-hrp.Position).Magnitude)).."st"
                end
                lbl.Text = surfType.." · "..distStr
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ─── Public API ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
PortalPhysics.clearPath   = _clearPreviewPath
PortalPhysics.drawArc     = _drawPathArc
PortalPhysics.showArrow   = _showMomentumArrow
PortalPhysics.analyzeSurf = _analyzeSurface

--[[
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  PORTAL GUN v3 ULTRA — COMPLETE SYSTEM REFERENCE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  ARCHITECTURE OVERVIEW
  ─────────────────────
  The script is organized into layered modules that build on each other:

    LAYER 0 — Original Script (Portalgun4)
      The base portal gun with Mel's model, core portal placement logic,
      surface detection, teleportation, settings panel (Colors/Size/Advanced/VFX),
      basic VFX, arm animation, and module API.

    LAYER 1 — Upgrade Patch v3 (Part I)
      • Advanced Multi-Layer Portal Renderer (15 visual layers)
      • Screen-Space Effects Engine (chromatic, vignette, scanlines, color leak)
      • GUI Overhaul v3 (status bar, cooldown arc, minimap, crosshair)
      • VFX Expansion Pack (30+ new effects)
      • Audio System v2 (layered, positional, proximity-reactive)
      • Portal Interaction Physics

    LAYER 2 — Ultra Upgrade (Part II)
      • VFX3 namespace (additional 20 effects)
      • VFX3_EXT namespace (20 more high-detail effects)
      • Particle Preset Library (30 presets)
      • Portal Art Presets (20 color schemes + gallery GUI)
      • Animation State Machine v2
      • Environment Effects (skybox tint, ground projection)
      • Extended GUI (stability bars, quick color, timer display)
      • Extended Sound Library (35+ sound IDs, AudioMgr, layered events)
      • Portal Shader Simulation (6 shader presets)
      • Portal Combo System (streak tracking, milestone rewards)
      • Portal Physics Simulation (gravity pull, surface analysis)
      • Portal Render Helpers (10 low-level utilities)

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  MODULE REFERENCE
  ─────────────────
  All modules are accessible as globals after the script runs.

  VFX (original)  — Basic effects from base script
  VFX2            — Expanded effects (Part I)
  VFX3            — Additional effects (Part II)
  VFX3_EXT        — High-detail extended effects (Part II)

  PortalRender    — Low-level rendering primitives
  PortalArt       — Color scheme presets and gallery
  PortalShader    — Visual shader presets for portal rings
  PortalPhysics   — Gravity simulation and surface analysis
  ParticlePresets — 30 named particle emitter configurations
  AudioMgr        — Sound channel manager and layered audio
  AnimSM          — Animation state machine
  ComboSys        — Fire streak combo tracking
  UCFG            — Upgrade configuration table

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  UCFG CONFIGURATION TABLE
  ─────────────────────────
  All upgrade behavior is controlled through UCFG:

    Portal layer toggles:
      showOuterRings    (bool)  — Concentric ring renderer
      showOrbitSparks   (bool)  — Orbital spark nodes
      showEdgeTendrils  (bool)  — Animated edge tentacles
      showNeonGrid      (bool)  — Grid overlay on portal face
      showDepthSpiral   (bool)  — Depth spiral effect
      showCornerArcs    (bool)  — Corner lightning nodes
      showGravityWell   (bool)  — Gravity well particle emitter
      showCrossBeam     (bool)  — Cross-portal energy beam
      showBreathing     (bool)  — Portal breathing animation

    Screen-space effects:
      ssFX_chromatic    (bool)  — Chromatic aberration on teleport
      ssFX_vignette     (bool)  — Vignette overlay
      ssFX_scanlines    (bool)  — Scanline overlay
      ssFX_colorLeak    (bool)  — Portal color bleeds on screen edge
      ssFX_speedLines   (bool)  — Speed line burst on teleport
      ssFX_fovDistort   (bool)  — FOV changes near portals

    Audio settings:
      audioAmbient      (bool)  — Positional ambient hum
      audioPositional   (bool)  — 3D positional audio events
      audioProximity    (bool)  — Proximity volume scaling
      ambientHumVol     (num)   — Volume of ambient hum (0–1)
      ambientHumPitch   (num)   — Pitch of ambient hum

    Portal behavior:
      breatheAmplitude  (num)   — Breathing pulse strength
      breathePeriod     (num)   — Breathing cycle duration (seconds)
      heartbeatPeriod   (num)   — Heartbeat flash interval (seconds)
      gravityWellRadius (num)   — Pull effect radius in studs
      fovDistortRange   (num)   — Distance for FOV distortion
      fovDistortAmt     (num)   — Maximum FOV change in degrees

    Visual parameters:
      vignetteIntensity (num)   — Vignette darkness (0–1)
      chromaticShift    (num)   — Chromatic offset in pixels
      scanlineOpacity   (num)   — Scanline darkness (0–1)
      colorLeakOpacity  (num)   — Color leak intensity (0–1)
      speedLineOpacity  (num)   — Speed line opacity (0–1)
      orbitSparks       (num)   — Number of orbital spark nodes
      tendrilCount      (num)   — Number of edge tendrils
      gridRows/gridCols (num)   — Neon grid resolution

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS (complete list)
  ────────────────────────────────────
    LMB / Activate  — Fire blue portal
    RMB / Q         — Fire orange portal
    R               — Close all portals
    Z / X           — Switch selected portal color
    [ / ]           — Rotate portal −15° / +15°
    ; / '           — Tilt portal up/down
    \               — Reset rotation and tilt
    Tab             — Cycle portal color (blue ↔ orange)
    G               — Apply random art scheme
    H               — Toggle keybind overlay
    F1              — Toggle debug panel
    ⚙ button        — Settings panel (Colors/Size/Advanced/VFX/FX+)
    🎨 button        — Art gallery panel

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  PERFORMANCE NOTES
  ─────────────────
    • The extra layers use ~15 parts per portal, plus particle emitters.
    • On mid-range devices, disable showNeonGrid, showDepthSpiral, and
      showEdgeTendrils for best performance.
    • The cross-portal beam uses a Beam instance (1 per pair), not parts —
      no significant performance impact.
    • VFX effects are all transient (auto-cleaned via _gc) and use the
      Workspace directly — no model hierarchy overhead.
    • AudioMgr limits to 16 concurrent sound channels and auto-evicts oldest.
    • Screen-space effects use ImageLabels at ZIndex > 10 — very cheap.

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  KNOWN LIMITATIONS
  ──────────────────
    • SpecialMesh with torus MeshId requires "rbxassetid://3270017987" —
      this is a community mesh that may be unavailable in all places.
    • FOV distortion can conflict with other camera scripts. Disable
      ssFX_fovDistort if you experience camera jitter.
    • The Prismatic shader runs a RenderStepped connection — only one
      prismatic portal at a time to avoid duplicate connections.
    • Combo system tracks time between fires using tick() — server resets
      will break the streak timer.

  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  EXTENSION GUIDE
  ────────────────
    Adding a new VFX effect:
      1. Add a function to VFX3 or VFX3_EXT namespace
      2. Call it from the Heartbeat portal-open handler
      3. Optionally add a UCFG toggle

    Adding a new color scheme:
      1. Call _defArt("SchemeName", r,g,b, r,g,b, "description")
      2. It auto-appears in the Art Gallery panel

    Adding a new shader:
      1. Call _defShader("ShaderName", function(ex, col) ... end)
      2. Apply with PortalShader.apply("blue", "ShaderName")

    Adding a new particle preset:
      1. Call _preset("PresetName", { ... config ... })
      2. Use with applyPreset("PresetName", parent, color)

    Adding a new audio event:
      1. Add the SoundId to SFX_EXT table
      2. Create a function using AudioMgr.play or AudioMgr.playAt
      3. Call from the appropriate event handler

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
]]

-- ─── End of documentation block ──────────────────────────────────────────────
print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA] Documentation block loaded")
print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA] Full system reference available in source comments")

--  STARTUP & INTEGRATION  —  Final wiring and initialization
