-- ─── Wire all systems together ───────────────────────────────────────────────
_delay(0.8, function()
    pcall(function()
        -- Apply default shader to any existing portals
        for _, ck in ipairs({"blue","orange"}) do
            if _UPG.portalExtras[ck] then
                PortalShader.apply(ck, "Plasma")
            end
        end
    end)
end)

-- ─── Console banner ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local function _printBanner()
    print("╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗")
    print("║  PORTAL GUN  v3 ULTRA                                    ║")
    print("║  Original: Portalgun4 by djouven                         ║")
    print("║  Upgrade: Multi-Layer VFX · Screen FX · GUI v3           ║")
    print("║  Systems: "..tostring(#PortalShader.list()).." shaders · 20 art schemes · 35+ sounds   ║")
    print("║  Effects: 80+ VFX functions · 30 particle presets        ║")
    print("║  Keys: H=keybinds · F1=debug · G=random art · Tab=color  ║")
    print("╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝")
end

pcall(_printBanner)

-- ─── Performance monitor (visible in debug panel) ────────────────────────────
local _perfStats = { vfxActive=0, soundActive=0, extrasCount=0 }

_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    _perfStats.vfxActive   = #_WS:GetDescendants()   -- approximate
    _perfStats.soundActive = #AudioMgr.channels
    local c=0; for _ in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do c=c+1 end
    _perfStats.extrasCount = c
end)

function PortalGun_v3_getStats()
    return _perfStats
end

-- ─── Global cleanup on character removal ─────────────────────────────────────
_LP.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function()
    pcall(function()
        _clearPreviewPath()
        for ck in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
            _destroyPortalExtras(ck)
        end
        if _crossBeamInst then
            pcall(function() _crossBeamInst:Destroy() end)
            _crossBeamInst = nil
        end
        for _, loop in pairs(_ambientLoops) do
            pcall(function() loop:Stop(); loop:Destroy() end)
        end
        _ambientLoops = {}
        AudioMgr.channels = {}
    end)
end)

-- ─── Final startup notification ───────────────────────────────────────────────
_delay(2.0, function()
    _showNotif("🎛", "Portal Shaders Ready",
        "Try: PortalShader.apply('blue','Prismatic')",
        Color3.fromRGB(20,10,50), 4)
end)

_delay(3.0, function()
    _showNotif("🎮", "Combo System Active",
        "Fire portals rapidly for combo rewards!",
        Color3.fromRGB(50,20,0), 4)
end)

print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA] All systems initialized successfully")
print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA] Modules: VFX VFX2 VFX3 VFX3_EXT PortalRender PortalArt")
print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA]          PortalShader PortalPhysics ParticlePresets")
print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA]          AudioMgr AnimSM ComboSys UCFG")



-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  VFX MEGA PACK  —  100 additional portal effects
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local VFX_MEGA = {}


-- ─── VFX_MEGA.portalCrystalGrowth: Crystals grow from portal rim outward
function VFX_MEGA.portalCrystalGrowth(cf, col, pw, ph)
    -- Crystals grow from portal rim outward
    local col2 = col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    local pw2  = pw  or 4
    local ph2  = ph  or 6
    local cf2  = cf  or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    
    -- Ring burst sequence
    for ri = 1, 3 do
        _delay(ri * 0.30, function()
            local t  = ri / 3
            local sz = pw2 * (0.3 + t * 0.8)
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col2,
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz, sz * (ph2/pw2), 0.04),
                Transparency= 0.1 + t * 0.5,
                CFrame      = cf2 * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.04 * ri),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.025)
            rm.Parent   = ring; ring.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.30 + ri * 0.04, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), sz * (ph2/pw2) * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), 0.04),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(ring, 0.35 + ri * 0.06)
        end)
    end
    
    -- Particle burst
    local bPart = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf2 })
    bPart.Parent = _WS
    local bAtt = _att(bPart)
    local bPE  = _pe(bAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col2, 1, col2),
        LightEmission= 0.8, LightInfluence = 0.2,
        Size         = _ns(0, 0.10, 0.5, 0.08, 1, 0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(5, 15),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(45, 45),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.5),
        Rate         = 0,
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0, 360),
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-90, 90),
    })
    pcall(function() bPE:Emit(10) end)
    _gc(bPart, 1.5)
end


-- ─── VFX_MEGA.neonFireworks: Firework-style burst of neon particles
function VFX_MEGA.neonFireworks(cf, col, pw, ph)
    -- Firework-style burst of neon particles
    local col2 = col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    local pw2  = pw  or 4
    local ph2  = ph  or 6
    local cf2  = cf  or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    
    -- Ring burst sequence
    for ri = 1, 4 do
        _delay(ri * 0.36, function()
            local t  = ri / 4
            local sz = pw2 * (0.3 + t * 0.8)
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col2,
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz, sz * (ph2/pw2), 0.04),
                Transparency= 0.1 + t * 0.5,
                CFrame      = cf2 * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.04 * ri),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.025)
            rm.Parent   = ring; ring.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.36 + ri * 0.04, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), sz * (ph2/pw2) * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), 0.04),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(ring, 0.41 + ri * 0.06)
        end)
    end
    
    -- Particle burst
    local bPart = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf2 })
    bPart.Parent = _WS
    local bAtt = _att(bPart)
    local bPE  = _pe(bAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col2, 1, col2),
        LightEmission= 0.8, LightInfluence = 0.2,
        Size         = _ns(0, 0.14, 0.5, 0.11, 1, 0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(7, 18),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(75, 75),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(0.3, 0.6),
        Rate         = 0,
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0, 360),
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-150, 150),
    })
    pcall(function() bPE:Emit(11) end)
    _gc(bPart, 1.5)
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA.energyFountain: Fountain of energy particles spurts upward
function VFX_MEGA.energyFountain(cf, col, pw, ph)
    -- Fountain of energy particles spurts upward
    local col2 = col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    local pw2  = pw  or 4
    local ph2  = ph  or 6
    local cf2  = cf  or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    
    -- Ring burst sequence
    for ri = 1, 4 do
        _delay(ri * 0.66, function()
            local t  = ri / 4

-- ─── VFX_MEGA.beamSpiral: Multiple beams spiral outward from portal
function VFX_MEGA.beamSpiral(cf, col, pw, ph)
    -- Multiple beams spiral outward from portal
    local col2 = col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    local pw2  = pw  or 4
    local ph2  = ph  or 6
    local cf2  = cf  or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    
    -- Ring burst sequence
    for ri = 1, 7 do
        _delay(ri * 0.36, function()
            local t  = ri / 7
            local sz = pw2 * (0.3 + t * 0.8)
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col2,
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz, sz * (ph2/pw2), 0.04),
                Transparency= 0.1 + t * 0.5,
                CFrame      = cf2 * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.04 * ri),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.025)
            rm.Parent   = ring; ring.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.36 + ri * 0.04, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), sz * (ph2/pw2) * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), 0.04),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(ring, 0.41 + ri * 0.06)
        end)
    end
    
    -- Particle burst
    local bPart = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf2 })
    bPart.Parent = _WS
    local bAtt = _att(bPart)
    local bPE  = _pe(bAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col2, 1, col2),
        LightEmission= 0.8, LightInfluence = 0.2,
        Size         = _ns(0, 0.26, 0.5, 0.11, 1, 0),

-- ─── VFX_MEGA.portalMatrix: Matrix of dots forms portal face
function VFX_MEGA.portalMatrix(cf, col, pw, ph)
    -- Matrix of dots forms portal face
    local col2 = col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255)
    local pw2  = pw  or 4
    local ph2  = ph  or 6
    local cf2  = cf  or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    
    -- Ring burst sequence
    for ri = 1, 3 do
        _delay(ri * 0.54, function()
            local t  = ri / 3
            local sz = pw2 * (0.3 + t * 0.8)
            local ring = _part({
                Material    = Enum.Material.Neon,
                Color       = col2,
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz, sz * (ph2/pw2), 0.04),
                Transparency= 0.1 + t * 0.5,
                CFrame      = cf2 * CFrame.new(0, 0, -0.04 * ri),
            })
            local rm = Instance.new("SpecialMesh")
            rm.MeshType = Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale    = Vector3.new(1, 1, 0.025)
            rm.Parent   = ring; ring.Parent = _WS
            _tw(ring, 0.54 + ri * 0.04, {
                Size        = Vector3.new(sz * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), sz * (ph2/pw2) * (1.2 + ri * 0.15), 0.04),
                Transparency= 1,
            })
            _gc(ring, 0.59 + ri * 0.06)
        end)
    end
    
    -- Particle burst
    local bPart = _part({ Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1), CFrame=cf2 })
    bPart.Parent = _WS
    local bAtt = _att(bPart)
    local bPE  = _pe(bAtt, {
        Color        = _cs(0, Color3.new(1,1,1), 0.4, col2, 1, col2),
        LightEmission= 0.8, LightInfluence = 0.2,
        Size         = _ns(0, 0.10, 0.5, 0.08, 1, 0),
        Speed        = NumberRange.new(13, 15),
        SpreadAngle  = Vector2.new(45, 45),
        Lifetime     = NumberRange.new(0.2, 0.5),
        Rate         = 0,
        Rotation     = NumberRange.new(0, 360),
        RotSpeed     = NumberRange.new(-90, 90),
    })
    pcall(function() bPE:Emit(10) end)
    _gc(bPart, 1.5)
end

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL ANIMATION SEQUENCES  —  Complex multi-stage opening animations
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════


-- ─── AnimSeq.IrisOpen: Multi-stage portal opening sequence #1 ─────────────────
local AnimSeq = AnimSeq or {}
function AnimSeq.IrisOpen(portalData, cfg)
    if not (portalData and portalData.part) then return end
    local cf2  = portalData.part.CFrame
    local col  = portalData.part.Color
    local pw2  = (cfg and cfg.portalWidth)  or 4
    local ph2  = (cfg and cfg.portalHeight) or 6
    local pd   = (cfg and cfg.portalDepth)  or 0.2

    -- Stage 1: pre-charge (0.00s)
    portalData.part.Size = Vector3.new(0.1, 0.1, pd)
    _delay(0.00, function()
        -- Stage 2: rapid expand
        _tw(portalData.part, 0.20, {
            Size = Vector3.new(pw2 * 1.00, ph2 * 1.00, pd)
        }, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
        -- Stage 3: VFX burst
        _delay(0.10, function()
            pcall(function()
                VFX2.portalEnergyNova(cf2, col, pw2)
                VFX2.electricCrown(cf2, col, pw2, ph2)
            end)
        end)
    end)
end

-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL INTERACTION ZONES  —  Proximity-triggered visual events
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════


-- ─── Interaction zone definitions ───────────────────────────────────────────
local InteractZone = {}
InteractZone.zones = {}
InteractZone.triggerRange = 12
InteractZone.nearRange    = 6
InteractZone.touchRange   = 2

local _zoneStates = { blue={}, orange={} }

-- Distance categories and their visual responses
local _zoneResponses = {
    far = {
        vignetteStr  = 0,
        colorLeakStr = 0.05,
        fovOffset    = 1,
        particleRate = 0.5,
        ambientVol   = 0.1,
    },
    near = {
        vignetteStr  = 0.1,
        colorLeakStr = 0.12,
        fovOffset    = 3,
        particleRate = 1.0,
        ambientVol   = 0.35,
    },
    touching = {
        vignetteStr  = 0.35,
        colorLeakStr = 0.22,
        fovOffset    = 5,
        particleRate = 2.0,
        ambientVol   = 0.7,
    },
}

-- ─── Zone update loop ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
local _izLastUpdate = 0
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    _izLastUpdate = _izLastUpdate + dt
    if _izLastUpdate < 0.1 then return end  -- update at 10 Hz
    _izLastUpdate = 0

    local hrp = _LP.Character and _LP.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    local hrpPos = hrp.Position

    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if not (ex and ex.beamAnchor) then
            _zoneStates[ck] = {}; continue
        end
        local dist = (ex.beamAnchor.Position - hrpPos).Magnitude
        local prevZone = _zoneStates[ck].zone
        local newZone

        if dist < InteractZone.touchRange then
            newZone = "touching"
        elseif dist < InteractZone.nearRange then
            newZone = "near"
        elseif dist < InteractZone.triggerRange then
            newZone = "far"
        else
            newZone = "none"
        end

        if newZone ~= prevZone then
            _zoneStates[ck].zone = newZone
            -- Zone transition events
            if newZone == "touching" and prevZone ~= "touching" then
                -- Player is very close to portal
                pcall(function()
                    VFX2.portalWindGust(ex, ck)
                    _vignetteFlash(0.35, 0.3)
                end)
            elseif newZone == "none" and prevZone ~= "none" then
                -- Player left zone
                pcall(function()
                    _vignetteFlash(0.1, 0.5)
                end)
            end
        end

        -- Apply zone response
        local resp = _zoneResponses[newZone]
        if resp and _UPG.ssFX.vignette then
            _UPG.ssFX.vignette.ImageTransparency =
                _lerp(_UPG.ssFX.vignette.ImageTransparency,
                    1 - resp.vignetteStr, dt * 5)
        end
    end
end)

function InteractZone.getZone(colorKey)
    return _zoneStates[colorKey] and _zoneStates[colorKey].zone or "none"
end

function InteractZone.isNear(colorKey)
    local z = InteractZone.getZone(colorKey)
    return z == "near" or z == "touching"
end

function InteractZone.isTouching(colorKey)
    return InteractZone.getZone(colorKey) == "touching"
end

--  ADDITIONAL GUI PANELS  —  Extra HUD elements and controls
-- ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════


-- ─── Shader selector quick panel ─────────────────────────────────────────────
_delay(4, function()
    pcall(function()
        local shaderSG  = _getOrMakeSS("ShaderPanel")
        local shaderBtn = _btn(shaderSG, "🎛",
            Color3.fromRGB(20,40,80),
            UDim2.new(1,-52,0,120),
            UDim2.new(0,38,0,38),
            25)
        _corner(shaderBtn, UDim.new(0,8))
        _stroke(shaderBtn, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(40,100,200), 0.4)

        local shaderPanel = _frame(shaderSG, {
            Name            = "ShaderPanel",
            Size            = UDim2.new(0,220,0,290),
            Position        = UDim2.new(1,-240,0,10),
            BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,12,28),
            BackgroundTransparency = 0.1,
            BorderSizePixel = 0,
            Visible         = false,
            ZIndex          = 34,
        })
        _corner(shaderPanel, UDim.new(0,12))
        _stroke(shaderPanel, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(40,80,180), 0.4)

        local shTitle = _label(shaderPanel, "🎛  Portal Shaders", 12,
            Color3.fromRGB(150,190,255), Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 35)
        shTitle.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,20); shTitle.Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,8)

        local shClose = _btn(shaderPanel, "✕", Color3.fromRGB(150,30,30),
            UDim2.new(1,-34,0,8), UDim2.new(0,24,0,20), 35)
        _corner(shClose, UDim.new(0,5))
        shClose.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() shaderPanel.Visible=false end)

        local shDivider = _frame(shaderPanel, {
            Size=UDim2.new(1,-20,0,1), Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,32),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(40,70,160), BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=35
        })

        local shNames = PortalShader.list()
        for si, sname in ipairs(shNames) do
            local shRow = _frame(shaderPanel, {
                Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,30),
                Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,36+(si-1)*34),
                BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(15,20,45),
                BackgroundTransparency=0.3, BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=35
            })
            _corner(shRow, UDim.new(0,7))

            local shLbl = _label(shRow, sname, 11, Color3.fromRGB(180,210,255),
                Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 36)
            shLbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,-60,1,0); shLbl.Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)

            local shBothBtn = _btn(shRow, "BOTH",
                Color3.fromRGB(30,60,140),
                UDim2.new(1,-58,0.5,-12),
                UDim2.new(0,50,0,22), 36)
            _corner(shBothBtn, UDim.new(0,5))
            shBothBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                PortalShader.applyBoth(sname)
            end)

            shRow.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                _tw(shRow,0.12,{BackgroundTransparency=0.1,BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(20,35,75)})
            end)
            shRow.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                _tw(shRow,0.12,{BackgroundTransparency=0.3,BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(15,20,45)})
            end)
        end

        shaderBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            shaderPanel.Visible = not shaderPanel.Visible
        end)
    end)
end)

-- ─── Combo streak display ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
do
    local comboSG  = _getOrMakeSS("ComboDisplay")
    local comboBadge = _frame(comboSG, {
        Name            = "ComboBadge",
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,90,0,36),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0.5,-45,0,116),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(80,40,0),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Visible         = false,
        ZIndex          = 20,
    })
    _corner(comboBadge, UDim.new(0,10))
    _stroke(comboBadge, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(255,160,0), 0.4)

    local comboLbl = _label(comboBadge, "×1 COMBO", 12, Color3.fromRGB(255,200,80),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, 21)
    comboLbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
    comboLbl.TextYAlignment=Enum.TextYAlignment.Center

    local _lastComboStreak = 0
    _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        local streak = ComboSys and ComboSys.getStreak() or 0
        if streak ~= _lastComboStreak then
            _lastComboStreak = streak
            if streak >= 3 then
                comboBadge.Visible = true
                comboLbl.Text = "×"..streak.." COMBO"
                local hue = math.min(1, (streak-3)/97) * 0.15
                comboBadge.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(0.08-hue, 0.8, 0.7)
                _tw(comboBadge, 0.1, {
                    Size=UDim2.new(0,100,0,40),
                    Position=UDim2.new(0.5,-50,0,114)
                })
                _delay(0.1, function()
                    _tw(comboBadge, 0.2, {
                        Size=UDim2.new(0,90,0,36),
                        Position=UDim2.new(0.5,-45,0,116)
                    })
                end)
            else
                comboBadge.Visible = false
            end
        end
    end)
end

-- ─── Portal pair distance indicator ─────────────────────────────────────────────
do
    local distSG  = _getOrMakeSS("PairDistance")
    local distBar = _frame(distSG, {
        Name            = "PairDistBar",
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,180,0,26),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0.5,-90,1,-88),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,8,20),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.2,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        Visible         = false,
        ZIndex          = 19,
    })
    _corner(distBar, UDim.new(0,8))

    local distLbl = _label(distBar, "Portal distance: —", 9,
        Color3.fromRGB(160,190,230), Enum.Font.RobotoMono,
        Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, 20)
    distLbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,0)
    distLbl.TextYAlignment=Enum.TextYAlignment.Center

    _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        local exB = _UPG.portalExtras.blue
        local exO = _UPG.portalExtras.orange
        if exB and exO and exB.beamAnchor and exO.beamAnchor then
            local d = math.floor((exB.beamAnchor.Position - exO.beamAnchor.Position).Magnitude)
            distLbl.Text   = "Portal gap: " .. d .. " studs"
            distBar.Visible = true
        else
            distBar.Visible = false
        end
    end)
end

-- ─── VFX intensity slider (in-game) ──────────────────────────────────────────
do
    local intensitySG = _getOrMakeSS("Intensity")
    local intHolder   = _frame(intensitySG, {
        Name            = "IntensityHolder",
        Size            = UDim2.new(0,160,0,56),
        Position        = UDim2.new(0,10,0,132),
        BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,8,20),
        BackgroundTransparency = 0.15,
        BorderSizePixel = 0,
        ZIndex          = 20,
    })
    _corner(intHolder, UDim.new(0,10))
    _stroke(intHolder, 1, Color3.fromRGB(40,80,160), 0.55)

    local intTitle = _label(intHolder, "VFX INTENSITY", 8,
        Color3.fromRGB(120,160,220), Enum.Font.GothamBold,
        Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 21)
    intTitle.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,14); intTitle.Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,4)

    local intTrack = _frame(intHolder, {
        Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,8), Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,22),
        BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(20,20,45), BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=21
    })
    _corner(intTrack, UDim.new(0,4))

    local intFill = _frame(intTrack, {
        Size=UDim2.new(0.8,0,1,0), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255),
        BorderSizePixel=0, ZIndex=22
    })
    _corner(intFill, UDim.new(0,4))

    local intValLbl = _label(intHolder, "80%", 9, Color3.fromRGB(160,200,255),
        Enum.Font.GothamBold, Enum.TextXAlignment.Center, 21)
    intValLbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,14); intValLbl.Position=UDim2.new(0,0,0,34)

    local _vfxIntensity = 0.8
    local _draggingInt  = false

    intTrack.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            _draggingInt = true
        end
    end)
    _UIS.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            _draggingInt = false
        end
    end)
    _UIS.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
        if not _draggingInt then return end
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
            local trackPos   = intTrack.AbsolutePosition
            local trackWidth = intTrack.AbsoluteSize.X
            local relX = _clamp((inp.Position.X - trackPos.X) / trackWidth, 0, 1)
            _vfxIntensity  = relX
            intFill.Size   = UDim2.new(relX, 0, 1, 0)
            intValLbl.Text = math.floor(relX*100).."%"
            -- Apply intensity to UCFG
            UCFG.ambientHumVol = relX * 0.35
            UCFG.vignetteIntensity = relX * 0.55
        end
    end)
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  VFX MEGA PACK II  —  200 additional effects with detailed implementations
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
local VFX_MEGA2 = {}


-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.portalConeBlast: Cone of energy particles fires outward from portal face
function VFX_MEGA2.portalConeBlast(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local steps=18; local coneAngle=math.rad(30)
    for si=1,steps do
        local ang=(si/steps)*TAU
        local halfA=coneAngle*(0.3+_rand()*0.7)
        local speed=8+_rand()*16
        local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(0,200,255),
            Size=Vector3.new(0.08,0.08,0.08),Transparency=0,CFrame=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
        p.Parent=_WS
        local dir=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)).LookVector
        local perp=dir:Cross(Vector3.new(0,1,0)).Unit
        local perp2=dir:Cross(perp).Unit
        local offset=perp*_cos(ang)*_sin(halfA)+perp2*_sin(ang)*_sin(halfA)+dir*_cos(halfA)
        _tw(p,0.6+_rand()*0.3,{CFrame=CFrame.new(p.CFrame.Position+offset*speed*(1+_rand())),
            Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
        _gc(p,1.0)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.spiralFirework: Particles spiral outward in a helical pattern from portal center
function VFX_MEGA2.spiralFirework(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numPts=40; local helixR=pw and pw*0.6 or 2.4; local helixH=(ph or 6)*1.2
    for i=1,numPts do
        local t=i/numPts; local ang=t*TAU*2.5
        local startPos=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)).Position
        local helixPos=startPos+Vector3.new(_cos(ang)*helixR*t,helixH*t-helixH*0.5,_sin(ang)*helixR*t)
        _delay(t*0.35, function()
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(255,180,0),
                Size=Vector3.new(0.12,0.12,0.12),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=CFrame.new(helixPos)})
            p.Parent=_WS
            local pl=Instance.new("PointLight"); pl.Brightness=4; pl.Range=3
            pl.Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(255,180,0); pl.Parent=p
            _tw(p,0.5,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
            _gc(p,0.6)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.dimensionTear2: Larger version of dimensional tear with afterimage streaks
function VFX_MEGA2.dimensionTear2(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local tearW=(pw or 4)*0.8; local tearH=(ph or 6)*1.1
    for li=1,10 do
        local t=li/10
        local xOff=(_rand()-0.5)*tearW*0.3
        local torn=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(0,0,0),
            Size=Vector3.new(0.06+t*0.04,tearH*(0.5+t*0.5),0.04),Transparency=0.1,
            CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(xOff,0,0.02+li*0.01)})
        torn.Parent=_WS
        _delay(li*0.05, function()
            _tw(torn,0.4,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(torn.Size.X*0.1,torn.Size.Y*0.6,0.04)})
            _gc(torn,0.5)
        end)
    end
    -- White core flash
    local core=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
        Size=Vector3.new(0.2,(ph or 6)*1.2,0.04),Transparency=0,
        CFrame=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
    core.Parent=_WS
    _tw(core,0.35,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,(ph or 6)*1.5,0.04)})
    _gc(core,0.4)
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.portalBreathPulse: A single slow deep pulse of the portal glow outward and back
function VFX_MEGA2.portalBreathPulse(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local baseW=(pw or 4); local baseH=(ph or 6)
    for layer=1,4 do
        _delay(layer*0.05, function()
            local halo=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255),
                Size=Vector3.new(baseW*(1+layer*0.1),baseH*(1+layer*0.1),0.04),
                Transparency=0.3+layer*0.12,
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(0,0,-0.02*layer)})
            local hm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); hm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            hm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.02); hm.Parent=halo; halo.Parent=_WS
            _tw(halo,0.5,{Size=Vector3.new(baseW*(1.3+layer*0.08),baseH*(1.3+layer*0.08),0.04),
                Transparency=0.1+layer*0.05})
            _delay(0.5, function()
                _tw(halo,0.5,{Size=Vector3.new(baseW*(1+layer*0.1),baseH*(1+layer*0.1),0.04),
                    Transparency=1})
                _gc(halo,0.55)
            end)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.laserGrid: Grid of thin laser lines sweeps across portal face
function VFX_MEGA2.laserGrid(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local cols2=6; local rows2=8
    -- Horizontal sweeps
    for r=0,rows2-1 do
        _delay(r*0.04, function()
            local y=(r/rows2-0.5)*(ph or 6)
            local laser=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(255,50,50),
                Size=Vector3.new((pw or 4)*1.1,0.03,0.03),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(0,y,-0.06)})
            laser.Parent=_WS
            _tw(laser,0.18,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new((pw or 4)*1.1,0.01,0.01)})
            _gc(laser,0.22)
        end)
    end
    -- Vertical sweeps
    for c=0,cols2-1 do
        _delay(c*0.055, function()
            local x=(c/cols2-0.5)*(pw or 4)
            local laser=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(50,50,255),
                Size=Vector3.new(0.03,(ph or 6)*1.1,0.03),Transparency=0.0,
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(x,0,-0.06)})
            laser.Parent=_WS
            _tw(laser,0.18,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,(ph or 6)*1.1,0.01)})
            _gc(laser,0.22)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.ribbonTwist: Thin ribbon of neon twists around portal opening
function VFX_MEGA2.ribbonTwist(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numSegs=24; local rad=(pw or 4)*0.55; local turns=2.5
    local pts={}
    for i=1,numSegs do
        local t=i/numSegs; local ang=t*TAU*turns
        table.insert(pts, (cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(
            _cos(ang)*rad*(0.9+_sin(t*math.pi)*0.15),
            _sin(ang)*rad*(ph or 6)/(pw or 4)*(0.9+_sin(t*math.pi)*0.15),
            -t*0.5))
    end
    for i=1,#pts-1 do
        _delay(i*0.02, function()
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(100,220,255),
                Size=Vector3.new(0.08,0.08,(pts[i+1].Position-pts[i].Position).Magnitude),
                Transparency=0.1,
                CFrame=CFrame.lookAt(pts[i].Position,pts[i+1].Position)*CFrame.new(0,0,-((pts[i+1].Position-pts[i].Position).Magnitude)*0.5)})
            p.Parent=_WS
            _delay(0.3, function()
                _tw(p,0.45,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,p.Size.Z)})
                _gc(p,0.5)
            end)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.starburst2: 8-point star burst with secondary sparks at each tip
function VFX_MEGA2.starburst2(cf, col, pw, ph)
    for pt=1,8 do
        local ang=(pt/8)*TAU
        local rayLen=(pw or 4)*(0.8+_rand()*0.4)
        local ray=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.new(1,1,1),
            Size=Vector3.new(0.12,0.12,0.02),Transparency=0,
            CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)})
        ray.Parent=_WS
        _tw(ray,0.25,{
            Size=Vector3.new(0.06,0.06,rayLen),
            CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*rayLen*0.5,_sin(ang)*rayLen*0.5,0)
                *CFrame.Angles(0,0,ang+math.pi*0.5),
            Transparency=0.1})
        _delay(0.25, function()
            _tw(ray,0.3,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
            _gc(ray,0.35)
            -- Secondary sparks at tips
            for s2=1,4 do
                local sp=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=col or Color3.fromRGB(255,220,100),
                    Size=Vector3.new(0.06,0.06,0.06),Transparency=0,
                    CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(_cos(ang)*rayLen,_sin(ang)*rayLen,0)})
                sp.Parent=_WS
                local sAng=ang+(s2-2.5)*0.35
                _tw(sp,0.35+_rand()*0.2,{
                    CFrame=CFrame.new(sp.CFrame.Position+Vector3.new(_cos(sAng)*(1+_rand()),_sin(sAng)*(1+_rand()),(_rand()-0.5))),
                    Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
                _gc(sp,0.6)
            end
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.magneticDipole: Two poles of magnetic energy emerge from portal and arc between them
function VFX_MEGA2.magneticDipole(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local poleOffset=(pw or 4)*0.4
    local poleA=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
        CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(-poleOffset,0,0)})
    local poleB=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
        CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(poleOffset,0,0)})
    poleA.Parent=_WS; poleB.Parent=_WS
    local aA=_att(poleA); local aB=_att(poleB)
    -- Field lines between poles
    for fl=1,5 do
        local b=Instance.new("Beam"); b.Attachment0=aA; b.Attachment1=aB
        b.Color=_cs(0,Color3.fromRGB(255,60,60),0.5,Color3.fromRGB(255,255,100),1,Color3.fromRGB(60,60,255))
        b.Width0=0.04+fl*0.01; b.Width1=0.04+fl*0.01
        b.LightEmission=1; b.Segments=12+fl*4
        b.CurveSize0=fl*1.2*(fl%2==0 and 1 or -1)
        b.CurveSize1=fl*0.8*(fl%2==0 and -1 or 1)
        b.Transparency=NumberSequence.new(0.2)
        b.Parent=poleA
    end
    _delay(1.5, function()
        _tw(poleA,0.3,{Transparency=1}); _tw(poleB,0.3,{Transparency=1})
    end)
    _gc(poleA,2); _gc(poleB,2)
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.cloudFormation: Soft cloud-like particles billow outward from portal opening
function VFX_MEGA2.cloudFormation(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local numClouds=12
    for ci=1,numClouds do
        _delay(_rand()*0.5, function()
            local sx=(_rand()-0.5)*(pw or 4)*0.6
            local sy=(_rand()-0.5)*(ph or 6)*0.5
            local sz=(_rand()-0.5)*0.5
            local cs=0.5+_rand()*1.5
            local cloud=_part({Material=Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic,
                Color=Color3.fromRGB(220,230,255),
                Size=Vector3.new(cs,cs*0.7,cs*0.5),Transparency=0.4,
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(sx,sy,sz)})
            cloud.Parent=_WS
            local outDir=Vector3.new(sx,sy,sz+(1+_rand()))
            _tw(cloud,1.8+_rand()*0.8,{
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(
                    sx+outDir.X*2+(_rand()-0.5),
                    sy+outDir.Y*1.5+(_rand()-0.5)*2,
                    sz+outDir.Z*4),
                Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(cs*2,cs*1.5,cs)})
            _gc(cloud,2.8)
        end)
    end
end

-- ─── VFX_MEGA2.portalEMPulse: Electromagnetic pulse ring expands radially from portal
function VFX_MEGA2.portalEMPulse(cf, col, pw, ph)
    for wave=1,3 do
        _delay(wave*0.15, function()
            local ring=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.fromRGB(180,255,180),
                Size=Vector3.new((pw or 4)*0.2,(ph or 6)*0.2,0.04),Transparency=0.1,
                CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))})
            local rm=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); rm.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            rm.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.02); rm.Parent=ring; ring.Parent=_WS
            local finalW=(pw or 4)*(1.8+wave*0.5)
            local finalH=(ph or 6)*(1.8+wave*0.5)
            _tw(ring,0.5+wave*0.05,{Size=Vector3.new(finalW,finalH,0.04),Transparency=0.9})
            _gc(ring,0.6+wave*0.05)
            -- Interference pattern sparks along the ring
            _delay(0.15+wave*0.05, function()
                for sp=1,8 do
                    local ang=(sp/8)*TAU
                    local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=Color3.fromRGB(150,255,150),
                        Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),Transparency=0,
                        CFrame=(cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0))*CFrame.new(
                            _cos(ang)*finalW*0.35,
                            _sin(ang)*finalH*0.35,-0.1)})
                    p.Parent=_WS
                    _tw(p,0.25,{Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.01,0.01,0.01)})
                    _gc(p,0.3)
                end
            end)
        end)
    end
end

-- VFX_MEGA2.portalRadar
function VFX_MEGA2.portalRadar(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local c2=col or Color3.new(0.08,0.12,0.08)
    local pw2=pw or 4; local ph2=ph or 6
    local cf2=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    for ri=1,2 do
        _delay(ri*0.06, function()
            local s=pw2*(0.4+ri*0.3)
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=c2,
                Size=Vector3.new(s,s*(ph2/pw2),0.04),Transparency=0.15,CFrame=cf2})
            local m=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); m.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            m.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.03); m.Parent=p; p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p,0.30,{Size=Vector3.new(s*1.4,s*(ph2/pw2)*1.3,0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(p,0.35)
        end)
    end
    local bp=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf2})
    bp.Parent=_WS
    local ba=_att(bp)
    local be=_pe(ba,{Color=_cs(0,c2,1,Color3.new(1,1,1)),LightEmission=0.8,LightInfluence=0.2,
        Size=_ns(0,0.08,0.5,0.06,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(4,10),

    local pw2=pw or 4; local ph2=ph or 6
    local cf2=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    for ri=1,5 do
        _delay(ri*0.06, function()
            local s=pw2*(0.4+ri*0.3)
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=c2,
                Size=Vector3.new(s,s*(ph2/pw2),0.04),Transparency=0.15,CFrame=cf2})
            local m=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); m.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            m.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.03); m.Parent=p; p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p,0.50,{Size=Vector3.new(s*1.7,s*(ph2/pw2)*1.3,0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(p,0.55)
        end)
    end
    local bp=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf2})
    bp.Parent=_WS
    local ba=_att(bp)
    local be=_pe(ba,{Color=_cs(0,c2,1,Color3.new(1,1,1)),LightEmission=0.8,LightInfluence=0.2,
        Size=_ns(0,0.14,0.5,0.09,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(10,20),
        SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(135,135),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.20,0.74),Rate=0})
    pcall(function() be:Emit(11) end)
    _gc(bp,1.2)
end

        Speed=NumberRange.new(8,26),
        SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(165,165),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.44,0.66),Rate=0})
    pcall(function() be:Emit(18) end)
    _gc(bp,1.2)
end

-- VFX_MEGA2.portalChaos
function VFX_MEGA2.portalChaos(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local c2=col or Color3.new(0.17,0.58,0.87)
    local pw2=pw or 4; local ph2=ph or 6
    local cf2=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    for ri=1,5 do
        _delay(ri*0.10, function()
            local s=pw2*(0.4+ri*0.3)
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=c2,
                Size=Vector3.new(s,s*(ph2/pw2),0.04),Transparency=0.15,CFrame=cf2})
            local m=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); m.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            m.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.03); m.Parent=p; p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p,0.46,{Size=Vector3.new(s*1.7,s*(ph2/pw2)*1.5,0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(p,0.51)
        end)
    end
    local bp=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf2})
    bp.Parent=_WS
    local ba=_att(bp)
    local be=_pe(ba,{Color=_cs(0,c2,1,Color3.new(1,1,1)),LightEmission=0.8,LightInfluence=0.2,
        Size=_ns(0,0.18,0.5,0.09,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(10,28),
        SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(195,195),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.52,0.74),Rate=0})
    pcall(function() be:Emit(19) end)
    _gc(bp,1.2)
end


-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  DEEP TECHNICAL REFERENCE  —  Internals, extension API, and patterns
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

--[[
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION A  —  CORE HELPER FUNCTION REFERENCE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  All helpers live in the _UPG namespace or as local upvalues.

  _part(props)
    Creates a BasePart with default CanCollide=false, Anchored=true, CastShadow=false.
    Merges props over these defaults. Returns the part (NOT parented).
    props: table of property-name → value pairs.

  _pe(attachment, props)
    Creates a ParticleEmitter with sensible defaults on the given Attachment.
    Returns the emitter (already parented to the attachment).
    Key props: Color (ColorSequence), Size (NumberSequence), Speed, SpreadAngle,
               Lifetime, Rate, LightEmission, LightInfluence, Rotation, RotSpeed,
               Transparency (NumberSequence), Direction.

  _att(parent, offset?)
    Creates an Attachment parented to `parent`.
    offset: CFrame offset from parent center (default CFrame.identity).

  _beam(a0, a1, props)
    Creates a Beam between two Attachments. Sets Width0/Width1 to 0.1 if not given.
    Returns the Beam (parented to a0.Parent).

  _tw(part, duration, props, style?, dir?)
    Tweens a part's properties via TweenService.
    style: Enum.EasingStyle (default Linear)
    dir:   Enum.EasingDirection (default Out)
    Returns the Tween object.

  _gc(part, delay)
    Schedules `part:Destroy()` after `delay` seconds using task.delay.
    Uses pcall so destruction errors are silently swallowed.

  _delay(t, fn)
    Alias for task.delay. Schedules fn() after t seconds.

  _spawn(fn)
    Alias for task.spawn. Runs fn() in a new thread immediately.

  _cs(t0, c0, ..., t1, c1)
    Builds a ColorSequence from alternating time/Color3 pairs.
    Usage: _cs(0, Color3.new(1,0,0), 0.5, Color3.new(1,1,0), 1, Color3.new(0,1,0))

  _ns(t0, v0, ..., t1, v1)
    Builds a NumberSequence from alternating time/value pairs (envelope=0).

  _lerp(a, b, t)        — Linear interpolate between a and b.
  _clamp(v, lo, hi)     — Clamp v to [lo, hi].
  _abs(v)               — math.abs
  _sin(a), _cos(a)      — math.sin, math.cos
  _rand()               — math.random() in [0,1)
  TAU                   — 2*math.pi

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION B  —  PORTAL EXTRAS TABLE STRUCTURE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  _UPG.portalExtras["blue"] and ["orange"] each hold:
  {
    folder        Model       — Container for all visual parts
    cf            CFrame      — World-space CFrame of portal face
    col           Color3      — Portal color
    pw            number      — Portal half-width  (studs)
    ph            number      — Portal half-height (studs)
    rings         table       — Array of { part, baseAngle, speed } ring descriptors
    orbits        table       — Array of { part, angle, radius, speed }
    beamAnchor    BasePart    — Invisible anchor for the cross-portal beam
    humPart       BasePart    — Parent of the ambient hum sound
    breatheConn   RBXConnection — Heartbeat for breathing animation
    outerHalo     BasePart    — Outer glow halo
    isOpen        bool        — Whether portal is currently placed
    age           number      — Seconds since portal was opened
    stableUntil   number      — tick() deadline for stability
  }

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION C  —  SCREEN-SPACE FX LAYERS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  _UPG.ssFX is a table holding references to all screen-space frames:
  {
    container     Frame        — Root container, full screen, ZIndex=10
    vignette      ImageLabel   — Dark radial gradient, ImageTransparency reactive
    scanlines     Frame        — Repeating stripe gradient, static
    colorLeak_bl  Frame        — Left-edge blue color bleed
    colorLeak_br  Frame        — Right-edge orange color bleed
    chromR        Frame        — Red channel offset layer
    chromG        Frame        — Green channel offset layer  (static)
    chromB        Frame        — Blue channel offset layer
    speedLines    ImageLabel   — Radial speed lines, shown on teleport
    flash         Frame        — Full-screen white flash
  }

  Each layer uses BackgroundTransparency animation to appear/disappear.
  Never destroy these — reuse them by tweening transparency.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION D  —  ANIMATION STATE MACHINE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  AnimSM is the animation state machine:

  States:
    IDLE        — Gun holstered or standing still
    AIM         — Player zooming/aiming
    FIRE_BLUE   — Just fired blue portal
    FIRE_ORANGE — Just fired orange portal
    TELEPORT_IN — Entering portal
    TELEPORT_OUT— Exiting portal
    SWAP_COLOR  — Switching selected color
    PORTAL_OPEN — Portal placement in progress
    PORTAL_CLOSE— Portal being removed
    DISABLED    — Gun temporarily disabled (cooldown etc.)

  Transitions are defined in AnimSM.transitions[from][to] as duration.
  Add new states by calling AnimSM.addState(name, onEnter, onExit, onUpdate).
  Fire a transition with AnimSM.transition(targetState).

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION E  —  PARTICLE PRESET SYSTEM
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  _preset(name, config) — Register a preset
  applyPreset(name, parent, colorOverride?) — Instantiate it

  config fields:
    color         ColorSequence    — Particle color gradient over lifetime
    lightEmission number (0–1)     — How much the particle emits light
    lightInfluence number (0–1)    — How much world lighting affects it
    size          NumberSequence   — Size over lifetime
    speed         NumberRange      — Min/max initial speed
    spread        Vector2          — SpreadAngle X/Y
    lifetime      NumberRange      — Min/max lifetime seconds
    rate          number           — Particles/second (0 = burst via Emit)
    rotation      NumberRange      — Initial rotation range (degrees)
    rotSpeed      NumberRange      — Rotation speed (degrees/sec)
    transparency  NumberSequence?  — Optional transparency over lifetime

  applyPreset returns the ParticleEmitter so you can call :Emit(n) on it.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION F  —  AUDIOMGR CHANNEL SYSTEM
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  AudioMgr enforces a 16-channel cap, evicting the oldest on overflow.
  This prevents audio saturation from heavy VFX use.

  AudioMgr.play(id, opts) → Sound
    opts: { volume, pitch, rollOff, parent }

  AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, opts) → Sound, BasePart
    Creates an invisible part at `pos`, plays sound from it.
    Auto-destroys part when sound ends (or after 8s).

  AudioMgr.playLayered(ids, pos, baseVol, pitchVariance) → Sound[]
    Plays multiple sounds with slight random pitch variation.
    Staggers each by 30ms for natural layering.

  To create a looping ambient sound, do NOT use AudioMgr — create the
  Sound manually and manage it in _ambientLoops[colorKey].

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION G  —  COMBO SYSTEM EXTENSION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  ComboSys.onFire(colorKey)
    Call whenever the player fires a portal. Internally increments streak,
    resets if > comboWindow seconds have elapsed, and fires milestone VFX.

  ComboSys.streak          — Current streak count
  ComboSys.comboWindow     — Time (s) before streak resets (default 4)
  ComboSys.milestones      — {5, 10, 20, 50, 100} milestone thresholds
  ComboSys.milestoneDone   — table[milestone] = bool, reset on streak break

  To add a custom milestone:
    table.insert(ComboSys.milestones, 200)
    comboEffects[200] = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        -- your VFX here
    end

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION H  —  PORTALGRAPH (Portal Relationship Tracker)
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  When both portals are open, the cross-portal beam activates.
  The beam is a single Beam instance connecting beamAnchor parts on each
  portal. Its CurveSize0/1 animate on Heartbeat to give it a living feel.

  Cross-portal beam properties:
    Color     — Blue portal col → White → Orange portal col (ColorSequence)
    Width0/1  — 0.05 studs (thin, electric)
    Segments  — 16 (enough for smooth curve)
    LightEmission — 1 (full neon glow)

  The beam connector also fires VFX2.crossPortalCharge() periodically
  (every UCFG.beamPulsePeriod seconds) to give energy bursts along the beam.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION I  —  PERFORMANCE TUNING GUIDE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  ULTRA quality (high-end PC):
    All UCFG toggles ON. VFX rate multiplier 1.0.
    Expected extra parts: ~120 per open portal pair.
    Expected particle emitters: ~24 active.

  HIGH quality (mid-range PC/console):
    Disable: showNeonGrid, showEdgeTendrils, showDepthSpiral.
    Reduce: orbitSparks=6, tendrilCount=4.
    VFX rate multiplier 0.7.
    Expected extra parts: ~55 per open portal pair.

  MEDIUM quality (low-end/mobile):
    Disable: showNeonGrid, showEdgeTendrils, showDepthSpiral, showCornerArcs.
    Reduce: orbitSparks=4, tendrilCount=0.
    Disable: ssFX_chromatic, ssFX_scanlines, ssFX_speedLines.
    VFX rate multiplier 0.4.
    Expected extra parts: ~25 per open portal pair.

  LOW quality (very low-end):
    Disable all showX toggles.
    Disable all ssFX_ toggles.
    Disable audioAmbient.
    Keep only: showOuterRings, showBreathing.
    Expected extra parts: ~8 per open portal pair.

  Tip: The most expensive element is showNeonGrid (up to 72 parts).
  Disabling it alone recovers significant performance on low-end hardware.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION J  —  KNOWN ROBLOX API CONSTRAINTS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  1. TweenService cannot tween CFrame and Size in the same tween on parts
     that use SpecialMesh — use two separate tweens or tween via script.

  2. Beam segments max is 32 in most Roblox versions. We use 16–20 for
     the cross-portal beam and field lines to stay safe.

  3. ParticleEmitter.Emit() is capped at 128 particles per call.
     For large explosions we call it multiple times with _delay.

  4. Workspace.Gravity affects particle physics — on custom-gravity places,
     some upward effects will look different. Account for this in speed.

  5. Material.Neon ignores ambient lighting completely — ideal for VFX.
     Material.ForceField creates the hexagonal pattern — use for holograms.
     Material.SmoothPlastic looks best for solid structural parts.

  6. PointLight with Range > 60 causes noticeable performance drops.
     Cap all point lights at Range=40 or below.

  7. Sound RollOffMaxDistance should be set before Play() for correct
     falloff. Setting it after Play() in Studio works but may not in-game.

  8. CFrame.lookAt() is preferred over CFrame.new(pos, target) for
     clarity and stability when pos == target is possible.

  9. task.delay and task.spawn are preferred over spawn() and wait().
     They use the Roblox scheduler and don't run on legacy threads.

  10. Destroying a part while a Tween is playing on it will error if the
      tween is stored. Always cancel tweens before destroying parts, or
      use pcall(_gc, part, 0) to silently destroy.

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION K  —  MODDING EXAMPLES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  Example 1: Play a custom VFX on every portal fire
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    local originalFire = PortalGun.fire -- assumes PortalGun module exposes this
    PortalGun.fire = function(color, ...)
        originalFire(color, ...)
        local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[color]
        if ex then VFX_MEGA.neonFireworks(ex.cf, ex.col, ex.pw, ex.ph) end
    end

  Example 2: Add a new portal color scheme mid-game
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    _defArt("MidnightOcean", 5,15,80, 0,100,160, "Deep midnight blue")
    PortalArt.apply("MidnightOcean")  -- applies to currently selected color

  Example 3: Register a custom combo milestone at 25
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    table.insert(ComboSys.milestones, 25)
    table.sort(ComboSys.milestones)
    comboEffects[25] = function(cf, col, pw, ph)
        VFX_MEGA2.spiralFirework(cf, col, pw, ph)
        _showNotif("✨", "25× Combo!", "On fire!", Color3.fromRGB(60,40,0), 3)
    end

  Example 4: Apply the Prismatic shader only when both portals are open
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        local bothOpen = _UPG.portalExtras.blue and _UPG.portalExtras.orange
        if bothOpen then
            PortalShader.applyBoth("Prismatic")
        end
    end)
    -- Note: Prismatic runs a RenderStepped loop — calling applyBoth repeatedly
    -- will create duplicate connections. Guard with a flag:
    local _prisApplied = false
    _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        local bothOpen = _UPG.portalExtras.blue and _UPG.portalExtras.orange
        if bothOpen and not _prisApplied then
            _prisApplied = true
            PortalShader.applyBoth("Prismatic")
        elseif not bothOpen then
            _prisApplied = false
        end
    end)

  Example 5: Make portals play a custom sound on open
  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    -- Hook into the Heartbeat portal-open watcher (see Section B)
    local _knownOpen = {}
    _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
            if ex and not _knownOpen[ck] then
                _knownOpen[ck] = true
                AudioMgr.playAt("rbxassetid://YOUR_ID_HERE", ex.beamAnchor.Position,
                    { volume=0.8, pitch=1.0, rollOff=60 })
            end
        end
        for ck in pairs(_knownOpen) do
            if not _UPG.portalExtras[ck] then _knownOpen[ck]=nil end
        end
    end)

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
  SECTION L  —  COMPATIBILITY NOTES
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

  This script is written as a LocalScript add-on. It expects:
    - To be a child of or run after the original Portalgun4 LocalScript
    - `portals.blue` and `portals.orange` to exist as module-accessible state
    - `CFG` table to exist with blueColor, orangeColor, portalWidth, portalHeight
    - `selColor` to be either "blue" or "orange"
    - `lastFire` to be a counter that increments on each shot

  It wraps all access to these in pcall so missing variables fail silently.

  If adapting to a different portal gun:
    - Update _syncFromOriginal() to read your gun's state variables
    - Update the Heartbeat portal-open watcher to match your portal part naming
    - Keep UCFG.enabled=true and the rest should work automatically

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
]]

print("[PortalGun v3 ULTRA] Deep technical reference loaded (12 sections)")



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  CONTROL REMAPPER  —  In-game keybind customization GUI
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local ControlRemap = {}
ControlRemap.binds = {
    toggleKeybinds = Enum.KeyCode.H,
    toggleDebug    = Enum.KeyCode.F1,
    randomArt      = Enum.KeyCode.G,
    cycleColor     = Enum.KeyCode.Tab,
    closePortals   = Enum.KeyCode.R,
}
ControlRemap.listeningFor = nil
ControlRemap.panel        = nil

_delay(5, function()
    pcall(function()
        local sg = _getOrMakeSS("ControlRemap")

        local remapBtn = _btn(sg, "⌨",
            Color3.fromRGB(20,30,60),
            UDim2.new(1,-52,0,82),
            UDim2.new(0,38,0,38), 25)
        _corner(remapBtn, UDim.new(0,8))
        _stroke(remapBtn, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(60,100,200), 0.4)

        local panel = _frame(sg, {
            Name            = "RemapPanel",
            Size            = UDim2.new(0,260,0,320),
            Position        = UDim2.new(1,-280,0,10),
            BackgroundColor3= Color3.fromRGB(8,12,28),
            BackgroundTransparency=0.05, BorderSizePixel=0,
            Visible         = false, ZIndex=40,
        })
        _corner(panel, UDim.new(0,12))
        _stroke(panel, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(40,80,180), 0.35)
        ControlRemap.panel = panel

        local title = _label(panel, "⌨  CONTROL REMAPPER", 11,
            Color3.fromRGB(150,190,255), Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 41)
        title.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,20); title.Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,8)

        local closeBtn = _btn(panel, "✕", Color3.fromRGB(150,30,30),
            UDim2.new(1,-34,0,8), UDim2.new(0,24,0,20), 42)
        _corner(closeBtn, UDim.new(0,5))
        closeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() panel.Visible=false end)

        local div = _frame(panel, {Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,1),
            Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,32),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(40,70,160),BorderSizePixel=0,ZIndex=41})

        local actions = {
            {"toggleKeybinds", "Toggle Keybinds"},
            {"toggleDebug",    "Toggle Debug"},
            {"randomArt",      "Random Art"},
            {"cycleColor",     "Cycle Color"},
            {"closePortals",   "Close Portals"},
        }

        for ai, action in ipairs(actions) do
            local key, label = action[1], action[2]
            local row = _frame(panel, {
                Size=UDim2.new(1,-16,0,36),
                Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0,36+(ai-1)*40),
                BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(15,22,50),
                BackgroundTransparency=0.3,BorderSizePixel=0,ZIndex=41
            })
            _corner(row, UDim.new(0,7))

            local lbl = _label(row, label, 10, Color3.fromRGB(180,210,255),
                Enum.Font.Gotham, Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, 42)
            lbl.Size=UDim2.new(1,-80,1,0); lbl.Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,0)

            local keyBtn = _btn(row,
                tostring(ControlRemap.binds[key]):match("KeyCode%.(.+)") or "?",
                Color3.fromRGB(30,50,120),
                UDim2.new(1,-76,0.5,-14),
                UDim2.new(0,68,0,26), 43)
            _corner(keyBtn, UDim.new(0,6))

            keyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if ControlRemap.listeningFor then return end
                ControlRemap.listeningFor = key
                keyBtn.Text = "Press key..."
                keyBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60,20,20)
                local conn; conn = _UIS.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp)
                    if inp.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end
                    ControlRemap.binds[key] = inp.KeyCode
                    keyBtn.Text = tostring(inp.KeyCode):match("KeyCode%.(.+)") or "?"
                    keyBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,50,120)
                    ControlRemap.listeningFor = nil
                    conn:Disconnect()
                end)
            end)
        end

        remapBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            panel.Visible = not panel.Visible
        end)
    end)
end)



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL HISTORY LOG  —  Logs portal events to an in-game scrolling panel
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local PortalLog = {}
PortalLog.entries   = {}
PortalLog.maxLines  = 40
PortalLog.panel     = nil
PortalLog.scrollFrame = nil
PortalLog.enabled   = true

local function _timestampStr()
    local t = tick()
    local mins = math.floor(t / 60) % 60
    local secs = math.floor(t) % 60
    return string.format("%02d:%02d", mins, secs)
end

local _logColors = {
    open    = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100),
    close   = Color3.fromRGB(200, 80,  80),
    tele    = Color3.fromRGB(100, 160, 255),
    fire    = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 80),
    system  = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 200),
    combo   = Color3.fromRGB(255, 140, 20),
}

function PortalLog.add(eventType, message)
    if not PortalLog.enabled then return end
    local entry = {
        time  = _timestampStr(),
        etype = eventType,
        msg   = message,
    }
    table.insert(PortalLog.entries, 1, entry)
    if #PortalLog.entries > PortalLog.maxLines then
        table.remove(PortalLog.entries)
    end
    PortalLog.refresh()
end

function PortalLog.refresh()
    if not PortalLog.scrollFrame then return end
    -- Clear old rows
    for _, child in ipairs(PortalLog.scrollFrame:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
    end
    for i, entry in ipairs(PortalLog.entries) do
        local row = Instance.new("Frame")
        row.Size  = UDim2.new(1,-8,0,18)
        row.Position = UDim2.new(0,4,0,(i-1)*20)
        row.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.ZIndex = 52
        row.Parent = PortalLog.scrollFrame

        local timeLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        timeLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0,38,1,0)
        timeLbl.BackgroundTransparency=1
        timeLbl.Text = entry.time
        timeLbl.Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono
        timeLbl.TextSize = 8
        timeLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100,110,150)
        timeLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        timeLbl.ZIndex=53; timeLbl.Parent=row

        local msgLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        msgLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1,-42,1,0)
        msgLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0,40,0,0)
        msgLbl.BackgroundTransparency=1
        msgLbl.Text = entry.msg
        msgLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        msgLbl.TextSize = 9
        msgLbl.TextColor3 = _logColors[entry.etype] or Color3.fromRGB(180,180,180)
        msgLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        msgLbl.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        msgLbl.ZIndex=53; msgLbl.Parent=row
    end
    PortalLog.scrollFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(1,0,0,#PortalLog.entries*20+4)
end

-- Build panel
_delay(5.5, function()
    pcall(function()
        local sg = _getOrMakeSS("PortalLog")
        local logBtn = _btn(sg, "📋", Color3.fromRGB(20,30,50),
            UDim2.new(1,-52,0,44), UDim2.new(0,38,0,38), 25)
        _corner(logBtn, UDim.new(0,8))

        local logPanel = _frame(sg, {
            Name="PortalLogPanel",
            Size=UDim2.new(0,240,0,260),
            Position=UDim2.new(1,-260,0,10),
            BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(6,10,22),
            BackgroundTransparency=0.05,BorderSizePixel=0,
            Visible=false,ZIndex=50,
        })
        _corner(logPanel, UDim.new(0,10))
        _stroke(logPanel, 1.5, Color3.fromRGB(30,50,120), 0.4)

        local logTitle = _label(logPanel,"📋  PORTAL LOG", 10,
            Color3.fromRGB(140,170,230),Enum.Font.GothamBold,
            Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,51)
        logTitle.Size=UDim2.new(1,-8,0,18); logTitle.Position=UDim2.new(0,10,0,6)

        local logClose = _btn(logPanel,"✕",Color3.fromRGB(140,25,25),
            UDim2.new(1,-30,0,6),UDim2.new(0,22,0,18),52)
        _corner(logClose, UDim.new(0,4))
        logClose.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() logPanel.Visible=false end)

        local sf = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        sf.Size = UDim2.new(1,-8,1,-30)
        sf.Position = UDim2.new(0,4,0,28)
        sf.BackgroundTransparency=1; sf.BorderSizePixel=0
        sf.ScrollBarThickness=4; sf.ScrollBarImageColor3=Color3.fromRGB(60,80,160)
        sf.CanvasSize=UDim2.new(1,0,0,0); sf.ZIndex=51; sf.Parent=logPanel
        PortalLog.scrollFrame = sf; PortalLog.panel = logPanel

        logBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            logPanel.Visible = not logPanel.Visible
        end)

        -- Seed with some example entries
        PortalLog.add("system", "Portal Gun v3 ULTRA ready")
        PortalLog.add("system", "All systems nominal")
    end)
end)

-- Hook into portal events for logging
local _loggedOpen  = {}
local _loggedClose = {}
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    pcall(function()
        for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
            if ex and not _loggedOpen[ck] then
                _loggedOpen[ck]  = true
                _loggedClose[ck] = false
                local surf = PortalPhysics and PortalPhysics.analyzeSurf
                    and ex.cf and PortalPhysics.analyzeSurf(ex.cf.LookVector) or "?"
                PortalLog.add("open", string.upper(ck).." portal opened on "..surf)
            end
        end
        for ck in pairs(_loggedOpen) do
            if _loggedOpen[ck] and not _UPG.portalExtras[ck] and not _loggedClose[ck] then
                _loggedClose[ck] = true
                _loggedOpen[ck]  = false
                PortalLog.add("close", string.upper(ck).." portal closed")
            end
        end
    end)
end)

local VFX_MEGA3 = {}



function VFX_MEGA3.auroraWave(cf, col, pw, ph)
    local c2=col or Color3.new(0.08,0.10,0.08)
    local pw2=pw or 4; local ph2=ph or 6; local cf2=cf or CFrame.new(0,0,0)
    for ri=1,2 do
        _delay(ri*0.28, function()
            local s=pw2*(0.35+ri*0.28); local aspect=ph2/pw2
            local p=_part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon,Color=c2,
                Size=Vector3.new(s,s*aspect,0.04),Transparency=0.12,CFrame=cf2})
            local m=Instance.new("SpecialMesh"); m.MeshType=Enum.MeshType.Sphere
            m.Scale=Vector3.new(1,1,0.025); m.Parent=p; p.Parent=_WS
            _tw(p,0.28+ri*0.05,{Size=Vector3.new(s*1.35,s*aspect*1.28,0.04),Transparency=1})
            _gc(p,0.28+ri*0.06)
            if ri==1 then
                local pl=Instance.new("PointLight"); pl.Brightness=3; pl.Range=12; pl.Color=c2; pl.Parent=p
            end
        end)
    end
    local bp=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),CFrame=cf2})
    bp.Parent=_WS; local ba=_att(bp)
    local be=_pe(ba,{Color=_cs(0,Color3.new(1,1,1),0.3,c2,1,c2),LightEmission=0.60,LightInfluence=0.2,
        Size=_ns(0,0.09,0.5,0.07,1,0),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(4,11),SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(30,30),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(0.22,0.48),Rate=0,
        Rotation=NumberRange.new(0,360),RotSpeed=NumberRange.new(-80,80)})
    pcall(function() be:Emit(8) end)
    _gc(bp,1.1)
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  EXTENDED PERFORMANCE MONITOR  —  Advanced FPS and memory tracking
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local PerfMon = {}
PerfMon.samples      = {}
PerfMon.maxSamples   = 60
PerfMon.updateRate   = 0.5   -- seconds between UI updates
PerfMon.lastUpdate   = 0

-- FPS sampling
_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    table.insert(PerfMon.samples, dt)
    if #PerfMon.samples > PerfMon.maxSamples then
        table.remove(PerfMon.samples, 1)
    end
end)

function PerfMon.getAverageFPS()
    if #PerfMon.samples == 0 then return 0 end
    local sum=0; for _,s in ipairs(PerfMon.samples) do sum=sum+s end
    return 1/(sum/#PerfMon.samples)
end

function PerfMon.getMinFPS()
    local worst=0
    for _,s in ipairs(PerfMon.samples) do
        if s > worst then worst=s end
    end
    return worst>0 and 1/worst or 0
end

function PerfMon.getMaxFPS()
    local best=math.huge
    for _,s in ipairs(PerfMon.samples) do
        if s < best then best=s end
    end
    return best<math.huge and 1/best or 0
end

function PerfMon.getExtraPartCount()
    local count=0
    for _, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        if ex and ex.folder then
            count=count+#ex.folder:GetDescendants()
        end
    end
    return count
end

function PerfMon.getActiveSounds()
    return AudioMgr and #AudioMgr.channels or 0
end

-- Build extended debug overlay
_delay(6, function()
    pcall(function()
        -- Find existing debug overlay and augment it
        local dbgLbl = _gv3 and _gv3.debugLabel
        if not dbgLbl then return end

        local _perfLine = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        _perfLine.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,10)
        _perfLine.Position = UDim2.new(0,0,1,2)
        _perfLine.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(0,0)
        _perfLine.BackgroundTransparency=1
        _perfLine.TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(0,220,150)
        _perfLine.Font=Enum.Font.RobotoMono
        _perfLine.TextSize=8
        _perfLine.TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        _perfLine.ZIndex=dbgLbl.ZIndex
        _perfLine.Parent=dbgLbl.Parent

        _RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
            if not _gv3.debugOverlay or not _gv3.debugOverlay.Visible then return end
            local now=tick()
            if now-PerfMon.lastUpdate < PerfMon.updateRate then return end
            PerfMon.lastUpdate=now
            local avg=PerfMon.getAverageFPS()
            local mn=PerfMon.getMinFPS()
            local mx=PerfMon.getMaxFPS()
            local pts=PerfMon.getExtraPartCount()
            local snd=PerfMon.getActiveSounds()
            local combo=ComboSys and ComboSys.getStreak() or 0
            _perfLine.Text=string.format(
                "FPS avg:%.0f min:%.0f max:%.0f | parts:%d | sfx:%d | combo:%d",
                avg, mn, mx, pts, snd, combo)
            -- Color-code by FPS
            if avg >= 55 then
                _perfLine.TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(0,220,80)
            elseif avg >= 30 then
                _perfLine.TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(220,200,0)
            else
                _perfLine.TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(220,60,60)
            end
        end)
    end)
end)



-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  EXTENDED ENVIRONMENT EFFECTS  —  World-space visual reactions to portals
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local EnvFX2 = {}

-- ── Proximity light sources ───────────────────────────────────────────────
local _envLights = {}

local function _makeEnvLight(pos, col, brightness, range, colorKey)
    local lightPart=_part({Transparency=1,Size=Vector3.new(0.1,0.1,0.1),
        CFrame=CFrame.new(pos)})
    lightPart.Parent=_WS
    local pl=Instance.new("PointLight")
    pl.Brightness=brightness; pl.Range=range; pl.Color=col
    pl.Parent=lightPart
    _envLights[colorKey]=lightPart
    return lightPart
end

local function _removeEnvLight(colorKey)
    if _envLights[colorKey] then
        local lp=_envLights[colorKey]
        _tw(lp:FindFirstChildOfClass("PointLight") or lp, 0.8, {Brightness=0})
        _delay(0.9, function() pcall(function() lp:Destroy() end) end)
        _envLights[colorKey]=nil
    end
end

-- Update env lights when portals open/close
local _prevEnvLightState={blue=false,orange=false}
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs({blue=_UPG.portalExtras.blue, orange=_UPG.portalExtras.orange}) do
        local isOpen = ex and ex.beamAnchor ~= nil
        if isOpen and not _prevEnvLightState[ck] then
            _prevEnvLightState[ck]=true
            if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
                local col=ck=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                    or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
                _makeEnvLight(ex.beamAnchor.Position, col, 3, 45, ck)
            end
        elseif not isOpen and _prevEnvLightState[ck] then
            _prevEnvLightState[ck]=false
            _removeEnvLight(ck)
        end
        -- Update position of existing light
        if _envLights[ck] and ex and ex.beamAnchor then
            _envLights[ck].CFrame=CFrame.new(ex.beamAnchor.Position)
        end
    end
end)

-- ── Ground glow decal (using Neon box) ───────────────────────────────────
local _groundGlows = {}

local function _makeGroundGlow(portalPos, col, colorKey)
    if not UCFG.showGroundGlow then return end
    local gDown = workspace:Raycast(portalPos, Vector3.new(0,-20,0),
        RaycastParams.new())
    if not gDown then return end
    local groundY = gDown.Position.Y
    local glow = _part({Material=Enum.Material.Neon, Color=col,
        Size=Vector3.new(4,0.04,6), Transparency=0.7,
        CFrame=CFrame.new(portalPos.X, groundY+0.05, portalPos.Z)})
    glow.Parent=_WS
    _tw(glow, 0.5, {Transparency=0.5})
    _groundGlows[colorKey]=glow
end

local function _removeGroundGlow(colorKey)
    if _groundGlows[colorKey] then
        local g=_groundGlows[colorKey]
        _tw(g, 0.5, {Transparency=1})
        _delay(0.6, function() pcall(function() g:Destroy() end) end)
        _groundGlows[colorKey]=nil
    end
end

UCFG.showGroundGlow = true

local _prevGlowState={blue=false,orange=false}
_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs({blue=_UPG.portalExtras.blue, orange=_UPG.portalExtras.orange}) do
        local isOpen = ex and ex.beamAnchor ~= nil
        if isOpen and not _prevGlowState[ck] then
            _prevGlowState[ck]=true
            if ex and ex.beamAnchor then
                local col=ck=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                    or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
                _makeGroundGlow(ex.beamAnchor.Position, col, ck)
            end
        elseif not isOpen and _prevGlowState[ck] then
            _prevGlowState[ck]=false
            _removeGroundGlow(ck)
        end
    end
end)

-- ── Atmospheric dust near portals ─────────────────────────────────────────
local _dustParts = {}

local function _spawnDust(pos, col)
    local dp=_part({Transparency=1, Size=Vector3.new(8,12,8),
        CFrame=CFrame.new(pos)})
    dp.Parent=_WS
    local da=_att(dp)
    local dpe=_pe(da,{
        Color=ColorSequence.new({
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(200,200,220)),
            ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, col)
        }),
        LightEmission=0.05, LightInfluence=0.9,
        Size=NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,0),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.3,0.4),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,0)
        }),
        Speed=NumberRange.new(0.1,0.8),
        SpreadAngle=Vector2.new(180,180),
        Lifetime=NumberRange.new(4,8),
        Rate=3,
        Transparency=NumberSequence.new({
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0,1),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.2,0.7),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0.8,0.7),
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1,1)
        })
    })
    return dp, dpe
end

local _dustEmitters={}
local _prevDustState={blue=false,orange=false}

_RS.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
    for ck, ex in pairs({blue=_UPG.portalExtras.blue, orange=_UPG.portalExtras.orange}) do
        local isOpen = ex and ex.beamAnchor ~= nil
        if isOpen and not _prevDustState[ck] then
            _prevDustState[ck]=true
            if ex and ex.beamAnchor and UCFG.showAtmDust then
                local col=ck=="blue" and (CFG and CFG.blueColor or Color3.fromRGB(0,130,255))
                    or (CFG and CFG.orangeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255,120,0))
                local dp,dpe=_spawnDust(ex.beamAnchor.Position, col)
                _dustEmitters[ck]={part=dp,pe=dpe}
            end
        elseif not isOpen and _prevDustState[ck] then
            _prevDustState[ck]=false
            if _dustEmitters[ck] then
                local d=_dustEmitters[ck]
                d.pe.Rate=0
                _delay(10, function() pcall(function() d.part:Destroy() end) end)
                _dustEmitters[ck]=nil
            end
        end
        -- Track position
        if _dustEmitters[ck] and ex and ex.beamAnchor then
            _dustEmitters[ck].part.CFrame=CFrame.new(ex.beamAnchor.Position)
        end
    end
end)

UCFG.showAtmDust = true

--  FINAL INITIALIZATION CHECK
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local function _countTable(t)
    local n=0; for _ in pairs(t) do n=n+1 end; return n
end

_delay(1, function()
    pcall(function()
        local vfxCount = _countTable(VFX2 or {}) + _countTable(VFX3 or {}) 
            + _countTable(VFX3_EXT or {}) + _countTable(VFX_MEGA or {})
            + _countTable(VFX_MEGA2 or {}) + _countTable(VFX_MEGA3 or {})
        local artCount = PortalArt and #PortalArt.getSchemes() or 0
        local shaderCount = PortalShader and #PortalShader.list() or 0
        
        print(string.format("[v3 ULTRA] Initialized: %d VFX funcs | %d art schemes | %d shaders",
            vfxCount, artCount, shaderCount))
    end)
end)

-- ─── One-line access convenience API ─────────────────────────────────────────
local pg = {}

-- Apply a named shader to both portals
function pg.shader(name)       PortalShader.applyBoth(name) end
-- Apply a named art scheme
function pg.art(name)          PortalArt.apply(name) end
-- Apply a random art scheme
function pg.randomArt()        PortalArt.random() end
-- Fire a named VFX3_EXT effect on the blue portal
function pg.vfx(name, ...)
    local ex = _UPG.portalExtras.blue or _UPG.portalExtras.orange
    if not ex then return end
    local fn = VFX3_EXT[name] or VFX3[name] or VFX2[name] or VFX_MEGA[name]
        or VFX_MEGA2[name] or VFX_MEGA3[name]
    if fn then pcall(fn, ex.cf, ex.col, ex.pw, ex.ph, ...) end
end
-- Toggle UCFG boolean flag
function pg.toggle(flag)
    if UCFG[flag] ~= nil then UCFG[flag] = not UCFG[flag]
    print("[pg.toggle] "..flag.." = "..tostring(UCFG[flag])) end
end
-- Print current status
function pg.status()
    print("═══ Portal Gun v3 ULTRA Status ═══")
    for ck, ex in pairs(_UPG.portalExtras) do
        print("  "..ck.." portal: open, age="..tostring(ex.age and math.floor(ex.age) or "?").."s")
    end
    if ComboSys then print("  combo streak: "..ComboSys.getStreak()) end
    if PerfMon   then print(string.format("  FPS avg: %.0f", PerfMon.getAverageFPS())) end
    print("  audio channels: "..(AudioMgr and #AudioMgr.channels or 0))
    print("═══════════════════════════════════")
end

-- Make pg accessible globally
if _G then _G.pg = pg end
_registry.pg = pg
