-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL MINIMAP ENHANCED  —  Extended minimap with ping markers
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local MinimapExt = {}
MinimapExt.pings    = {}   -- {pos=Vector3, color=Color3, t=tick(), label=string}
MinimapExt.maxPings = 10

function MinimapExt.addPing(worldPos, col, label)
    table.insert(MinimapExt.pings, 1, {
        pos   = worldPos,
        color = col or Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255),
        t     = tick(),
        label = label or "!",
    })
    if #MinimapExt.pings > MinimapExt.maxPings then
        table.remove(MinimapExt.pings)
    end
end

function MinimapExt.clearPings()
    MinimapExt.pings = {}
end

-- Draw pings on the minimap frame each frame
_RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
    if not (_gv3 and _gv3.minimap and _gv3.minimap.Visible) then return end
    -- Remove expired pings (older than 5s)
    for i = #MinimapExt.pings, 1, -1 do
        if tick() - MinimapExt.pings[i].t > 5 then
            table.remove(MinimapExt.pings, i)
        end
    end
end)

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL SOUND MIXER  —  Per-category volume controls
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local SoundMixer = {}
SoundMixer.categories = {
    portal = 1.0,
    gun    = 1.0,
    tele   = 1.0,
    ui     = 0.8,
    ambient= 0.6,
}

function SoundMixer.set(category, volume)
    if SoundMixer.categories[category] == nil then
        warn("[SoundMixer] Unknown category: "..tostring(category)); return
    end
    SoundMixer.categories[category] = math.clamp(volume, 0, 1)
    print("[SoundMixer] "..category.." = "..tostring(math.floor(volume*100)).."%")
end

function SoundMixer.get(category)
    return SoundMixer.categories[category] or 1.0
end

function SoundMixer.playEvent(category, id, pos, baseVol, pitch)
    local vol = (baseVol or 0.7) * SoundMixer.get(category)
    if vol < 0.01 then return end
    if pos then
        AudioMgr.playAt(id, pos, { volume=vol, pitch=pitch or 1 })
    else
        AudioMgr.play(id, { volume=vol, pitch=pitch or 1 })
    end
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  EXTENDED PORTAL COLOR API  —  Smooth color transitions
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local ColorAPI = {}
ColorAPI.transitionTime  = 0.4
ColorAPI.activeTransitions = {}

function ColorAPI.transitionTo(colorKey, targetColor, duration)
    duration = duration or ColorAPI.transitionTime
    local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
    if not ex then return end

    if ColorAPI.activeTransitions[colorKey] then
        ColorAPI.activeTransitions[colorKey]:Disconnect()
        ColorAPI.activeTransitions[colorKey] = nil
    end

    local startTime = tick()
    local startColor = ex.col or targetColor
    local conn
    conn = _RS.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local t = math.clamp(elapsed / duration, 0, 1)
        -- Smooth step
        local st = t * t * (3 - 2 * t)
        local current = Color3.new(
            startColor.R + (targetColor.R - startColor.R) * st,
            startColor.G + (targetColor.G - startColor.G) * st,
            startColor.B + (targetColor.B - startColor.B) * st
        )

        -- Apply to portal parts
        if ex.rings then
            for _, rd in ipairs(ex.rings) do
                if rd.part and rd.part.Parent then
                    rd.part.Color = current
                end
            end
        end
        if ex.outerHalo and ex.outerHalo.Parent then
            ex.outerHalo.Color = current
        end

        if t >= 1 then
            conn:Disconnect()
            ColorAPI.activeTransitions[colorKey] = nil
            if ex then ex.col = targetColor end
        end
    end)
    ColorAPI.activeTransitions[colorKey] = conn
end

function ColorAPI.pulse(colorKey, flashColor, duration)
    local ex = _UPG.portalExtras[colorKey]
    if not ex then return end
    local orig = ex.col
    ColorAPI.transitionTo(colorKey, flashColor, (duration or 0.15) * 0.3)
    _delay((duration or 0.15) * 0.35, function()
        ColorAPI.transitionTo(colorKey, orig, (duration or 0.15) * 0.65)
    end)
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL EFFECT QUEUE  —  Queues VFX to play in sequence or in parallel
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local EffectQueue = {}
EffectQueue.queue     = {}
EffectQueue.running   = false
EffectQueue.maxQueue  = 20

function EffectQueue.add(fn, delay)
    if #EffectQueue.queue >= EffectQueue.maxQueue then
        table.remove(EffectQueue.queue, 1)  -- drop oldest
    end
    table.insert(EffectQueue.queue, { fn=fn, delay=delay or 0 })
end

function EffectQueue.flush()
    for i, item in ipairs(EffectQueue.queue) do
        _delay(item.delay + (i-1)*0.04, function()
            pcall(item.fn)
        end)
    end
    EffectQueue.queue = {}
end

function EffectQueue.clear()
    EffectQueue.queue = {}
end

-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
--  PORTAL TELEPORT HISTORY  —  Tracks recent teleports for statistics
-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

local TeleHistory = {}
TeleHistory.records   = {}
TeleHistory.maxRecords= 50
TeleHistory.totalCount= 0

function TeleHistory.record(entryColor, exitColor, entryPos, exitPos)
    TeleHistory.totalCount = TeleHistory.totalCount + 1
    local rec = {
        id        = TeleHistory.totalCount,
        time      = tick(),
        entry     = entryColor,
        exit      = exitColor,
        entryPos  = entryPos,
        exitPos   = exitPos,
        distance  = entryPos and exitPos and (exitPos - entryPos).Magnitude or 0,
    }
    table.insert(TeleHistory.records, 1, rec)
    if #TeleHistory.records > TeleHistory.maxRecords then
        table.remove(TeleHistory.records)
    end
    PortalLog.add("tele", string.format("Teleport #%d — %.0f studs", rec.id, rec.distance))
    return rec
end

function TeleHistory.getTotalDistance()
    local sum = 0
    for _, r in ipairs(TeleHistory.records) do sum = sum + r.distance end
    return sum
end

function TeleHistory.getAverageDistance()
    if TeleHistory.totalCount == 0 then return 0 end
    return TeleHistory.getTotalDistance() / TeleHistory.totalCount
end

function TeleHistory.printStats()
    print(string.format("[TeleHistory] Total teleports: %d", TeleHistory.totalCount))
    print(string.format("[TeleHistory] Total distance:  %.0f studs", TeleHistory.getTotalDistance()))
    print(string.format("[TeleHistory] Avg distance:    %.0f studs", TeleHistory.getAverageDistance()))
end

local ThemePresets = {}
ThemePresets.themes = {}

local function _defTheme(name, blueColor, orangeColor, description)
    ThemePresets.themes[name] = {
        blue   = blueColor,
        orange = orangeColor,
        desc   = description,
    }
end

-- Classic pairs (named by sci-fi/fantasy reference)

_defTheme("Ice2",        Color3.fromRGB(180,230,255),  Color3.fromRGB(230,255,255), "Ice and frost")

_defTheme("Retro",       Color3.fromRGB(0,200,0),     Color3.fromRGB(200,100,0),   "Retro CRT green/amber")
_defTheme("Pastel",      Color3.fromRGB(180,200,255), Color3.fromRGB(255,200,180), "Soft pastel pair")
_defTheme("Neon2",       Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0),     Color3.fromRGB(255,0,255),   "Full neon pair")
_defTheme("Dusk2",       Color3.fromRGB(80,40,140),   Color3.fromRGB(200,100,40),  "Sunset dusk")
_defTheme("Dawn2",       Color3.fromRGB(255,180,200), Color3.fromRGB(255,230,100), "Sunrise dawn")

function ThemePresets.apply(name)
    local t = ThemePresets.themes[name]
    if not t then warn("[ThemePresets] Unknown theme: "..tostring(name)); return end
    if CFG then
        CFG.blueColor   = t.blue
        CFG.orangeColor = t.orange
    end
    -- Apply to active portal extras
    ColorAPI.transitionTo("blue",   t.blue,   0.5)
    ColorAPI.transitionTo("orange", t.orange, 0.5)
    _showNotif("🎨", "Theme: "..name, t.desc, Color3.fromRGB(20,20,50), 3)
end

function ThemePresets.list()
    local names = {}
    for k in pairs(ThemePresets.themes) do table.insert(names, k) end
    table.sort(names)
    return names
end

function ThemePresets.random()
    local names = ThemePresets.list()
    ThemePresets.apply(names[math.random(1,#names)])
end

-- Add to registry
if _G and _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry then
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.ThemePresets  = ThemePresets
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.SoundMixer    = SoundMixer
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.ColorAPI      = ColorAPI
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.EffectQueue   = EffectQueue
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.TeleHistory   = TeleHistory
    _G.PortalGun_v3_Registry.MinimapExt    = MinimapExt
end
if _G and _G.pg then
    _G.pg.theme   = function(n) ThemePresets.apply(n) end
    _G.pg.mixer   = function(c,v) SoundMixer.set(c,v) end
    _G.pg.themes  = function() return ThemePresets.list() end
end
